 
Wacabanga kanye, wase enquma ukuthi makaziyele yena mathupha laphaya
kuSydney aboleke imali kuyena kunokuba aphuthelwe yilemtitilizo engaka.

Ingane yentombazana, yona lena eseduze kwakho.

Uyangizwa MaMathenjwa, uyangizwa? Yilokho-ke.

La magama okugcina aphuma elandelana ngokushesha.

Wagcina ngokungigqolozela ezinhlamini zamehlo.

Kwaba kuhle ngabona ukuthi sekuyithuba lami manje.

Uma ngingase ngiphazame, awu...?

Kwathi-ke noma ngethuka kakhulu ngokuzwa lokhu, ngabuye ngazibamba.

Ngezwa ngifikelwa yisibindi sokuthi yonke into ngiyithathe lula.

Ngaqala ukumoyizela ngabuye ngahleka ngabe sengimbamba isandla, ngakhuluma
naye. 

Ngivele ngakuzwa uqala ukukhuluma ukuthi ufuna igazi.

Ngibuye ngazibamba ngobo ngifuna ukubona ukuthi unaso yini isibindi.

Sengibonile ukuthi awunaso neze.

Le nto ayisiyo nakancane inkinga, ngabe kudala wayikhuluma.

Ingane lena yalethwa yithi sobabili lapha emhlabeni.

Konke okwenzeka kuyo kufuna mina nawe.

Bokungaba yini ufe ungishiye nomthwalo ongaka wezingane ezimbili. 

Uyazi ukuthi kungcono khona ukuthi singehlukani thina nawe.

Samletha sobabile lapha emhlabeni uNoNhlanhla, manje-ke nokumphumuza
ngokwethu.

Angiboni-ke ukuthi yini elukhuni uma thina nawe sivumelene.

"Hawu nkosikazi! Hawu Mathenjwa'. Be..be..Hawu!

Bengingazi ukuthi le ndaba enjena uzoyithatha kanjena.

Kusho ukuthi .. Hawu nkosikazi!

Mina bengifuna ukukumangaza.

Ngifuna ukukukhombisa ukuthi nginesibindi ongenaso wena.

Konke ngizokulungisa.

Ngichazele ukuthi bakufuna nini lokhu, kanjani.

Ngiyabonga mkani.

Impela bengingazi ukuthi ungangephula kulenkinga engazifaka kuyo
ngokungazi.

Ngibone indlela esijabula ngayo nezingane zethu.

Ngabona kulukhuni kuyitshe ukuba ngikutshele ngale ndaba.

UBusisiwe wayengenkulu impelesi kaThuli.

Wayeqokwe uye uThuli ngoba wayenolwazi oluningi ngomsebenzi wezimpelesi.


Kodwa-ke uBusisiwe kwangathi akanawo neze umdlandla walo-khu okwenzekayo.


Waqala ngokwenqaba ukuba yimpelesi ngokuthi wayenohambo.

Iningi lamnqabela kulokho.

Lamcindezela ekutheni nakanjani abe khona ukuba abe yimpelesi kaThuli
umngane nomzalwane lokho.

Wasale esephoqeleka ukuthi akwenze.

Ukundonda kukaBusisiwe ngalo msebenzi kwakwenziwa isazelo sokwake kwenzeka
esikhathini esingalinganiselwa eminyakeni eyisihlanu eyedlule.

Uyakhumbula ukuthi basuka bengumthimba kubo kwaSizakele nxa beyosina
eDlangaleni.

Ukhumbula kahle ukuthi babengabangani noSizakele besafunda isikole.

Isimemezelo sokuthi uBheki noThuli bayashada sawushiya siwuxovile
umphefumulo wakhe.

Wayebona ukuthi uBheki lona wayengasamfanisi nakancane.

Engaboni ukuthi uBusisiwe wayekhona kuleliya muva lakhe uBheki
angasaliphuphi nakuliphupha ngenxa yempilo entsha nothando asenalo manje
ngoThuli.

Ukwazana kukaBusisiwe noThuli kudalwe ukukholwa ndawonye, hhayi ukuthi
bangamathe nolimi.

Kwasuke kwamuma nje uBusisiwe ukuthi le ndaba ka Bheki angayithini ngoba
akasezwa nakuzwa uThuli ngoNgcamane wakhe.

Bobabili bafakaza mihla le ukuthi kwaba nguMoya Oyingcwele owababonisa
ukuthi bona bafanelene.

Nalo nje udaba olunje noma wayengaluveza komunye wabazalwane.

Lwalungeze lwathathwa njengamaqiniso ngoba nakhu uBheki uyincwadi evulekile
emehlweni eningi.

Futhi akukho nasici esinjena esinganamathela kuye.

Wabona-ke uBusisiwe ukuthi kuzothathwa ngokuthi uyahhema noma-ke
uyisifa mona uhlose ukonisa.

Uyazi ngifika nje ngizobuza ukuthi wena ukubona kunganjani ukuthi
ngishayele uMabuza ucingo ngivele ngimazise ngendaba leyo.

Uma ngicabanga ngale ndaba ngivele ngehluleke ukuthi yena
ngiyombhekelwa ubani uma ngimtshela le ndabo enzima kangaka.

Kusho yena okaMthombeni ofuna usizo kumngane wakhe.

Ha! Ungaqali ukwenze lokho dade, uyoba uzibizela okukhulu.

Uzovela athukuthelele uMabuza.

Alikho enginalo, kepha elokushaya ucingo lizokhombisa indelelo
emangalisayo.

Washo uMaMvila wabona ngokusobala ukaMagagula ukuthi usengazona izinto
ngakho ukushaya ucingo lokho.

Ekhaya ushiye utshwala buyothengelwa imvubelo noshukela nguye uSimangele.

Nango unina kaSimangele esencoma ukuya kudadewabo owendele kwaLobamba.

Phela udadewabo lowo wake wehlelwa ukuthi indodakazi yakhe ikhululwe
isafunda.

Uya nje kuye ngoba ethemba ukuthi angathola umbono oyomsiza kule nkinga.


Watheleka emzini kadadewabo uKaMagagula emini wavele wamthela
ngezinyembezi.

Walwendlala udaba lolo.

Kwamdabukisa udadewabo waze naye wabonakala eseciphiza.

UkaMagagula omncane lo yena ayibanga nzima kangako eyakhe indaba.

Kwenziwa yikho ukuthi uninazala wayesadla amabele.

Kwaba wuye owayethulela umnumzana wakwakhe.

Kwazise futhi namfenijwana leyo wayengayikhathelele okutheni owakwakhe.


UKaMagagula useze ubuyela kwakhe nje akatholanga lisu elingamsiza kule
nkinga.

Endleleni eya ekhaya wayehlwathiza nje kungekho nakubonayo ngoba nakhu
ephethwe yiyo imicabango.

Ibhasi lamthatha engazelele waze wakhumbula lapho esebona izitolo
esiteshini sakwaMahlanya.

Yilapho ake wacabanga ukuthenga ibhodlela lotshwala elaliyomsiza ukwehlisa
le micabango.

Nango eseqonda khona esitolo sokuphuzwayo lapho aphuma esenethemba
lokuphumula azoke abe nakho kulobo busuku. 

Makhathaleni linqamuke izulu.

Abantu bathole isithuba sokuphefumula.

Kube yikhona bephuma behlola umonakalo owenziwe yizulu.

Kulaba abayaluzayo ayikho Ndlunkulu.

Akekho futhi no Mkabayi. 

Kube yima kukhunjulwa ukuthi konje iNdlunkulu ibibike umzimba okuthaka.


Izintombi zesigodlo zinikele khona eNdlunkulu.

Nxa zingena emnyango zethuke zishoqongane nxa zelamela iNdlunkulu igobodise
phezu kweziko.

UMkabayi olokhu ehlezi ngezansi kukanina azibheke ngokumangala. 

Zibuze ukuthi iNdlunkulu isinjani angaphenduli.

Adimede aziqhunsulele amehlo nje.

Nazo zimeqe ngaphezulu ziyokuzwa ukuthi ngabe iNdlunkulu igobodise nje
izizwa isinjani.

Zithi nxa zithi ziyayiphendula, zafica ukuthi isiyabanda.

Zethuka nazo kubande kwamancane.

Zithi zibheka amehlo, zihlangane namehlo, inhlamvu emnyama ayisabonwa.


Zehluleke ukuzibamba, kusuke esinamathambo isidumo sezithwele imikhono
ekhanda zidinda isililo.

Zinikele kuManqina, inceku yakoMkhulu. 

Zithi zingambikela naye asukumele phezulu ezozibonela.

Afike adelele khona ukuthi iNdlunkulu isithule.

Kube yisimanga ukufa komufi engagulanga.

Kucace futhi ukuthi akuwona umphezulu lona kepha iNdlunkulu ithathwe
ngukufa.

Kuzobuzwa bani lokhu yona isithule?

Siqhubeke isililo.

UMmama asizwe isililo ekwenye indlu, aye eNdlunkulu esenhlanhlatheka
umntwana.

Anele abone ukuthi wonke umuntu uyakhala naye asho ngengila yize engazi
ukuthi kukhalelwani.

Akubuke konke lokhu okwenzekayo uMkabayi kodwa yena angaze athi shu.

Abakhalaya akabanakile kangako kodwa uzibhekele unina.

Amehlo aseze ayizinsungulo, ubhekile.

Uyabona manje ukuthi konakele kunina kodwa akazi ukuthi ngabe konakeleni.


Unina angaphenduli.

Kube yikhona becabangayo abadala ukuthi izingane azikhishwe kulendlu.

Nempela aphume uMkabayi nonxa elusica, engathandisisi. 

Abikelwe uJama ngalenhlekelele kepha adimede adwale nje kube sengathi
akezwa ezindlebeni.

Siqhubeke isililo, manje sesenanelwa ngisho nawomakhelwane.

Beze abozalo nabo behhoyiza bethwele izandla ekhanda.

Kufike nabafowabo benkosi, oNkwelo noMhlaba, bezozwa ukuthi ngabe umphezulu
yini noma kwenzenjani.

Kodwa uJama angabaniki impendulo, kuphela abaqhusulele amehlo. 

Basuke bayozidelela khona eNdlunkulu.

Wafisa sengathi kungakhona omelulekayo ngalokhu.

Kwaba yikhona ekhumbulayo ukuthi ngisho uTozi, inkosazana kayisekazi
uNkwelo wayengakaze ameluleke ngezomaqomana.

Wayengazi ukuthi isesheli siphendulwa kanjani.

Wayazi khona nje ukusiphoxa ukuze sijokole nxa ezwa ukuthi siyamdina.

Wazibuza eziphendula uMkabayi wagcina esezunywe wubuthongo.

Wachiphatheka njalo ULamula waze wayokhuleka kulowomuzi ayengeniswe kuwona
ngayizolo wafike wacela isikhundla.

Baphinda bamemukela kahle.

Ngenxa yokuthi wayesazizwa isidubuli zendlela ende esuka kwaNgcolosi,
washeshe wabeka uhlangothi, walala.

Nokho ubuthongo abusheshanga ukufika.

Wayenakashelwe yimicabango.

Wayecabanga ngoMkabayi.

Wayengakaze ehlulwe yintombi kodwa lokho kakumnikanga isibindi sokuthi
noMkabayi uzomehlula.

Ngenye-ke lentombazana.

Nanxa ingakavuthwa ebuntombini inesithunzi samaqhikiza.

Ugazi lwayo lwamukha umfo kaBhengu.

Wabona ukuthi nxa ingangena emasangweni asesigodlweni sikayise,
angahalaliselwa kuhle kwesihlabani sibuye empini sinqobile.

Nxa engehlulwa nguMkabayi kungangcono angaphinde asikhulumise isidalwa
esingumuntu wesifazane.

Ukuthi intombi kayimnikanga gama kulokhu akucele kuyo akuzange kumhluphe
ULamula.

Wabonga khona nje ukuba imemukele ngomsa, wathokoziswa yindlele ayibone
imkhiyazelela ngayo.

Bathule babhekane futhi omathiloni nosayitsheni bese bekhuluma ngesiBhunu,
ngoba usayitsheni usethatha ucingo bathi ukubonisana ngalo kungathi
bayaphikisana noma kufanele bamnikeze yini lona noma qha, usayitsheni yena uthi
makanganikezwa.

Wafika-ke esangweni waqonda kuNdlovu ukuba amsize ayombizela uNgobese lona
ofundela ubudokotela lapha ngaphakathi.

UNgobese wayekutshele ukuthi ufundela ubudokotela lapha eWits? sekubuza
uNdlovu njengoba nguye obhekene nesango lokungena abahamba ngezinyawo kanti-ke
uMchunu yena ungenisa izimoto lezi asayinise abashayeli uma esezwile ukuthi
kungabe bazofunani.

=Kaniti, ntate, kifuna yena Ngobese=. 

Uqedile iminyaka emihlanu lapha efundela ubudokotela.

Kuzikhalela uNaomi eneka izandla ezilungisa ubala nakhu ugqoke umfaniswana
yobuhlengikazi kanye nebhantshi leli elimnyama elinomfaniswana ebomvu eligqokwa yibona abahlengikazi.

Bathule babhekane oMchunu benoNdlovu.

Nayo lentokazi bayibhekisise.

Cha, yona abaqali ukuba bayibone lapha; konje isuke ifike nobani kulaba
abafundela ubudokotela?

Kube nguMchunu oyikhumbulayo.

Enwaye impandla uma esekhumule isigqoko lesi sobuphoyisa lapha.

Lonke ilanga lanamhlanje nezisebenzi ezinye ziyamangala nje ukuthi ngabe
uZungu uguqulwe yini.

Akanamusa nje.

Kanti nguyena abebezama ukumlingisa bonke ngokuba nobuso obungenguqunguqu.


Unele abe yedwa nje, enhliziyo yakhe ididizele, abone esejuluka nje. 

Kudamane kufika izwi likanembeza lisho lithi akayeke indaba yokuthatha
imali engayinikwanga ngoba uzozibizela amaphoyisa.

Kuthi esekhiphe indodana yakhe ejele isikhundla sayo siyovalwa nguyena
uqobo.

Kusho ukuthi ngcono vele ayeke ihlale ejele indodana kunokuba aze ebe kanti
igama lakhe bese lilihle kangaka. 

Athi uma esebuye ezihlola zonke izinto aqiniseke ukuthi uMaDonela ngeke
abone.

Unemali eningi, futhi akusumuntu onaka izinto kangako.

Kwenye inkathi yena wakwaZungu uke athole imali enkulu nje amnike
uMaDonela.

Futhi-ke ngisho kungalahleka imali manje abasoze basolela kuye.

Kuyophuma inqina nje kupeketulwa kwezinye izisebenzi ngoba kwaziwa ukuthi
yena akasoze athatha lutho anganikiwe.

Nokho inhliziyo yakhe ibe ilokhu ibuhlungu noma enayo nje lemibono.

Ngakusasa avuke ahambe uMaDonela nomkakhe, imoto ize iyoshona ezinkalweni
kude eyibuka uZungu.

Lanele langena endlini nje, inhliziyo yashaya ngamandla ekhehleni.

Sekuyiso phela isikhathi sokuba lenze into elingazange liyicabange selokhu
lafika lapha.

Futhi alizange nje lafundiswa lendlela.

Sekumele lizinikele nje.

Bese liqala ukusebenza njengasemihleni.

Lihambe lishanela lize lingene endlini.

Lishanele phansi.

Lesule lesula, lime. 

Liqalaze ngewindi.

Emva kwalokho liqale ukwesula izintuli nokungcola ezitulweni ezilapha.

Uhambe impela uMaDonela futhi akukho muntu ozongena lapha endlini.

Selisele lodwa ngempela lapha endlini, futhi kalinakubuzwa muntu ukuthi
ngabe lenzani uma kukhona elikwenzayo lapha endlini.

Nezihluthulelo zezindawo zonke ezibalulekile uyazazi, futhi angazithinta
ngokuthanda.

Ingani isethenjwa soqobo.

Kumele silungise kuwo onke amagunjana nala okungangeni muntu omunye kuwo.


Beseliwuthathile ukhiye wekhabethe lapho kuye kuhlale khona imali namanye
amabhuku kaMaDonela.

Ngiqala ukufundisa nje ngingumuntu ozimisele ukuthi angisoze ngaphambuka
endleleni engayikhonjiswayo.

Enyakeni wokuqala khona ngazibonela nje ukuthi kunzima phandle lapha,
izimpisi zibhokile.

Pho nami ngiyazibonela nje ukuthi ngisangcwele impela, angisoleki ndawo.


Pho-ke uma umuntu enento abambelele kuyo enjengenkolo kuthi noma kufika
izikhukhula abambelele.

Nami ngizabalaza nje ngiyathokoza ngobo ngibona ukuthi kuyothi
sebengithatha abangithathayo ngibe sengimsebenzele umama ongithanda kangaka.

Futhi ngiyobayisifundo kubantu bangakithi abesaba ukufundisa amantombazane
bathi azokonakala izimilo.

Waze waphela golokoqo unyaka ngisazabalazile ngoba ngikubona okungamahumusha
lokhu ukuthi akunanjongo etheni kukhuluma nami nje.

Futhi kuthi uma ngikuphosa esikolweni senkolo eyinsika yami kubelula lokhu.

Ngikubone nje okunye ukuthi kuzama ukuzenza amakholwa kuthi kuzongithola
ngesu.

Ngingasho nje ukuthi kwakuze kube nguSipho lo owayengcono ngoba elandela
ezindabeni zasesontweni.

Kodwa naye angicasule ngoba ebhema.

Kwase kungena ubusika ngakho amacece ayeyinsada.

Abanumzane babekhulisa amantombazane abo, babezihlaba ngazimbili
ngazintathu izinkabi, lungekhonto yokuthi inyama ingahle yonakale masinya.
 

ULamula wayesezwile ukuthi kuzoba nelinye futhi icece ngakusasa. 

Ngakho wanquma ukuba angaphindeli emumva engazange edlulise uthi lomzimba
futhi kuMkabayi.

Walala ubuthongo obumnandi-ke umntaka Dlabazane.

Ubuthongo abulala athi kazi kuyosa nini.

Ngakusasa wake wathi ukuxoxa ngezwe lakwaZulu nezinsizwa zakwa Khumalo
lapho ayekhuleke isiKhundla khona.

Wajabula ukubona ukuthi zimesasele kanti futhi zingamadlandaba.

Amaxoxo asheshe abuyela kumntwana wenkosi uJama, inkosazana yakwa Nobamba.

Abe makhulu kakhulu lamazwi ezindlebeni zika Mkabayi.

Akhumbule ukuthi nasendleleni ubebingelelwa ngamazwi acishe afane nalana.


Ngenkathi enqamula emizini yothulasizwe bombuso.

OBiyela, oMpungose, oNtombela nabanye ukuphawulile ukuthi lomoya wegugu
nesasa ayebingelelwa ngawo eya emkhosini kwaBulawayo kawusekho. 

Abantu babelusizana bekhathazekile.

Bonke bebenovalo entanyeni kuhle kwenyoni yona ehlala yethuka izanya ngoba
yazi ukuthi ingahle ibe ukudla kwezagila noma nini.

Aqale ukuzisola uMkabayi.

Okusho ukuthi wathi ukuba abone ukuthi izinto zihamba kahle mhla eye
emkhosini kwaBulawayo; wabe eseba nokudebesela okuthile.

Akabe esawunaka umbuso kaNdaba.

Kodwa phela wayecabanga ukuthi uShaka uqhuba ngendlela.

Abanumnzane edlula kubo babekufakazela lokho.

Yilokho okwamenza ahlale phansi akhihlike.

Kanti kuzothi kulokhokuhlala kwakhe konakale izinto.

Kusho khona ngempela ukuthi umbuso ufana nenkomo yona okufaneka ihlale
yelusiwe.

Nxa ungayelusi intshontshwa ngamasela okanye ithunjwe ngaba phangi
kungenjalo kwayona inkomo leyo ikudalela amacala ngokudla amasimu abantu.

Kodwa phela ubecabanga ukuthi isizwe sesimtholile umelusi onguShaka,
umelusi obedlula bonke abanye.

Nakhu-ke uDingane esembingelela ngalamazwi ashaqisayo,

Nokho ucabanga ukuthi isikhalo esikhulu uyasazi.

Abantu abaningi edlule kubo balibekile elokuthi uShaka ulibhubhisile izwe
ekushoneni kweNdlovukazi, uNandi.

Umthetho kaShaka wokuthi bonke labo abangamlileli mababulawe waletha
olukhulu usizi ezweni.

Baningi abafayo bengenacala.

Abanye babekubulala hhayi ngoba benamagqubu nawe kodwa ngoba befuna
ukuziveza nokuzenza bahle kuShaka.

Kuthe lapho abantu sebecabanga ukuthi seledlule lelofu elimnyama, uShaka
wabuye washaya eminye imithetho enzima esizweni.

Phela wanquma ukuba kuzilwe unyaka wonke.

Wathi amadoda azile amakhosikazi awo.

Inkosikazi etholakele, ikhulelwe ngalesosikhathi ibulawe.

Wathi amasoka azile izintombi zawo.

Wathi izinkomo ezizele zingasengwa, amankonyane ahambe nonina.

Wathi amasimu angalinywa.

Aselinyiwe angahlakulwa.

Ukudla kwangcengca okhuleni abantu baqothulwa ngumshayandawonye.

Phela ichwane lemvubu alikaze lidliwe yingwenya qede kucwebe iziziba.
Ngeke!

Asho sengathi uphelelwa umoya. 

Athi qimu ngomhlane.

Aphuthume kumkakhe elandelwa nguJakobe.

Umuntu useyimbune nje.

Bamthele ngabandayo, athi ukuqabuka.

Mnewethu! Sesiwuzwile umbiko wakho osidabula izinhliziyo kabili.

Akukho esingabe sisakukhuluma uma sekunje.

Ngicela ukusishiye, Ndima, kesishaywe umoya.

Qhubeka nokufuna, mnewethu, kodwa usazise uma uthuke uwuvusa umkhondo.


Empeleni sengathi ungawuvusa ngoba kungenjalo asisayuphinde singenelane.


Angikusongeli ngokusho njalo, kodwa ngithi ake usishayise umoya.

Nathi sizosale sifuna ngendlela esifuna ngayo.

Ngikuzwa kahle, ntandane kababa. 

Namazwi aqatha owasho kimi, akufanele mfowethu, ngakho angikubambeli gqubu.


Ngiyazi nginecala.

Nokho ngizolithwala.

Elokugcina nje wukuba nginikhumbuze ukuthi nakimi kusika njengoba kusika
nakini.

Kazi usho okunjani ukuyingena ngoba uthe shi.

Isimanga wukuthi muva nje unolukhulu uzwelo ngoNdima.

Kazi ukuthengisele inyama yamalini.

Mina nje ngiyintombi kaMkhondolo akudikizi ngisho inqulu ngoBhekuzalo wabo
lowo.

Futhi nje noma angalubheka uzalo, uyobheka lolo lwakwaNdima, hhayi
olwakwaThango.

Asazike njengoba engabonakali nje ukuthi uyolubheka kwabaphansi yini lolo
zalo.

MaThango asehlukane ngingaze ngikwenze kabi mina. 

Ngiyabona awubazi abantu wena.

Ukuba wumngani wakho ngeke ngikuthenge ngokuchwenswa nguwe mina. 

Uma ushiseka ngezomndeni wakho ungalokothi ugaxe uThembi phakathi.

Sala sikhohlakali ndini. 

Hawu! Kazi ngangicabanga ukuthi ungaba ngumngani wami nje ngangiphuze
obamaganu yini. 

Mngani wami, asingaxatshaniswa yizinto ezincane.

Ithafa lagcwala izinqola zamaBhunu. Wasuka-ke uMnumzane uPieter =Retief=
nabathile abangafikile emashumini amabili, behamba neNgisi elalizobahumushela,
baqonda khona eMgungundlovu emzini omkhulu kaDingane.

Amehlo akhe aba esinye isimo manje, kawabesagcwala igazi.

Asuka akhanya aba izinhlansi.

Avuleka athi bha, okwawomuntu ovuleka ingqondo ebona izinto akade
engaziboni.

Kwabonakala ukuthi impi akade eyilwa nenhliziyo yakhe uyinqobile.

Usekwazi azokwenza.

Waphefumula kwasengathi umoya uphuma wonke emzimbeni.

Uthe esuka lapho wayebiza inceku, ethi kayibize uNzobo, ithi ingambiza
ilethe izinkamba ezimbili zotshwala, olunye ilunike yena uNzobo, olunye
luzophuza nguye uDingane uqobo lwakhe.

Wangena uNzobo, kodwa uDingane kazakhuluma naye, wamhlalisa ngesandla
phansi.

Wahlala uNzobo emangele ukuthi ingabe kwenzenjani; naye uDingane uzihlalele
laphaya enhla nendlu kuyo indawo yakhe ayejwayele ukuzihlalela kuyo.

Dukuduku angene uSilwane ephethe ukhamba lweNkosi, alubeke phambi
kukaDingane.

Aqale akhuleke, besekhothama esusa ingwebu.

Aphume futhi, usebuya nolukaNzobo.

Uselubeka phambi kwakhe' ekhothama esusa ingwebu.

Uzithulele uthe du uDingane' ubheke phansi.

Selokhu engenile uNzobo amehlo kaDingane kawahlangani nempela nawakhe.

Uzibhekele phansi. Useqala ukushaywa uvalo manje uNzobo.

Usezifuna enhliziyweni ukuthi angabe wenzeni konje angase abulawele lona
nguDingane.

Ayigeqe impela ingqondo yakhe, efuna isici angabe usenzile esingabangela
iNkozi yakhe imbulale kabi, angasitholi: kodwa uvalo lugcwale enhliziyweni
yakhe; ezwe efikelwa ukubanda emzimbeni sengathi ushaywa umoya woKhahlamba.

Ethuke agxume uNzobo lapho ezwa izwi likaDingane kade engalilindele, futhi
libanda kangako.

Iningi lawo impi yawafica elele ebusuku.

Into eyaba buhlungu kakhulu ukuthi nezulu labe lingelihle neze
ngalezonsuku.

Lalide lina nsuku zonke, namaBhunu ehleli inhlalo embi yokukhandleka
impela.

Yawafikela impi ebusuku engazelele lutho nempela, kade ezingela nje emini,
amakhosikazi ezihlalele emakhaya nezingane.

Phela labo babesalinde ukubuya kukaPieter =Retief= neqembu lelo ayehamba
nalo, kuyiwa eMgungundlovu.

Wazenzela emaBhunwini elele ebusuku, kazakhetha ndoda, nkosikazi, ngane,
wabhokoda ngemikhonto, igazi lagobhoza okomfula.

Into eyabambi futhi ukuthi imizi yamaBhunu yayigqagqene yonke: omunye
ulaphaya, omunye ulaphayana.

Kawakwazi ukushesha ahlangane azivikele - azumeka.

Kodwa kuthe lapho impi isabhubhisa kweminye imizi babevuka abakhelene nayo
abanye, bezilungiselela ukulwa; bazidela amathambo, abanye babhaca ezintabeni.

Kuthe kanti ethi uZulu ubesewaqedile ebusuku, kanti amaBhunu ansondo
asindileyo alindele ukusa.

Asehloma ephelela.

Lithe lithi chaphasha ilanga, liphuma, sasikhala isibhamu.

Ayafika belu amanye avela kweminye imizi.

Afika esethukuthele asexhaphe igazi.

Izinqola lezi asezimise zaba yizigungu, wawubona ngamehlo nemilomo yezibhamu
kulunguze ezintubeni.

Izibhamu sezihlohlwa ngamakhosikazi nabantwana.

Waqala uZulu ukuhlehla manje.

Uthe ukuba ahlehle, aphuma manje ezinqoleni amaBhunu, amsukela uZulu.

Lapho kwafa abantu izinhlangothi zombili.

"Hawu, nithini?" kubuza uDingane, egxuma.

Ngamthethelela ngoba eliqhawe.

"Hawu, kasazi nathi, Nkosi.

Ubesibizele utshwala bakhe.

Kepha kuthe lapho buthungwa sabona umhlapho untanta phezulu.

Kubuzisisa uDingane, sengathi keziswanga.

Usethuma uNdlela uDingane ukuba aye kobiza uSokufoca.

Uthe lapho esefika naye wammisa phambi kweNkosi.

Wasethi kuye uDingane: "Sokufoca."

"Ndabezitha." Useguqa phansi ngamadolo.

"Qha, Ndaba, kangisiye, Nkosi.

Nami ngethukile kakhulu lapho ngibona umhlapho untanta etshwaleni bami.

Mina bengithe bekuqondwe ukubulawa mina nje, Ndaba."

"Nxephe, Ndaba," esezikhalela uSokufoca.

"Nami impela kangiyiqondi nempela indaba yalobutshwala."

Hawu, bamangale bonke lapho bezwa uDingane ethi kahambe uSokufoca
engambulali.

Kanti baluqeda lolu uSenzangakhona. Useza.

izinduna ngoba ebanga nazo ubunduna.

Wabe ngasenakuphika lutho emuva kwaloko uSokufoca.

Wabulawelwa kwaMatiwane.

Okwaba kuhle kakhulu impela yikuthi inkosana kaSokufoca uTokothi nayo

Qha; wayinqumela izinkomo wathi kayakhe umuzi wayo.

Kwabahlaba umxhwele abantu lokho kwenza kweNkosi okuyimvelakancane.

Kuthi uma sekuhlangenwe nje kuxoxwe ngalabantu, kukhonjiswane nezithombe.


Sengizotholoza nje mina, akumnandi-ke lokho.

Nokho-ke lobobunzima abukangigudluzi emgomeni wami.

Kwathi ngelinye ilanga sisesitolo nenye inkosazana esasifundisa nayo

Ingamunwe nje ifake iyembe elimhlophe elinemikhono emifishane.

Emehlweni lapha ifake izibuke zelanga.

Amadevu lana iwancwele ngobunono obukhulu.

Yangena yafike yathenga iphakethe letiye.

Ithe uma iphenduka ibheka ngakithi ngashaywa uvalo engingalwazi ukuthi

Ngase ngiphenduka ngibuka ezimpahleni.

Izinkulumo zabantu nazo azipheli edolobheni laBantu besho lokhu nalokhuya

Naye uMaNkosi akasabonwa ngisho nasesontweni.

Bobabili bagoyile ekhaya lapha.

Uyasoleka uThulisile.

Waba yinkathi eselweneka udaba lonke uXhakaza nesisusa sengxabano kanye

Nango-ke esethi usaya ngaphandle uzosheshe abuye. 

Omunye umcabango wami wathi angihambe naye, ngabuye ngazikhuza ngathi

Muntu uzobuya, muntu uzobuya, phinde uSiziba.

Akusashiwo-ke manje ukuthi liyaduma izulu.

Angikhumbuli impela liduma kanjeya.

Ngize ngizilahle manje ngiyotshela abafana bami kwenye indlu.

Akusadlalwa manje.

Ake ngiphinde ngichithe amathambo ami ngizwe ukuthi sekunjani manje.

UMusa-ke naye uthe angabuya esontweni, wase ezihlalela lapha endlini ethi
uyafundafunda, kodwa sabhoka isizungu yize ubeziduduza ngokuvulela umsakazo.

Uthe ngoba nebhantshi ubefike walikhumula, wase ethi okungenani makelule
izinyawo akashaywe nangumoya nakhu ngisho nakhona lapha edolobheni laBantu
eMpophomeni, ugcina nje ebuka ekude.

Avale-ke endlini bese ezihambela nje edla ingadi bese indlebe yakhe
ithathwa yinhlokomo yomsindo abantu bememeza, abanye beshaya izandla bese
ekhumbula ukuthi konje bekuke kwaxoxwa ukuthi kuzobe kufike abadlali
baseSweetwaters abazobe bedlala neqembu leli lalaphaya eNjolobeni.

Aphelela kuyena wonke amanzi lawo angcolile.

Ucwecwele kuwona amazambane wabuye wawagezela kuwona futhi - anodaka kanye
nawo amakhasi lawo amazambane.

Eme lapho aphubuke ahleke. 

Umame naye adinge ukuthi kodwa uzoxolisa athini ngalento aseyenzile.

"Ngixolele kakhulu bandla, thisha.

Okungenani, sala sewungena khona lapha endlini ungaze uhlekwe abantu
abadlulayo, mfana wami."


Naye bandla uMaNkosi usebhajaza nje ukuthi kodwa lomuntu amthele ngamanzi

Phela uma bekuyilaba abalapha edolobheni laBantu, ngakube sekukhulunywa
ezinye zisuka nje phansi, ngoba bona abasichithi isikhathi nakancane - babuza
sebegalele.

UMusa bese elihlangula ikhasi leli elilenga kuye ehlombe, kodwa lusale lona
udaka lapha ejezini naseyembeni namakhasana katamatisi lawa abelapha emanzini,
bese elandela lomame beyongena endlini.

Naye phela uMusa wethuke ngakhona. 

Athi uyaluthatha ucingo lolo, ethuke seluqathakele phansi.

Alucoshe uMtshali bese ebona ukuthi isandla siyaqhaqhazela, sesinedumbe
lapha kuMusa.

Amtatamise aye amhlalise phezu kombhede.

Obembuka uMusa ngenkathi ezihambela eziqinele, eyoshona endlini yabo,
uzibonele uma esehamba kancane ukuthi kukhona okonakele, ngoba nakhu esexhakwe
nguMtshali sebeyongena endlini.

Naye lomfana waseposini bambonile eyoshona ngakhona esikoleni. 

Lwaze lwavulwa uyena uMtshali esemnikeza uMusa ukuba alufunde.

Ucingo lubika ukuthi uMaMhlongo useze wathuthelwa esibhedlela kwaMakhotho
=McCord's Hospital=.

Kuyisifiso sakhe uMaMhlongo ukuba ambone uMusa.

Laduma-ke manje ikhanda kuMusa: uzokwenzenjani lokhu nemali kayikho
njengoba inyanga izophela ngesonto elizayo.

Ibhuku lakhe, leli akhweza kulo, angaze ayokhipha eMgungundlovu.

Kube nguMtshali-ke manje osemduduza ezama nokummisa isibindi, ngoba nangu
esechiphiza izinyembezi.

Bayixoxe nayo indaba yemali kuthi bengakaqedi, nakhu sekudum' ithekisi
khona lapha egcekeni sekuphuma uMaNkosi ephuma eqonda khona lapha endlini.

Usho njalo uMaNkosi uyeza uqonde khona lapha endlini yezimpohlo.

"Bheka, ngoba lufika nje ucingo, ubesangilandisa ukuthi unina ugula kabi
kanti nalu ucingo lusendleleni .... muphi yena uMusa ngimbone?"

UmfokaMtshali lokhu yena akasiye nomuntu ojwayelene nabo oNaNkosi laba,
futhi akasiye nomuntu okhulumela futhi, wasimze azithulele nje agqolozele
uMaNkosi ezwe kuthi xhifi uma emuzwa impela esembiza ngegama uthisha Xaba.


Ngisho njalo, uthisha Xaba?" lisho njalo liyasondela ishobolo elinguMaNkosi
- uxamu kavinjelwa ongabuzwa.

Cha, uMtshali ayivimbe indlela ngokuba eme khona emnyango uqobo.

"Uma ungafuni ukuba ngingene, ngibizele yena avele lapha khona sizohamba
naye uma ngabe uya ngaseMgungundlovu."

"Odokotela bafike bathola ukuthi isifuba sakhe kasizwani nendawo ephakemeyo
futhi emakhaza njengaseGoli yikho nje ebuyile uThuli," sekusho uMaNkosi uma
ekhonzela uThulisile kuMusa behlangana esitolo. 

Azethukise naye uMusa kube sengathi lendaba uyiqabuke ngayekhona lapha
kwaNogqaza.

"Into nje nami, ndodana, uma sengikhuluma iqiniso lonke, ngangivele
ngingathandisisi ukuba uThulisile aye ezibhedlela zaseGoli futhi abe kude
nasekhaya.

Ekuhambeni lapha, umntwana uhlangana nabantu bezinhlobonhlobo zezimilo
abanye abangenazo uqobo." 

Sekusho ishobolo elinguMaNkosi mhla behlangana okokuqala selokhu bevulile.


"Cha, Mame, ngakube kade ngafika, into bengingazi ukuthi ulapha kanti
uThulisile," sekulandula uMusa.

Ngisho nabantu balapha eMpophomeni bambalwa kakhulu asebeke bambona
uThulisile.

Bagcina nje bezwe ngendaba ukuthi ikhona indodakazi kaMaNkosi.

Uma uqabuke wambona, uyomfica egqoke ijazi ngisho noma libalele kanjani.


Akalubeki unyawo esontweni.

Kuwona nje lawomasonto, wethuka uMusa, ngoba esethola incwadi eyayivela
kuLungile esibhedlela.

Kulencwadi kwakukhona incwadi eyabe ibhalwe ngowesifazane isongela uLungile
ukuthi makehlukane noMusa uma engafuni ukufa ngokubulawa ngezandla.

Isizathu salokho, kusho umbhali wencwadi leyo, wukuthi uMusa unezingane
ezimbili naye umbhali.

Ekuphetheni kwencwadi, angaze alibhala igama lakhe.

UMusa uthe uma eyifunda incwadi lena ebukisisa nemvilaphu, wathola ukuthi
yabe iposwe eMgungundlovu.

Wathula wathula wase eyithatha incwadi ngelinye ilanga ntambama,
esevakashela kwaMaNkosi efika ezidlalela ugubhu njengokujwayelekile.

Uthe uma esehamba, wase eyishiya ngabomu yona incwadi leyo phezu kogubhu.


Walindela-ke ngakusasa ethi bazothumela babuze ukuthi akakhohlwanga yilutho
yini ekhaya ngangayizolo, kodwa phinde babuze.

Wathi noma esefika yena qobo lwakhe ngeSonto, ethi bazoke bambuze, noma
kambe bamtholisele ngayo incwadi leyo, phinde.

Kwazikhanyela ukuthi kanti lokhu abekuzindla ukuthi ngubani owabe ebhale
leyoncwadi, wazithulela umntakaXaba wayethumela abakhongi ngePhasika ukuba
bayokokha umlilo kwaGumede.`

Athule lapho umfundisi Mahlombe abheke phansi ehluleke ngisho
nawukukhuluma.

Okokuqala, ubengazange akasho ukuthi osifundile isahluko leso makeze lapha
ngaphambili.

Bekwenele nje ukuba uma uGatsheni esifundile isahluko leso, aphakamise
isandla esendaweni yakhe.

Kusho khona nje ukuthi uGatsheni ulisakabuli - unontanda kubukwa yibandla
leli.

Yathi ukuba ingene esigodlweni sikaDingane, yangena maqede washaywa
uvalo uDingane, kwazise ukuthi yabe inesithunzi esesabekayo kakhulu.

Kusho yena umfundisi efikelwa ngamahloni. 

Amlindele uGatsheni aze ayohlala endaweni yakhe ehamba esho oAmeni bakhe
laba bemihla.

"Uma libandla nikhumbula kahle, ngathi ngesonto eledlule ngizobe
ngishumayela ngesifo samanga ngaze nganicela ukuba nize nifunde isahluko leso
athi umfowethu othandekayo wasifunda waze wasiphinda kabili isahluko leso
sikaGenesisi wamashumi ayisi-90."

Athi ukuthula lapho umfundisi Mahlombe, bese eqisa amehlo ngaphezulu
kwezibuko zakhe.

Impela, bazalwane, mangisho ngokusobala ukuthi amanga lawa ayisifo esibi
esilethwa nguSathane.

Amanga futhi awanaso ngisho nesincane isibusiso empilweni yomuntu ngakho-ke
masiwexwaye amanga.

Nami-ke njengoba ngangishilo, namhlanje ngizoshumayela ngesifo samanga lesi
esabhubhisa oAnaniya benoSafira.

Namhlanje nakhu sesiphoxe umzalwane ebesimethemba futhi simhlonipha lapha
enkonzweni yethu.

Ngithanda ukusho ngokusobala ukuthi makube yisifundo kinina nonke ukuthi
amanga lawa ayinto eyisono futhi elethwa nguSathane.

Bheka ngoba asikho lesosahluko eBhayibhelini, kodwa nangu umzalwane, uyasho
uyaqinisa ukuthi usifundile isahluko leso.

Aze asho nokuthi uze wasiphinda kabili.

Bazalwane eNkosini, xwayani amanga, ngoba akanayo nakancane imbuyiselo.

Wathi eqeda ukusho lawomazwi, wabe eqala ingoma yakhe ayikhonze kakhulu
umfundisi Mahlombe, lena ethi, "Bayomiswa phambi kweNkosi," kwaduma indlu yonke.

Lathi ibandla liyiqeda ingoma leyo, wabe engena entshumayelweni yakhe
umfundisi Mahlombe.

Selokhu ngashintshelwa KwaNgwanase nje lo msebenzi wethu wesitolo
angiwuboni into osasenzela yona.

Engikubonayo nje yizona izikweletu esezingene zagamanxa ekhukhwini kimi.


Isitolo sesiyehluleka ukuzikhokhela ngisho ezaso izikweletu lezi.

Eyenzuzoke yona angifuni nokuyiphatha nje ngoba ukucabanga inzuzo
akwehlukene nokuphupha emini kulona owethu umsebenzi.

Sengiyazisola ngokuchitha yonke imali yami engayiqongelela kanzima kangaka
ngakha lesi sakhiwo, kusho uKhuluse kumkakhe uMaMhlongo owayesedume ngelika
`Njoms' elokishini lase Wembezi, eMtshezi. 

UMaMhlongo owayefika nje ngakho kodwa noSiqeda umshayeli wakhona lapha
esitolo bevela kothenga impahla yakhona esitolo, amcasula la mazwi omyeni wakhe.


Waphendula ngokuhlohloloza wathi, `Uye ungehlule nje wena Khuluse ngoba
ucabangisa okwengane ekhasayo.

Siyasebenza sinoSiqeda noMakhilomitha, siyazikhandla sizama ukuba umsebenzi
ulethe inzuzo.

Kodwa konke lokho kuwena kungukusinisa amahleza nje. 

Sengiyingane namhlanje MaMhlongo?' kubhavumula uKhuluse. 

Indaba yenqubekela phambili esitolo sakwaKhuluse yaphela mhla esuswa
endaweni yakubo kuthiwa akayokweluleka kwezolimo KwaNgwanase endaweni
yaseNgwavuma.

Lokhu kushintshwa kwakhe kwabangela ukuba uMaMhlongo awuphathe yena
ngokugcwele umsebenzi wasesitolo.

Wayesethatha izinqumo, athenge impahla, aqashe abasebenzi aphathe nemali.

Nanxa izinto zake zathi ukuhamba kahle ezinyangeni ezimbili eqalile
uKhuluse ukusebenza KwaNgwanase, zaqala izikweletu zasesitolo ukuba ngaphezu
kwamandla.

Impahla yayithengiswa kepha ingabuyisi nzuzo.

Kwasekubuya leyo mali ebekade kuthengwe ngayo kuphela.

Ngokuqhubeka kwesikhathi kwayona okwakuthengwe ngayo ayikwazanga ukuba
isabuya.

UKhuluse kwakumumangalisa ukubona impahla ingekho esitolo kepha nemali ibe
ilandulwa, uma evakashele ekhaya.

Ekugcineni wabuye wabona umonakalo ungaphezulu kokwakungathathwa ngozwane
amagundane.

Wayethi uma ebuza kuMaMhlongo ukuthi kwakwenzekani emsebenzini wabo amane
ambhokele ngolaka athi akayeke phansi abeluleki bezolimo uzoziphathela yena
mathupha isitolo sakhe uma engeneliswa yimizamo  yabo noSiqeda noMakhilomitha,
bezama ukusisimamisa.

Wayethi uyabethuka uma ekhononda kanjalo, uqonde ukuthi imali esetshenzwa
yisitolo bona bayayisobozela `Sekuyangesinda MaMhlongo ukuthwala umsebenzi
wesitolo ngomholo wami,' kusho uKhuluse kumkakhe ngolunye usuku evakashile
ekhaya.

'Phephisa mama. Bengingaboni ukuthi kushayeka wena,' kuthayiza
uThengezakhe.

Ngale nkathi uThembekile wayemi eceleni komnyango esabibitheka.

'Ubungaboni ukuthi ushaya mina nje ubuthi ushaya bani?' Kuphinda unina
ebuza.

'Bengithi ngishaya lo mfazi ongangazi ukuthi ngiyindoda,' kuphendula
uThengezakhe.

'Akakwazi ukuthi uyindoda yakhe ngokwenzanjani Thengezakhe? Akakuphekeli?
Akakuwasheli? Akalali endlini? Ngiyabuza?' Kufutheka uMaSithole.

'Kunini ngimtshela ukuthi akapheze ukungibuza ipasi nesipesheli uma
ngizelukele ngiyindoda?' Kusho uThengezakhe.

Uma engakubuzi lokho ngubani onelungelo lokukubuza lokho.

'Ingani ngiyamelapha? Uma eyinyumba mina nithi angenzenjani?' Kuhlohloloza
uThengezakhe.

Mina nginezingane zami eziyisithupha ezintombini zami eziyisithupha.


Kungethi nje ngoba akukho neyodwa esadla amabele kuzona.

Kusontwa nje uGatsheni ujuluka kancane lapha emhlane - ujuluka nje
limakhaza phandle.

Umjuluko waze wawuzwa sewehla ngomgogodla imbala.

Kodwa lona isonto liyoze liphume nini azigodukele.

Nokho abuye aziduduze ngokuthi kubengcono, ngoba ubengekho uMaMthethwa
lapha enkonzweni yanamuhla.

Kwathi nje ingaphuma inkonzo, wabe engena indlela uGatsheni wawashiya
amakholwa esabuzana impilo exhawulisana emva kwenkonzo njengento ejwayelekile.


Kwathi lapho unyaka ugamenxe, ngalanga limbe bavuswa uMchunu ezonxusa yena
uMuzi ukuthi angeze asiza ahambise abakhongi bakaNtombizini abayise eManzimtoti
lapho besebenza khona.

Lokhu naye uMchunu wazifikela nje engekho noVelaphi, akufikanga ngisho
nokusola ukuthi uMchunu lo uhlobene noVelaphi.

Bathi uma bezama ukubonisana ngenani angalibiza uMuzi, wazibika kuqala
ukuthi indaba yemali angaze ayilinganisa eselibonile ibanga lelo.

"Into mina engiyibona ingabangcono, wukuba size sibahambise laba
abakwaXimba siye sibabeke emakhaya, bese-ke sibonisana ngezindleko kamuva,"
kusho uMuzi.

"Impela ngingabonga kakhulu wena kaNjomane ngoba lababantu basebenza kude
kanti kufanele sibahambise khona ebusuku ngosuku lomcelo," sekubonga yena
uMchunu evalelisa.

Nebala-ke lwafika usuku lomcelo kaNtombizini.

UVelaphi akayiphathi nakuyiphatha nalendaba yokucelwa kukuNtombizini.

Ngisho nayo indaba yokuhlobana kwabo oVelaphi noNtombizini, waze wayiqabuka
ngaye uZamekile uma esemtshela ukuthi uNtombizini lowo, nguye owayemeshelela
uVelaphi.

"Mina uma benginguwe, bengingeke ngiye kulowomcelo waseMaMchunwini,"
sekusho uZamekile lapho kade beluxoxa loluhambo.

"Ngingayeka kanjani, ngoba sengavuma ukuthi ngiyobahambisa abakhongi labo?"
kusho uMuzi eqala amanye amehlo.

"Impela igazi lami lithanda ukungishiya uma ngiyizwa lendaba ngabanye
abantu wena ungasangitshelanga lutho ngokwakho," kubelesela uZamekile.

"Angisakwazi ukuyeka, ngoba sakhuluma ngesonto eledlule ngavuma.

Manje bangathi ngigumuntu onjani uma sengishaya ingwijikhwebu emini
libalele?" nakuMuzi akusemnandi manje.

"Bengingathi wathatha nomuthi esokeni lakho ukuba ubulale iNkosi."

Ake ubheke, ngoba ngisho noVelaphi uqobo lwakhe uyakufihlela ukuthi
uyisihlobo sakhona.

Uthi ukwenzelani lokho uma ingekho inyoka esesikhwameni?" kusho uZamekile.


Behlukana lapho kuqundeka amehlo esemphelezele ngemoto eyombeka kwaKhathi
lapho ehlala khona.

Wathi efika esitolo, wayesefica incwadi evela kwaMchunu yokuthi sebelindele
yena ukuba abathathe laba abasemzini.

Wathi esathi uzothumela umuntu wokuba ayobika ukuthi kukhona akusolayo
emotweni, wethuka sekufika yena uMchunu uqobo lwakhe ngenjomane.

"Uma wawungafuni, wawungasho ngani ekuqaleni ukuze sizame abanye abantu
abanezimoto?" kubhoka uMchunu ehla nje ehhashini.

Engani ngezwa umoyana wokuthi usacelwa nje? sekubuza uZondo. 

Thina intombi uma sibona ukuthi idlala inkawu, kufanele siyiduduze! kusho
yena uZungu ehleka kancane.

Bayihleke impela leyondaba yakhe noThembi, ngoba wayephika elala ngomhlane,
kodwa namuhla useyivuma esezibonga ngayo.

UXhakaza yena ayiphethe ngokuthi, "Impela sesiyakhuluma namuhla, ngoba
nakhu seladuma ledlula ngoba uMaNkomo wayelimisa ngesihloko ukuthi ngamhla
ngawubeka umcondo emzini wakhe, uyongithela ngamanzi abilayo.

Selize ladlula, ngoba nakhu uThembi lowo esashada wasuka lapha kwaMakhutha,
ngoba wayeyizwe yonke indaba ukuthi uqonde ukuwuchitha umuzi wakhe." 

Kuthi ukuthula kancane lapho uZungu ephuma evala amafasitele emotweni.


"Madoda, thina sisaya emabhasini afinyelela ekhaya kusakhanya," sekuvalelisa
uZondo eqoqa amaphephandaba lawa abewafunda.

Thina bothina laba, singakutshela libe linye nje elokuthi umkakho kufanele
umfundise zisuka nje phansi ukuthi nguwe owaba imali njengendoda.

Uma umkakho uzomejwayeza ukuthi kube nguye okunqumelayo, esazi nemali
oyiholayo emsebenzini, kuyothi lapho sewubika lokhu nalokhuya, bese ekudla
akufele athi sekukhona abakufaka umoya wezikhova.

Ungakhohlwa phela Thiyane, ukuthi umfazi umbona edela ikubo elifudumele
nje, azogana, usuke eqonde khona ukuba azokwengamela isikhwama sakho semali -
ubobuza lapha kithina, mfanakithi."

Sekusho uMthalane ehleka kakhulu.

"Engabe uyasho lapho, nfokaMthalane, indlela yaziwa ngumhambi wayo!"
sekusho uXhakaza ehleka kakhulu.

Kodwa phela kuliqiniso lokho, ngoba nami ngihlezi nje uMaKhumalo akazi
ukuthi ngihola malini emsebenzini, ngoba lokho kungasixabanisa.

Mina ngimnikeza lokho engimnikeza khona naye emukele abonge anconcoze.

Kodwa phela asingakhohlisani, madoda, ngoba nayo imizi lena kayakhiwe
ngokufana.

Kufana nazo izibongo lezi zabantu ezingefani.

Uma ungase uthathe izeluleko ozithola ebandleni, ufike uthi uzama leyonto
oyizwe beyixoxa, uyohamba umfazi. 

Nidla imali yami manje senizama nokungikhohlisa senidlala ngokufa!
esho eyigaxa eyomngenisa ngayo ekamelweni.

Kwaze kwancenga yena futhi uDlamini uma sebengene endlini ukuthi okungenani
makamnikeze ithuba lokuba angene ekamelweni ayogqoka ukuze balusingathe udaba
lolu amshayela lona. 

Wathi noma ethi uyangqongqotha lapha kuMaNkomo, wenqaba waphetha ukuba
amvulele, ngoba uyizwile yona imvubu uMaNkomo.

Wethuka ngokunye naye uDlamini uma esefica ukuthi kukhona nomkhonto nomzaca
lapha endlini naye wakhuza ekhuzile manje.

Kahle phela, mfokaXhakaza, asikhulume njengamadoda.

Ngiyavuma ukuthi angisigcinanga isethembiso sami, kodwa-ke asikhulume
njengamadoda wemukele lokho enginakho esandleni okuseleyo, ngizobuye
ngikulungisele, kuzikhalela uZungu eqalaza, ngoba nazi izikhali zikaXhakaza
afike nazo usethembele kuyena umakhelwane wakhe ukuthi uyolamula uma kusuka
isidumo. 

Wabe eqonda esicabheni sasekamelweni eshaya isicabha ememeza ethi, MaNkomo,
letha leyomali ebesiyibala ekuseni engamakhulu amabili.

Leli elinye ikhulu sengokunika kusasa uma sengibuya eManzimtoti. 

"Ayisekho indaba yakusasa lapha kimi - ngiyifuna lapha yonke imali yami uma
ningafuni ukuba ngishiye ngikhiphe isidumbu sangempela kulomuzi wenu
wokungcola!" washo efutheka lapho ebuka umzaca kusobala usecabanga nokuba
agalele lapha ekhanda. 

Wabuka uDlamini uZungu okusobala usezincengela ukuthi makalamule.

Kungcono kona ukwethemba lona itshe - ngigeze izandla! kusho uXhakaza
ewabala amakhulu amabili lawo.

Pho yena uMakoti uma ayezala angazala kanjani wena usuwaba ngumgulukudu
nje, into ehamba ilala ishiya izingane ezintabeni? Kukhankatha unina.

'Noma kunganjalo Mama akanakungibuza ngiyindoda ukuthi bengilelephi.'

'Ngena weKoti!' Kusho uMaSithole. 

Wangena esenaso isilokozane uThembelile.

Kuhle ukhumbule ukuthi uMakoti lona ngowami.

Yimina engakulobolela yena ngemali yami yempesheni.

Wawungenawo ngisho upeni wodwa lona ulahlekelwe ngumsebenzi, ngakho njalo
ukuzenza umhogwane. 

Umntanomuntu lona mina ungiphethe kahle kabi.

Uyangondla. Uyanginakekela. Ungipha ukudla, uyangiwashela, ungipha nemithi
yami yodokotela, ungenzela konke.

Uzongivusela izifo zami esehayihayi nesenhliziyo uma uqhubeka nokumphatha
kanje.

Empeleni uma umshaya akwehlukene nokuthi ubeka mina uqobo isandla njengoba
nempela usukwenzile nje lokho. 

Makoti, lala mntanami.

Ngeke esakwenza lutho lona, kweluleka uninazala.

Kokunye ukonakala kobukhosana kudalwa yithina bazali.

Kwenye inkathi boniwa ngontanga balabo abazalelwe ebukhosaneni.

Ngiyabona ukuthi ukusetshenziswa kwelobundlalifa okunukubeza ubukhosana.

Kusuke kuqhakambiswe ukuthi ubukhosana buyilungelo lobundlalifa. 

Kungumkhuba omubi kabi ukugcingca izingane zisencane umoya wobukhosana.

Yizona kanye lezi zingane eziba amakhosana angasile.

Yilo lolu hlobo lwamakhosana okuduma ubundlalifa emakhanda kuwo
engakafinyeleli nasebangeni lobukhosana.

Aphoxa leli siko lakithi.

Ayahlupheka amantombazane.

Wona eyawo ayiphathwa nakuphathwa uma inkosana seyaba ifa, uma ngabe
iyababela abanawayo.

Ngisho nenkosazana ayelamayo lona oseyinkosana ayibe isanakwa kwakunakwa.


Iphenduka ize leze.

Ubukhosana nobukhosazana yinto yinye.

Nenkosazana ingaba yindlalifa.

Kunjalo kwezinye izizwe.

Ingababela abafowabo nodadewabo ifa.

Mhlawumbe yona ingaba nanesandla nanokuba nesandla ekwabeni.

Nobukhosana bomame bukhona ngokwesiZulu.

Lobo bukhosana phela yibo ubukhosazana lobu.

Nanxa inkosazana ingenalungelo lokwabelwa nokwaba ifa, kodwa iyahlonishwa
ngobukhosazana bayo.

Izindaba zomndeni ezinohlonze azilokothwa zidingidwe ngaphandle kwayo.

Ngisho ngabe seyenda, iyalandwa emzini izoveza amakhambi ekuxazulekekeni
kwezinkinga zakwabo.

Izwi layo aliweli phansi. 

Thina kwethu kithina inkukhu yayinqunywa umlomo uma uNtombizini kaBaba
esethe:`Ngiyintombi kaMbikwa ngithi akwenzeki lokho lapha ekhaya!'

OBaba babesixoxela ukuthi nabo babethula swayi uma sekukhulume umafungwase
wakwabo uPhikelela.

Bebeyizeka indaba bathi; ukuhlonipha inkosazana nabo babekufunde
kobabamkhulu, okwakuma zonke izindaba ezinqala zomndeni uma engekho
uNomanjebese.

Ngisho kunomsebenzi ekhaya kugingqwe ubugingqigingqi bezinkabi, inkosazana
inendawo yayo kwabo.

Angazi-ke nami ukuthi ihlala kuphi nesilili noma kwehluka ngokungefani
kwemizi yini.

KokaBaba umuzi, ayethi akuwona owakhe kodwa okayise, inkosazana yayihlala
enhla nesilili sikanina uma kuyikwabo.

Kodwa uma ingene exhibeni noma elawini yayihlala enhla nesilili sikayise.


Onke-ke amanye amadodakazi ayelamayo ahlale ngenzansi kwayo.

Wayehlala lapho-ke uNonkonzo kaMcanjana, izibulo lakwabo kaBaba. 

Uma sebehlangene izindlu zombili zasodibini, ngenzansi kwakhe kwakuhlala
izibulo lakwethu kwakhulu uMaGwala, uNonsuze.

Umona ngumhobholo. 

Kubuye kuthiwe futhi ngumgolo noma umhawu.

Kuyashiwo futhi ukuthi ngumgababa. 

Lokhu-ke kusho ukuhawukela noma ukufisa into okungeyona eyakho ukuba ibe
ngeyakho.

Bambalwa abantu abangenawo umona, uma bekhona. 

Ubungako bomgababa kulabo abanawo kuyedlulana. 

Nezilwane zinawo umhobholo.

Mhlawumbe uma usuhlaziya kahle izinhlobo zomona, uzibeka ngononina,
kungavela ukuthi ukufisa into okungeyona yamuntu, uma ngabe ikhona into enjalo,
nokufisa ukuba nento efana neyomunye umuntu, akuwona umona.

Phela awufisi yona into enomnikaziyo.

Futhi ufisa into efanayo neyomunye, kodwa hhayi yona.

Wena uzifisela ukuba neyakho into, kodwa efanayo neyalona onefana nofisa
ukuba nayo.

Kuhle umuntu athi uma esefisile, bese ezizamela yena ngokwakhe ukuzitholela
eyakhe into njengokwesifiso sakhe, nangangokwesifiso leso sakhe.

Kuhle ukuba umuntu azenzele lokho afisa ukuba yikho.

Kwenye inkathi umuntu uke azondelwe ukuba nguyena, njengokubunjwa kwakhe

nithi nibuya lapho BESE niyovunula seniza ebandla, lapho kobe
sekubuthene abantu abazobikelwa ngenkatha.

ABESE qhubeka masinyane ethi.

Waqhweba uZwangedwa, induna yakhe enkulu EYABIPHETHE yonke imikhosi
yakhe.

Kwase kuzobakhona nesiqiniseko sokuthi umuntu uzoziphuzela
ngenkululeko, angathi ephethe ingilazi yotshwala ngapha, EBE ejeqeza,
elindele ukudonsa ivolovolo ngokuphazima kweso. 

USiphepho lowo KWABE kungumnumzane ovelele endaweni yaseMaBheleni.


LIBE-KE selihlehliswelwa olunye usuku icala, kunqunywe nemali
engaba yisibambiso sokukhululwa kwakhe okwaleso sikhashana ibheyili.

Phela LABESELIKHALA igazi likaShaka, selibuzwa kuye.

Wayezizwa kahle umfokaKhumalo ukuthi kuyoyonke le misebenzi
ababhekene nayo, nguyena OWABE ezokwenza umsebenzi osemqoka kunabo
bonke. 

Sekuzwakala nezigqi zokuphefumula kubantu: umoya lona ungasathi
nyaka, nezinyoni imbala EZABE zixokozela, zathula, kwasengathi
zitsheliwe ukuthi nansi indaba embi.

Washo ngokunengwa uNobuhle ngoba unina WABE embuza into esobala.

YABE inenhliziyo elukhuni njengetshe; ingesabi lutho' umzimba wayo
umuhle ubunjwe kahle kakhulu, uthandeka; amehlo ayo lawa ekhanya
inhlansi, elokoza umlilo - lapho esethukuthele ayeba bomvu sengathi
agcwele igazi.

Bala washesha ukukwamukela loko abe ekufundiswa, into eyakhombisa
uMaqhuzu ukuthi WABE ezimisele kangakanani ukufa lapho efa khona.


Kwasalapha NGABE ngifika nehwanqa noma nentshebe noma nempandla.

Ukukhalipha komqondo wakhe nxa kubuthene amadoda, kwakumeleka
ngesithunzi esimphumela waso KWABE kuwukuhlonishwa ngisho nayiyo inkosi
imbala. 

Lesi simo SABE sesimvula amehlo uMaqhuzu, wazibona kahle ukuthi
ukuhlakanipha kwakhe kuphelela obala uma kungenasisekelo
esiyisitifiketi. 

Komkhulu, emzini wenkosi yesigodi, WABE aziwa njengendoda okuyoba
lukhuni ukuluphetha udaba uma ingekho esigcawini. 

Yathi ukuba ingene esigodlweni sikaDingane, yangena maqede washaywa
uvalo uDingane, kwazise ukuthi YABE inesithunzi esesabekayo kakhulu.

WABE eseyicabangisisa wadepha indaba yokuziqhuba izifundo zakhe
ngembawula, okungenani abekeke ebangeni leshumi. 

Kuthe lapho besikhipha isidumbu sakhe emanzini, kwahlaluka ukuthi
okaSenzangakhona WABEFINYELE umsipha, wambamba ngamandla esemanzini
ajulile, kazathola nathuba lokuphefumula.

Bala kwaba wukuqeda inkomishi yetiye ababemenzele yona ukwehlisa
izintuli zendlela, WABE esebamba ebheke eMnsinsini emaphoyiseni. 

Sizoke siyizwe lento enkulu eyasusa uthuli olungako ezweni
lakwaZulu, yaphemba umlilo omkhulu ongacimiyo kuze KUBE namuhla usazinge
ulokoza.

Ngase KUBE ukhuluma indaba yokuthi uyashada nje kanti ukhuluma indaba
yalowa ntanga yethu owayefuna ukungihlaba ngesibhakela emgwaqweni kubukela
abantu?
 
"Kulungile, ngomuso kusasa nizoqonda emfuleni, njengemihla yonke,
nithi nibuya lapho bese niyovunula seniza ebandla, lapho KOBE
sekubuthene abantu abazobikelwa ngenkatha.

Wamane wasola uSteve ukuthi le ndaba KUYOBE iyogcina kude uma ihamba
kanje. 

Uma NGABE ukhuluma indaba yokuthi uyashada nje uqonde ukuthi ushada
nalesiya salukazi engisaziyo, ngiyaxolisa ndodana, a-ngi-zi. 

Bala washesha ukuwamukela loko ABE ekufundiswa, into eyakhombisa
uMaqhuzu ukuthi wabe ezimisele kangakanani ukufa lapho efa khona.


Wakubona kuwumsebenzi wakhe oKaMemela ukuthi kubekhona akushoyo,
yize KWABE kungeke kwawuphendula umbuzo kaSiphepho. 

Njengoba wayesehambe bonke ubusuku, kwenye indawo ehamba
ngokugijima, wazumeka waze wavuka emini enkulu, KWABE nokulamba
sekuthe ngilapha. 

Ukuba akangifanele NGABE angizange ngizihluphe nokuzihlupha
ngokumthatha. 

"Ngakho-ke ngomuso kusasa," kuqhuba uMkabayi "nizothi lapho nibuya

Kwaba yimithonselana nje engemingaki eyathi ukuhambahamba emgxaleni

Nokho WABUYE wafekela lowo mqondo, wabona ukuthi kuyobe uyasehlisa
isithunzi sakhe, nokuhlonishwa kwakhe, nokwaziwa kwakhe njengomuntu
ongasohlangothini lomthetho. 

Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,

WAWUNGABUYI ulambatha owakhe umkhondo.

Kuzothi-ke lapho inyanga ithathe yonke lemibengo IYIXUBE ndawonye

Uthi USELIHAMBE kakhulu naleli lakwaZulu kodwa akazange ayibone

WALIQALA futhi iculo umbhidi wathi aliculwe neminwe isemilonyeni.

uMaqhuzu ukuthi wabe ezimisele kangakanani ukufa lapho efa khona.


Ukuphuthuma lokhu kwenziwa ukuba babegcina ukuthi yinhloli,
uthunywe kwaZulu ukuba azohlola kulandele impi ngoba ukulanda 
kwakhe ezweni labo AKUBAHLABANGA umxhwele. 

ENgilandi KABASIVUMANGA isenzo somnumzane omkhulu uSir Benjamin
=D'Urban= sokudla izwe labantu.

ONGALIPHETHE lolo qwenjana wayeyogcina esangweni, akukhathalekile
ukuthi waziwa kangakanani nokuthi wejwayele kangakanani ukuzophuza
kwaMaqhuzu. 

Washo ngokunengwa uNobuhle ngoba unina wabe EMBUZA into esobala.

WAYELIVUMA elokuthi bangcono kunaye ngoba banezitifiketi ezingcono
kunaloko ayebambelele kukona, kodwa-ke yize kunjalo, umuntu akahlali
ephethe isitifiketi ngesandla. 

Ngesizathu sokuthi WAYEBAHLONIPHA abathengi bakhe uMaqhuzu, wabona
kunesidingo sokubachazela ukuthi sivezwe yini isidingo sokuba bashiye
okusazikhali abakuphethe endlini ethize eduze kwesango, nokuthi kufanele
ngani kusungulwe ikilabhu yabaphuzi, okuyothi labo abafisa ukuba
ngamalunga ayo baphathe izingqwenjana ezifakazela ukuthi bangobani,
ezinezithombe zabo, ukuze bemukeleke. 

WAYENGAWAZI amandla kaNobuhle uMaqhuzu, ngaleso sizathu wamfundisa
amasu nezindlela zokusetshenziswa kwesibhamu, enzela ukuthi uma
imqhamukela kabi eyabafo, akwazi ukwelekelela uNobuhle. 

Nxa bengingumuntu okhululekileyo BENGIZOLIHAMBA lelilizwe elibanzi
ngiye ngiyibone. 

Kufanele AKWAZI loku, senzele ukuthi noma ngabe kwenzekani
kuNobuhle, noma ngabe kwenzekani lapha ekhaya, angasisoli ukuthi
sasingamtsheli ngani. 

Kanti ixoxwa nje lendaba uJeqe usengenwe yisifiso esikhulu
sengathi angake AYIBONE lentombi eseyehlule amadoda nenhle kangaka.

Inyanga izolwephula iluthele imithi, ILUQOBE amaqashana
iluhlanganise nenyama. 

Mhla kuzokusa kube umkhosi iNkosi iyophuma lapho endlini kuvalwe,
iholwe inyanga iphethe ukhamba lwentelezi, IYIFAFAZE intelezi baye
bafike emfuleni, uJeqe elandela iNkosi ephethe eminye imithi okuzofikwa
emfuleni phakathi kobusuku yelapha. 

Sekukhona izinkunzi ezimbili ezimnyama ezicijileyo, ezihlabayo,
ezingazange ZIYIZEKE insikazi, ezanela ukwephusa zakhethwa eziyobanjwa
amabutho ngezandla bazidonye ngesibhakele zize zife. 

Sizoke SIYIZWE lento enkulu eyasusa uthuli olungako ezweni
lakwaZulu, yaphemba umlilo omkhulu ongacimiyo kuze kube namuhla usazinge
ulokoza.

Lingena nje sebeke bahlangana abazali bezigebengu, bavumelana
ngokuthi kungeze kwaba yinto enhle uma bethatha ummeli ngoba loko
kuyobonakala sengathi kuyindlela abavuna ngayo izingane zabo, nabazama
ngayo ukuba izingane zabo ZINGASITHOLI isijezo esifanele isenzo sazo.


Akuvamile ukuba ummangalelwa abuzwe ukuthi uyalivuma yini noma
UYALIPHIKA icala abekwe lona. 

"Qha; NGIYAMBONA umfokazana lowo," kuphendula uMkabayi.

Nempela BAMTHOLA umuntu ongumngani kaJeqe. 

Loku kuhleka kwakhe kwamdida uMaqhuzu, akangaba nalwazi noma uhleka
nje UMBONA ubuphukuphuku yini noma kuyisima kanjani. 

Ayi UYASIBULALA uShaka. 

Kuya ngoba uhlala lapha koMkhulu, AWUZIZWA izindaba ezikhulunywa
ngabantu ezifundeni lapha. 

Ukhuluma nje lomfo uShaka uyamphikisa uthi: "AWUKALIHAMBI leli
lakithi ubone izintombi ezinhle. 

Uthi bangaphezu kwesikhombisa abantu abahlukene ebezwa BEYIKHULUMA
le ndaba. 

Abone uMkabayi ukuthi uma ENGAYIQEDI lendaba zingahle zidumelane
khona lapho izinsizwa zomfowabo uSenzangakhona.

Namabutho ayesezikhalela ethi: Size siqhakaze izimvu singaganiwe,
SINGABAZI ubumnandi bokuhlala emakhaya, kube yilokhu sihamba
ezintabeni, silale endle, sifa yindlala! 

Komkhulu, emzini wenkosi yesigodi, wabe aziwa njengendoda okuyoba
lukhuni UKULUPHETHA udaba uma ingekho esigcawini. 

"Ngoba nike naxoxa naye uButhelezi, kuhle uphindele umncenge uthi
uDingane UYOKUHLANZA bonke ubumnyama bensila kaShaka akwakhele umuzi
omkhulu emva kokuba usugezwe ngentelezi, futhi mhla efayo uShaka
uyokulondoloza ungambelwa naye." 

Zazimthatha izinsizwa ZIYA komlahla umfazi kwangaba ndaba zalutho.


Esabasebenza ngemvubu abafana `umbhidi' kwangena othisha,
abanumzane uNgubane noNgobeni bevela lapho babehlala khona lapho babekade
BESAYOKUDLA ukudla kwasemini. 

YAWAKHIPHA seyiyophuma ngomnyanmgo amagama okugcina into yakwabo. 

Bathe lapho beziphonsa phakathi esizibeni oNdongeni noSiphepho
noZidumo BAMFICA esephangalele okaSenzangakhona.

Naso-ke isizathu sokuqala esabangela amaBhunu SIWABONE esephungwa
ngezithebe kwaZulu, ekhumbuza uDingane izinkonjane ezabikwa nguShaka
mhla efayo.

Lokhu iNkosi bayigwaze ntambama, WAYITHABATHA esizwa abesifazane,
wayifaka endlini nezinye izinceku zayo, wayigoqonga, wayembathisa
ngengubo yayo. 

Athi angalithola ithuba aye exhibeni lalo, limzekele okuningi
nga lentombi, waze wacishe WAYAZI engezange ayibone. 

Wathulisa wabuka, WAMBONA emi ethe ne ngomhlane othangweni. 

WABATAXA, wabataxa ethi bayabhimba. 

Onke amehlo abantu anamathela kuDingane, BAMBONA ubuso bakhe
sebumanzi izinyembezi, ziwohloka emehlweni.

WAKUBONA kuwumsebenzi wakhe oKaMemela ukuthi kubekhona akushoyo,
yize kwabe kungeke kwawuphendula umbuzo kaSiphepho. 

ASIMUZWA esithandazela. 

ZAZIMTHATHA izinsizwa ziya komlahla umfazi kwangaba ndaba zalutho.


Wazelula, waphuma esihlahleni, wahamba eqonda ezinkomeni
AYEZIBONA, ziklabile, ziyibanga. 

Izwe ladliwa kumaXhoza, kwamiswa iziMantshi, ukuba ZILIBUSE,
selahlukanisiwe.

Kuthe lapha kuthi hwaqa, wabanga emasimini, lokhu UWAFICA
ekhihliza, nemfe isiyikhiphile iminyani, lokhu ingakavuthwa kahle. 

Uthi bangaphezu kwesikhombisa abantu abahlukene EBEZWA beyikhuluma
le ndaba. 

Kwaphela isonto uJeqe neNkosi nenyanga befumbeleke kuleyondlu,
ibaphethe inyanga IBAGCABA, iphalazisa iNkosi ngezintelezi ezinkulu,
ezimhlophe nezimnyama. 

Lokhu iNkosi BAYIGWAZE ntambama, wayithabatha esizwa abesifazane,
wayifaka endlini nezinye izinceku zayo, wayigoqonga, wayembathisa
ngengubo yayo. 

Izinkomo sithi sibuya nazo zimboze izintaba nezinkalo, igazi
labaningi bakithi lichithekele ezizweni, singakaphumuli USEYASIBIZA
ukuba siyekohlasela kwezinye izindawo." 

Ngabe UYAMBONA ukuba usebuyile Ma. 

Kwaba uye osondeza amanzi okuyigeza, kwaba yilokhu IMTHUMA ukuba
abheke ukuthi ukudla kwayo kulungiswe kahle na. 

Ngangingazi ukuthi ukuzinikela eNkosini yami KUYAKUNGENZA ngize
ngenze izinto ezinengeka kanje. 

Nawe uma umlalela UYOKUSIZA ukuba uphenduke ukhethe iNkosi. 

Amadoda asondela kuye abuza ukuthi uphumaphi, WAWATSHELA ukuthi
uphuma kwaZulu uze kulelizwe uzofuna imithi yokwelapha ngobawezwa
idumela ngabasuka lapha bethi miningi imithi. 

Ndabezitha, uthe okaNdaba ANGIKUBIKELE ukuthi ungesabi.

Ayilandise kahle, AYITSHELE nokuthi uzwe esesendleleni kuthiwa
uShaka ubulewe umnawakhe uDingane. 

Hamba UMTSHENE ukuthi ngithi kakukho engikwesabayo mina lapha
ezweni.

Kufanele akwazi loku, senzele ukuthi noma ngabe kwenzekani
kuNobuhle, noma ngabe kwenzekani lapha ekhaya, ANGASISOLI ukuthi
sasingamtsheli ngani. 

NGIZOKUTSHENA ukuthi uMhlangana sengimbonele elakhe icebo, kodwa
kusweleke siqaphe ngoba unabalandeli abaningi okungaswelekile babone
ukuthi siqondeni.

Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,
kwabuye kwavunyelwanwa ngokuthi okungenani yena angahluthulela izicabha,
aqinisike ukuthi zihluthulekisisile phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi obucayi wokudidizelisa uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi BEMBAMBA ukuze angaloku eba yisiphazamiso. 

Oyena WAYIQEDAYO owayephethe amabutho amhlophe 

Lokhu iNkosi bayigwaze ntambama, wayithabatha esizwa abesifazane,
wayifaka endlini nezinye izinceku zayo, WAYIGOQONGA, wayembathisa
ngengubo yayo. 

Balala, kuthe ekuseni uJeqe BAMTHATHA bamyisa eNkosini. 

Wathi ungathi shiqe NGAWUGWADLULA. 

Wafula ummbila WAWETSHATHA, wakhohlwa manje ukuthi uzowosa
ngani. 

Cishu sakhohlwa ukulanda ukuthi laphaya oPhongolo lapha uJeqe
wayegula khona, kukhona inja yakuwo lowo muzi eyamejwayela, kuthi
lapho lomfazi owayelethela uJeqe ukudla eya kuJeqe, ihambe naye,
adle nokuncane ayishiyele, yaze yamejwayela, kwathi mhla ehambayo
yamlandela ngomkhondo yaze YAMFICA, yaba seyiba yinja yakhe njalo.


Ofihlayo wayengasho nje ukuthi ungqubuzeke odongeni, noma kambe
athi uvule isivalo budedengu saye SAMSAKAZA, kodwa kwakucace njengezinqe
zeselesele ukuthi yizisihle zesibhakela leziya. 

Wasondela emzini wabona ukuthi kuphekwe emnyango, waququbala
buqamamana nomuzi, baze bephula bangena endlini, wasondela, izinja
zamuzwa, ZAMKHONKOTHA wabuyela emuva, wafuna isu lokuyothatha
isikhuni esivuthayo lapho bekade bepheke khona. 

Wabe uyazikhalela owesifazane; WAMQAQA uJeqe. 

Phela uma ikhona, babethi omakade ebona babasingi, uzibona
ngokubungela kwazo othini; zingqengqe ngalo uma ULUSHUTHEKA esidlekeni
sazo njengomkhuba ezisuke ziwejwayele

Ngadumela umgxala NGAWUSHUTHEKA embhacwini owawuphakathi
kwezinguzunga ezimbili zamatshe ezazilakanyene. 

UNgubane naye WAYISHUTHEKA iminwe njengabo abafundi. 

Munye kuphela owasola sengathi kukhona okukhona phakathi kukaMkabayi
noDingane - uMhlangana: ngoba nalapho bekhuluma esigodlweni sikaMkabayi
uDingane kwaba sengathi ukwazi konke okwasekuqondwe nguMkabayi - nokho
kaze azihlupha kakhulu ngalokho; naye WAYENGAKULINDELE neze lokho
ababekuqondile.

Wayengawazi amandla kaNobuhle uMaqhuzu, ngaleso sizathu wamfundisa
amasu nezindlela zokusetshenziswa kwesibhamu, enzela ukuthi uma
IMQHAMUKELA kabi eyabafo, akwazi ukwelekelela uNobuhle. 

Naphezu lokhu kuhlola abafana bami babeqale ngakho NGANGIKUPHINDELA
ukuzenelisa ukuthi kwakungekho halakasha yini lwenyoka ezazingenise
emgodini walo zihlala nalo izinyosi lezi. 

Sengishilo ngathi okaSithayi uyafa namuhla. NGITHUMELE kuZidumo
ngathi kakhulume naye.

Ngangingazi ukuthi UKUZINIKELA eNkosini yami kuyakungenza ngize
ngenze izinto ezinengeka kanje. 

Ushu ukuthi kufanele ngihambe ngivimbela izinsizwa phandle lapha
ngithi ngicela ZINGESHELE khona ngizoziqoma. 

Kuthe lapho isidumbu BESIKHIPHELA phandle waquleka oweNkosi,"
esho ebheka uDingane.

Nokho wayengakehlelwa yilokhu OKWAMEHLELA ngelinye ilanga,
besesigodlweni esingaphandle lapho kuhlala khona izinceku eziganiweyo.


Cishu sakhohlwa ukulanda ukuthi laphaya oPhongolo lapha uJeqe
wayegula khona, kukhona inja yakuwo lowo muzi eyamejwayela, kuthi
lapho lomfazi owayelethela uJeqe ukudla eya kuJeqe, ihambe naye,
adle nokuncane ayishiyele, yaze yamejwayela, kwathi mhla ehambayo
YAMLANDELA ngomkhondo yaze yamfica, yaba seyiba yinja yakhe njalo.


Wayengazimisele uSteve ukuxabana noMama wakhe ngalelo langa kodwa
le mibuzo AYEMBELESELE ngayo yayiholela engxabanweni. 

Luyavuthwa laphaya uselwa, iNkosi iqale YALUHLABELA ngoba nxa
lungaphathwanga yiyo abakwaZulu bathi aluvuthwa. 

Uma wayeshilo kwakobulawa yena uJequ kuthiwe UMYEKELENI. 

Ngenxa kaShaka mina ngethembekile kuye ngesivumelwano engasenza naye
ukuba NGIMUFELE noma kunjani. 

Bala kwaba wukuqeda inkomishi yetiye ABABEMENZELE yona ukwehlisa
izintuli zendlela, wabe esebamba ebheke eMnsinsini emaphoyiseni. 

Akukabi sikhathi sokuba uye kwagoqanyawo Jeqe kukhulu izwe lakini
OSAZOLENZELA kona kunokuhlabana kwakho uhlabanela uShaka. 

"Ngoba nike naxoxa naye uButhelezi, kuhle uphindele umncenge uthi
uDingane uyokuhlanza bonke ubumnyama bensila kaShaka AKWAKHELE umuzi
omkhulu emva kokuba usugezwe ngentelezi, futhi mhla efayo uShaka
uyokulondoloza ungambelwa naye." 

Athi angalithola ithuba aye exhibeni lalo, LIMZEKELE okuningi
nga lentombi, waze wacishe wayazi engezange ayibone. 

UMaZwane wathi ngokubona ukuthi uzalelwe yinja endlini, wacela
umkhokheli uMaNzuza ukuba AZOMNCENGELA uMdlalose ukuba asihoxise isinqumo
sakhe sokumkhipha enkonzweni. 

Usazobona okukhulu, uzwe okukhulu UNGAKAMLANDELI nawe uShaka.

Ngizokutshena ukuthi uMhlangana SENGIMBONELE elakhe icebo, kodwa
kusweleke siqaphe ngoba unabalandeli abaningi okungaswelekile babone
ukuthi siqondeni.

Ukukhalipha komqondo wakhe nxa kubuthene amadoda, kwakumeleka
ngesithunzi ESIMPHUMELA waso kwabe kuwukuhlonishwa ngisho nayiyo inkosi
mbala. 

Inyanga izolwephula ILUTHELE imithi, iluqobe amaqashana
iluhlanganise nenyama. 

Sonke lesi sikhati efuna umsebenzi, umqondo wakhe umtshela ukuthi
BAYOMCABANGELA labo abayomqasha, bamnike khathisimbe umsebenzi wokubhala
ehhovisi limbe noma-ke bamfake emsebenzini wokwengamela ophikweni
oluthile. 

Uthe ebuyela ezigabeni wafika lesi sithunywa sikaDingane sesihambile,
ethi UZOSIXOXELA lendaba embi nebuhlungu yokuhlinza umuntu wesifazane
ekhulelwe. 

Lelozwi lavuma ukuthi njengoba izigqila lezo bezibasiza abaninizo
ZIBASEBENZELA yonke imisebenzi lena bazobuyiselwa ukulahlekelwa kwabo
izigqila ngohlamvana lwemali.

Bayasho-ke asebake balunguza khona ukuthi AKUSIBHAKELA sidida
ompetha. 

Umfundisi esizwa kuthiwa uDingane WAMVUMELA ukuba ahlale eduze
naye afundise abantu bakhe, kuthiwa nguMfundisi =Owen=Lowo.

Yilapho-ke lapho bamthathelela khona abangane bakhe, BAMBHEBHEZELA
ukuba angabi yisiphukuphuku sensizwa, bamgxisha ngomoya wokuthi kufanele
uPamella azikhombise zonke izidingo zokuthi uyintombi lapha kuMaqhuzu,
hhayi umngane. 

Lokhu ZIKWENZELA ukuba sithi sifinyelela ojwini lwazo sifice itshe
selome inhlama. 

Ngesizathu sokuthi wayebahlonipha abathengi bakhe uMaqhuzu, wabona
kunesidingo SOKUBACHAZELA ukuthi sivezwe yini isidingo sokuba bashiye
okusazikhali abakuphethe endlini ethize eduze kwesango, nokuthi kufanele
ngani kusungulwe ikilabhu yabaphuzi, okuyothi labo abafisa ukuba
ngamalunga ayo baphathe izingqwenjana ezifakazela ukuthi bangobani,
ezinezithombe zabo, ukuze bemukeleke. 

Hhayi indaba YOKUSIBABAZELA ukuthi benithilileka kwasha kwacima.


Kwakusilele kona nje ukuthi zazingekho izincwadi EZAZIMFAKAZELA
ukuthi uhlakaniphe kangakanani. 

Sonke lesi sikhati efuna umsebenzi, umqondo wakhe UMTSHELA ukuthi
bayomcabangela labo abayomqasha, bamnike khathisimbe umsebenzi wokubhala
ehhovisi limbe noma-ke bamfake emsebenzini wokwengamela ophikweni
oluthile. 

Cishu sakhohlwa ukulanda ukuthi laphaya oPhongolo lapha uJeqe
wayegula khona, kukhona inja yakuwo lowo muzi EYAMEJWAYELA, kuthi
lapho lomfazi owayelethela uJeqe ukudla eya kuJeqe, ihambe naye,
adle nokuncane ayishiyele, yaze yamejwayela, kwathi mhla ehambayo
yamlandela ngomkhondo yaze yamfica, yaba seyiba yinja yakhe njalo.


Cishu sakhohlwa ukulanda ukuthi laphaya oPhongolo lapha uJeqe
wayegula khona, kukhona inja yakuwo lowo muzi eyamejwayela, kuthi
lapho lomfazi owayelethela uJeqe ukudla eya kuJeqe, ihambe naye,
adle nokuncane ayishiyele, yaze YAMEJWAYELA, kwathi mhla ehambayo
yamlandela ngomkhondo yaze yamfica, yaba seyiba yinja yakhe njalo.


Yilapho-ke lapho BAMTHATHELELA khona abangane bakhe, bambhebhezela
ukuba angabi yisiphukuphuku sensizwa, bamgxisha ngomoya wokuthi kufanele
uPamella azikhombise zonke izidingo zokuthi uyintombi lapha kuMaqhuzu,
hhayi umngane. 

'SINGAMLEKELELA nathi basizikazi abanye uma esebambeke kanjalo
okhuleni ukunokuba aze ayeke umsebenzi weNkosi ongaka', kuncenga
uMaNzuza'. 

UBAXOXELA ngentombi enhle yakubo athi seyehlula namakhosi akhona.


Wazi ngani noma lo muntu othi uyamthatha UKULUNGELE. 

Phela uma ikhona, babethi omakade ebona babasingi, uzibona
ngokubungela kwazo othini; zingqengqe ngalo uma ulushutheka esidlekeni
sazo njengomkhuba ezisuke ZIWEJWAYELE. 

Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi OWAWUNGAMLUNGELA, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,
kwabuye kwavunyelwanwa ngokuthi okungenani yena angahluthulela izicabha,
aqinisike ukuthi zihluthulekisisile phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi obucayi wokudidizelisa uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi bembamba ukuze angaloku eba yisiphazamiso. 

Cishu sakhohlwa ukulanda ukuthi laphaya oPhongolo lapha uJeqe
wayegula khona, kukhona inja yakuwo lowo muzi eyamejwayela, kuthi
lapho lomfazi owayelethela uJeqe ukudla eya kuJeqe, ihambe naye,
adle nokuncane AYISHIYELE, yaze yamejwayela, kwathi mhla ehambayo
yamlandela ngomkhondo yaze yamfica, yaba seyiba yinja yakhe njalo.


Wathi ubazondiswa ulunya nesihluku abaxhaphaza ngaso abantu bakubo
uma BEBASEBENZELA. 

Asimuzwa ESITHANDAZELA. 

"Ngoba nike naxoxa naye uButhelezi, kuhle uphindele umncenge uthi
uDingane uyokuhlanza bonke ubumnyama bensila kaShaka akwakhele umuzi
omkhulu emva kokuba usugezwe ngentelezi, futhi mhla efayo uShaka
uyokulondoloza ungambelwa NAYE." 

Ngenxa yokwazi ukuthi kuhlwa ngomnyama njengoba inyanga yayifile,
ngangena mina emgodini owawusumbiwe abafana bami BEWUQALELWE amachalaha
ami. 

INkosi ithi: "Akukho lutho kulo muntu, MTHATHENI nimyise emzini
kNdlovu ambhekisise ukwenza kwakhe nokuhamba kwakhe. 

Kwaba uye osondeza amanzi OKUYIGEZA, kwaba yilokhu imthuma ukuba
abheke ukuthi ukudla kwayo kulungiswe kahle na. 

Ukuba akangifanele ngabe angizange ngizihluphe nokuzihlupha
NGOKUMTHATHA. 

Sekukhona imvunge enkulu phakathi kwabantu, kodwa engayazi ngoba
besaba UKUMTSHELA. 

UMaZwane ngizoke ngithi UKUMYEKA-KE aqhubeke nokusonta. 

USika-ke yena njengomnikazi wesithuthi, owakhe umsebenzi kwakuzoba
WUKUYINYATELA ayinyathelisise, ingayi ngasesiteshini eMthwalume, ngoba
leyo ndlela idlula emaphoyiseni aseMnsinsini, kodwa ayikhwabule ibheke
ngaseMzumbe =Home=. 

Ngwane elihle, yizithunywa zikaSathane lezi, zihlonza kona ukuthi
zithunywe UKUZOSILINGA. 

AYILANDISE kahle, ayitshele nokuthi uzwe esesendleleni kuthiwa
uShaka ubulewe umnawakhe uDingane. 

Wathi UBAFUNDISA ukukhamisa ngoba wayesethole kahle ukuthi
bayabhimba. 

Kwathi esanda kufika nje uJeqe esigodlweni iNkosi YAMSONDEZA kuyo.


Ithe lapho ISILIVEZA obala ezindlebeni zikaDingane lelocebo
lokugudluza uMhlangana noMbopha endleleni, uDingane wezwa eshaywa uvalo
olukhulu.

Balala, kuthe ekuseni uJeqe bamthatha BAMYISA eNkosini. 

Izinhliziyo zabantu sezinamathele kuDingane ezethemba ukuthi izwe
uzo-ke ALIPHUMUZE empini. 

INkosi ithi: "Akukho lutho kulo muntu, mthatheni NIMYISE emzini
kaNdlovu ambhekisise ukwenza kwakhe nokuhamba kwakhe. 

Ngaphezu kokudideka kwakukhona novalo lokuthi loku kuhamba
isikhathi eside kangaka, KWAKUZOMXABANISA noyise, uSiphepho, uPamella.


Inyanga izolwephula iluthele imithi, iluqobe amaqashana
ILUHLANGANISE nenyama. 

Lokhu iNkosi bayigwaze ntambama, wayithabatha esizwa abesifazane,

ngengubo yayo.

Bathi dedelele lapho bezwa ukuthi akukho sigigaba esibabazekayo
ABALANDISA ngaso uMaqhuzu. 

Naye futhi WAYEYAZISA sengathi umuntu. 

"NGIYAKUQINISA, ngoba usazobhekana nokukhulu okwedlula lokhu.

UDingane UYALUZISA izwe nje lapha eNatali nakwaZulu, nakhona lena

amasu nezindlela zokusetshenziswa kwesibhamu, enzela ukuthi uma

Lathi liqambe liba sokhakhayini, base bebuyile UKUYOYIGCWALISA

ngokuhamba.

Nokho wabuye wafekela lowo mqondo, wabona ukuthi kuyobe UYASEHLISA
isithunzi sakhe, nokuhlonishwa kwakhe, nokwaziwa kwakhe njengomuntu
ongasohlangothini lomthetho. 

Wawungafunga ukuthi ubekhona kuntshontshwa izimbuzi zomnumzane
mumbe, ngoba kwakhuthi lapho amaphoyisa ecela ukuba AWACEBISE ukuthi
ngase kube lowo monakalo wenziwe ngubani, amane ashaye emhloleni, bala

Zazingashwabene izingubo wawungafunga ukuthi bezihlafunwe yinkomo
qede YAZIPHIMISA. 

Komunye umhlangano wabo baveza icebo lokuba bathume umuntu
njengesikhonzi ayothola uJeqe ukuba naye abe ngakubona, ABADLISELE
uShaka ngobuthi ekudleni kwakhe. 

Mayelana nokuthi ungena kanjani ngaphakathi wathi ziningi
izindlela namasu okuvula izicabha namafasitela njengoba labo asuke
ezobabulala uqala NGOKUBASHUNQISELA udosi lwempisi. 

Wathi UKULEHLISA u`Thakathi.' 

Loko kwakufakazelwa yizisihle ezazibonakala lapha phansi kwamehlo abo

"Lalela-ke, Dingane. Indaba kaMbopha kaSithayi SENGIYILUNGISILE.

Naye kuyamkhanyela ukuthi izwe uliphethe kabi, kodwa wethembekile

UNGIFANELE Ma. Ngineqiniso laloko.

INTABAZWE lena - =Harrismith= - yaqanjwa ngaye, kuhlonishwa yena.

Lathi liqambe liba sokhakhayini, base bebuyile ukuyoyigcwalisa

Wayengawazi amandla kaNobuhle uMaqhuzu, ngaleso sizathu WAMFUNDISA
amasu nezindlela zokusetshenziswa kwesibhamu, enzela ukuthi uma
