bonke.
 
Sibona ukuphuma nje kwezimali zami ngendlela ENGEMTHETHO ziyothelwa
laphaya eSontweni. 

SEKUKHONA izinkunzi ezimbili ezimnyama ezicijileyo, ezihlabayo,
ezingazange ziyizeke insikazi, ezanela ukwephusa zakhethwa eziyobanjwa
amabutho ngezandla bazidonye ngesibhakele zize zife. 

Ibutho ELIYINTANGA yeNkosi lifake umnyakanya wesakabuli, kube
yilelo libe nento eliyenzileyo elehluke ngayo, noma okulenga esiphundu,
noma umqhele nje wombhijo wotshani obuthile. 

Abanye babethi uzogwetshwa iminyaka ENGAMASHUMI amabili.

Lesi simo sabe sesimvula amehlo uMaqhuzu, wazibona kahle ukuthi
ukuhlakanipha kwakhe kuphelela obala uma kungenasesekelo
ESIYISITIFIKETI. 

Nempela bamthola umuntu ONGUMNGANI kaJeqe. 

Kuthe kuntambama kwakufika izinsizwa EZIYISIHLANU ziphuma eNkosini
ithi azilande uJeqe aye kuyo. 

Ngelinye ilanga kwasuka esikhulu isidumo esigodlweni kuthukana
izintombi ezimbili EZINGUMDLUNKULU kaShaka zixabene. 


Kwathi ukuba sisuke isidumo leso uMfundisi =Owen= wabopha
OKUNGOKWAKHE wabamba indlela eqonde eThekwini, lapho wafika khona
wadlulela phesheya eNgilande.

Lokho kwabaphatha kabi kakhulu abeLungu balelizwe, ikakhulu
amaBhunu, OKUYIWONA ayemaningi impela lapho.

Ayisebenzi indaba yokuthi ukuba BENGINGUWE. 

Phela uma ikhona, babethi omakade EBONA babasingi, uzibona
ngokubungela kwazo othini; zingqengqe ngalo uma ulushutheka esidlekeni
sazo njengomkhuba ezisuke ziwejwayele. 

Cishu sakhohlwa ukulanda ukuthi laphaya oPhongolo lapha uJeqe
wayegula khona, kukhona inja yakuwo lowo muzi eyamejwayela, kuthi
lapho lomfazi owayelethela uJeqe ukudla eya kuJeqe, ihambe naye,
adle nokuncane ayishiyele, yaze yamejwayela, kwathi mhla ehambayo
yamlandela ngomkhondo yaze yamfica, yaba SEYIBA yinja yakhe njalo.


Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,
kwabuye kwavunyelwanwa ngokuthi okungenani yena angahluthulela izicabha,
aqinisike ukuthi zihluthulekisisile phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi obucayi wokudidizelisa uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi bembamba ukuze angaloku EBA yisiphazamiso. 

Ilokhu ethunywa uJeqe nje ukuba abulale abantu, iNkosi ifuna
ukususa isihawu kuye abenjengayo ngesibindi sokubulala njengoba
EYINSILA yayo nje. 

Wazelula, waphuma esihlahleni, wahamba eqonda ezinkomeni
ayezibona, ziklabile, ZIYIBANGA. 

Manje-ke zase ZIMATASATASA zigonxana noju. 

Phela kwase kubusa iNkosikazi elungileyo phesheya ngalesikathi,
igama layo LINGUNKOSIKAZI =Victoria=.

Esewelele kwelama Thonga yahlonga imizi eduze nomfula, wahamba
waze wadundubala phezu kwesihlambo somfula kwaba YIKHONA ebona imizi,
ezwa izinkomo zikhonya. 

Abanye babethi IYOBA ngamashumi amathathu. 

MUNYE kuphela owasola sengathi kukhona okukhona phakathi kukaMkabayi
noDingane - uMhlangana:ngoba nalapho bekhuluma esigodlweni sikaMkabayi
uDingane kwaba sengathi u kwazi konke okwasekuqondwe nguMkabayi - nokho
kaze azihlupha kakhulu ngalokho; naye wayengakulindele neze lokho
ababekuqondile.

"Angazi, noma KUBUHLUNGU kangaka ukubona abantu imihla namalanga
becekelwa phansi lapha ekhaya nangemikhonto yezizwe." 

Kwakungalula kabi ukuba uma itshe ulinyathele kabi, bheka! 

Onke amehlo abantu anamathela kuDingane, bambona ubuso bakhe
SEBUMANZI zinyembezi, ziwohloka emehlweni.

Nababengahlakaniphile ngaphezu kwakhe babenamathuba ANGCONO kunaye
uma benazo izitifiketi ezikhomba ukuthi bafunda bagcina emabangeni
angaphezu kwalelo yena agcina kulo. 

Kwafika umqondo othi ake nisuke lapha nihambe, mhlawumbe ningase
nithole enye ingosi ENGCONO kunalena lapho ningahlala khona nabantwana
benu ngokuthula nangoxolo, nisuke eduze namaNgisi.

Phezu kwakho konke lokhu OSEKULUTHUTHUVA phakathi kukaZulu abanye
babengavumelani. 

Yabe inenhliziyo elukhuni njengetshe; ingesabi lutho' umzimba wayo
umuhle ubunjwe kahle kakhulu, uthandeka; amehlo ayo lawa ekhanya
inhlansi, elokoza umlilo - lapho esethukuthele AYEBA bomvu sengathi
agcwele igazi.

Yabe inenhliziyo ELUKHUNI njengetshe; ingesabi lutho' umzimba wayo
umuhle ubunjwe kahle kakhulu, uthandeka; amehlo ayo lawa ekhanya
inhlansi, elokoza umlilo - lapho esethukuthele ayeba bomvu sengathi
agcwele igazi.

Asukume ESEMANZI ubuso njalo uDingane.

Nxa umuntu ebuka ubona SEKUMNYAMA izinkalo abantu. 

KUMNANDI abantu behlezi emakhaya izwi lithule. 

Wayelivuma elokuthi BANGCONO kunaye ngoba banezitifiketi ezingcono
kunaloko ayebambelele kukona, kodwa-ke yize kunjalo, umuntu akahlali
ephethe isitifiketi ngesandla. 

Wayelivuma elokuthi bangcono kunaye ngoba banezitifiketi EZINGCONO
kunaloko ayebambelele kukona, kodwa-ke yize kunjalo, umuntu akahlali
ephethe isitifiketi ngesandla. 

Wayeloku ebabaze nje UKUBA mnandi kokuhambisana negugu lakhe, aze
alikhiphe ngisho ukulikhipha elokuthi ubengakaqonywa sonke lesi sikhathi,
ubesadlala nje. 

Ngenxa kaShaka mina ngethembekile kuye ngesivumelwano engasenza naye
ukuba ngimufele noma KUNJANI. 

"Kuthe KUNJALO wavuka esihlwathini oweNkosi, wavuka ekhala
izinyembezi, wathi mabamfihle khona lapho okayise.

Besesukuma uMkabayi ephonsa elakhe KUSENJALO abantu besadabukile,
enzela ukuze bayaqala bayacabanga useliphonsile.

Ngesizathu sokuthi wayebahlonipha abathengi bakhe uMaqhuzu, wabona
kunesidingo sokubachazela ukuthi sivezwe yini isidingo sokuba bashiye
okusazikhali abakuphethe endlini ETHIZE eduze kwesango, nokuthi kufanele
ngani kusungulwe ikilabhu yabaphuzi, okuyothi labo abafisa ukuba
ngamalunga ayo baphathe izingqwenjana ezifakazela ukuthi bangobani,
ezinezithombe zabo, ukuze bemukeleke. 

Nxa bengingumuntu okhululekileyo bengizolihamba lelilizwe ELIBANZI
ngiye ngiyibone. 

ISIMNYAMA manje iNkosi ihlikihlwa, inindwa ngemithi, ayisabonakali
isimo sayo. 

Kwathi ashone phansi uJeqe, pho, uzothini sekukhulume izulu
ELIPHEZULU. 

Sizoke siyizwe lento enkulu eyasusa uthuli OLUNGAKO ezweni
lakwaZulu, yaphemba umlilo omkhulu ongacimiyo kuze kube namuhla usazinge
ulokoza.

Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,
kwabuye kwavunyelwanwa ngokuthi okungenani yena angahluthulela izicabha,
aqinisike ukuthi zihluthulekisisile phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi OBUCAYI wokudidizelisa uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi bembamba ukuze angaloku eba yisiphazamiso. 

Izinduna lapho sezijuluke ZIMANZI zishaya, ziqoqa, eputshuka
ngalapha nangalapha. 

Owokuqala umqondo wakhe UKUBA afe neNkosi yakhe njengoba nasempini
wayelungele ukufa. 

LeNkosikazi yasemaNgisini yayinenhliziyo emhlophe impela, ithanda
izinto ezilungileyo zodwa, ibusa ngesandla esilungileyo, esinozwela,
esikhuthazayo kuzo zonke izinhlangothi zezizwe ezingaphansi kwentende
yombuso wayo; kakhulu ezizweni ezimnyama, nezibuthakathaka, yayifike
igcizelele ekuthini bonke abaziphetheyo - isho oHulumeni phela
ababengaphansi koMbuso waseNgilandi - mabazikhuthaze ekuhlaleni kwazo,
bazivulele izintuba zokuzakha, nazo ZIBENGABANTU abazihloniphayo
nabazethembayo, ingafuni nempela ukuba kube khona umahluko ekubusweni
kwabantu, kuthiwe laba banje ngakho kufanele baphathwe kanje.

`Singamlekelela nathi basizikazi abanye uma ESEBAMBEKE kanjalo
okhuleni ukunokuba aze ayeke umsebenzi weNkosi ongaka', kuncenga
uMaNzuza'. 

Umbiko lowo waye watholwa nangabangane bakhe imbala, bathi yize
noma BABEXAKEKE kangakaya ezindaweni ezahlukene lapho babesebenza
khona, babengeke behluleka ukuza esifweni sikayise womngane wabo. 

Futhi nje APHATHEKA kabi, ngoba leli lephucwa kuwo yiwo namaNgisi
lawo.

Abese QHUBEKA masinyane ethi.

Umuntu uya athi fuqaqa phansi noma yini abeyenza, akukhathalekile
ukuthi BEYIBALULEKE kangakanani, aphuthume lapho kuvele khona isidumo.


Uma kuvuma wayezozabalaza AQHUBEKE njalo aye ayogasela izifundo
zaseNyuvesi. 

Yathi ukuba ingene esigodlweni sikaDingane, yangena maqede washaywa
uvalo uDingane, kwazise ukuthi yabe inesithunzi ESESABEKAYO kakhulu.

Emuva kwesikhashana washaya insimbi umfo kaShabalala izingane zonke
eziculayo zabuthana ehholo ZISAQHUBEKA nokumpongoloza zicula. 

Umbiko lowo waye watholwa nangabangane bakhe imbala, bathi yize
noma babexakeke kangakaya ezindaweni ezahlukene lapho babesebenza
khona, babengeke BEHLULEKA ukuza esifweni sikayise womngane wabo. 

BESEPHONSEKILE eduze kwawo uMkabayi, evutha ulaka.

Kwaphela isonto uJeqe neNkosi nenyanga BEVUMBELEKE kuleyondlu,
ibaphethe inyanga ibagcaba, iphalazisa iNkosi ngezintelezi ezinkulu,
ezimhlophe nezimnyama. 

Ofihlayo wayengasho nje ukuthi UNGQUBUZEKE odongeni, noma kambe
athi uvule isivalo budedengu saye samsakaza, kodwa kwakucace njengezinqe
zeselesele ukuthi yizisihle zesibhakela leziya. 

Naye kuyamkhanyela ukuthi izwe uliphethe kabi, kodwa WETHEMBEKILE
eNkosini yakhe akanakuze ayilimaze. 

Wabe eseyicabangisisa wadepha indaba yokuziqhuba izifundo zakhe
ngembawula, okungenani ABEKEKE ebangeni leshumi. 

Bathe lapho BEKHULEKA kuMkabayi amehlo abantu ayenamathele kubo
nezindlebe zivulekile, zilinde ukucosha abazokusho.

Ngenxa kaShaka mina NGETHEMBEKILE kuye ngesivumelwano engasenza naye
ukuba ngimufele noma kunjani. 

Wagcina eyinike uNgubane ikwaya wathi AKAQHUBEKE yena nayo. 

UMaZwane ngizoke ngithi ukumyeka-ke AQHUBEKE nokusonta. 

Ukukhalipha komqondo wakhe nxa kubuthene amadoda, KWAKUMELEKA
ngesithunzi esimphumela waso kwabe kuwukuhlonishwa ngisho nayiyo inkosi
mbala. 

Wayedinwa agqunqe nasebusweni uma ecabanga ukuthi phakathi kwabantu
abaziyo abafunda emaNyuvesi, kukhona ABEHLULEKA ngokungazenzisi
ukuhlonza ukuthi bayizifundiswa kangakanani. 

Kufanele akwazi loku, senzele ukuthi noma ngabe Kwenzekani
kuNobuhle, noma ngabe KWENZEKANI lapha ekhaya, angasisoli ukuthi
sasingamtsheli ngani. 

Kufanele akwazi loku, senzele ukuthi noma ngabe KWENZEKANI
kuNobuhle, noma ngabe kwenzekani lapha ekhaya, angasisoli ukuthi
sasingamtsheli ngani. 

Ukuba uMaqhuzu wayenazo ezinye izindlela zokuziphilisa, neziletha
imali ngamawala njengomsebenzi wokudayisa utshwala, wayezothatha zona,
ABUYEKE utshwala ngoba babusondeza abantu abaningi eduze kwakhe, into
eyayingenza ukuthi nesitha esiqonde ukwenza umonakalo, singene kalula
ekhaya. 

OSiphiwosakhe benoSibongiseni besazitika ngoju nezinja zisazitika
ngamakhafilithi amanye ayemfimfithwa aphinyiswe yibo abanikazi bazo
izinja laba, ngaphumelela UKUSHUTHEKA umgxala ungene ntshi phakathi
kwamatshe lawo. 

"Uvalo lwabashaya bonke," KUQHUBEKA uZwangedwa.

Lapho yasukuma yaze yagquma into yakwabo, kwazise umkhaba
wawunyomfozeka uma isukuma bese INCISHEKA umoya. 

Ngizokutshena ukuthi uMhlangana sengimbonele elakhe icebo, kodwa
kusweleke siqaphe ngoba unabalandeli abaningi OKUNGASWELEKILE babone
ukuthi siqondeni.

"Dingane, ubizwe yimi, ngoba uMhlangana uthi nawe KUSWELEKE ube
khona lapha nxashana siqala lendaba yokuqeda lombango phakathi kwenu."

Ngizokutshena ukuthi uMhlangana sengimbonele elakhe icebo, kodwa
KUSWELEKE siqaphe ngoba unabalandeli abaningi okungaswelekile babone
ukuthi siqondeni.

Ngithe onqobile ohluliwe KOSWELEKA azi kahle ukuthi wahluliwe,
angaphindi asuse uchuku ezweni.

KUSADINGEKA niphekwe impela nivuthwe tobo namuhla, kusho yena
uMphathi-sikole. 

Ukuze kuphele uchuku nengozi engasivele, KUSWELEKE niye emfuleni
nezinceku zami kuphela, zisale ezenu ekhaya.

Bobabili bamane BASHAQEKA nje ukuthi uThisha Omkhulu uqale nini ukuba
ngumbhidi. 

Ongaliphethe lolo qwenjana wayeyogcina esangweni, AKUKHATHALEKILE
ukuthi waziwa kangakanani nokuthi wejwayele kangakanani ukuzophuza
kwaMaqhuzu. 

Umuntu uya athi fuqaqa phansi noma yini abeyenza, AKUKHATHALEKILE
ukuthi beyibaluleke kangakanani, aphuthume lapho kuvele khona isidumo.


Lapho yasukuma yaze yagquma into yakwabo, kwazise umkhaba
WAWUNYOMFOZEKA uma isukuma bese incisheka umoya. 

YEHLULEKA ibhesi. 

Kuthe lapho isidumbu besikhiphela phandle WAQULEKA oweNkosi,"
esho ebheka uDingane.

Njengoba wayesehambe bonke ubusuku, kwenye indawo ehamba
ngokugijima, WAZUMEKA waze wavuka emini enkulu, kwabe nokulamba
sekuthe ngilapha. 

Izinkomo sithi sibuya nazo zimboze izintaba nezinkalo, igazi
labaningi bakithi LICHITHEKELE ezizweni, singakaphumuli useyasibiza
ukuba siyekohlasela kwezinye izindawo." 

Ngaphezu KOKUDIDEKA kwakukhona novalo lokuthi loku kuhamba
isikhathi eside kangaka, kwakuzomxabanisa noyise, uSiphepho, uPamella.


Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,
kwabuye kwavunyelwanwa ngokuthi okungenani yena angahluthulela izicabha,
aqinisike ukuthi ZIHLUTHULEKISISILE phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi obucayi wokudidizelisa uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi bembamba ukuze angaloku eba yisiphazamiso. 

Kwathathwa izinyathelo zokuphepha eziqinile, ukuze KUGWEMEKE ingozi
yokufela ekhaya. 

Ziyajabula izinsizwa EZIKHULULEKILEYO eziya lapho zithanda khona.

NoSolomon Mpungose useduze kwebhokisi lofakazi ngenqola
YABAKHUBAZEKILE. 

Nxa bengingumuntu OKHULULEKILEYO bengizolihamba lelilizwe elibanzi
ngiye ngiyibone. 

Bathe lapho bekhuleka kuMkabayi amehlo abantu ayenamathele kubo
nezindlebe ZIVULEKILE, zilinde ukucosha abazokusho.

Hhayi indaba yokusibabazela ukuthi BENITHILILEKA kwasha kwacima.


Ngesizathu sokuthi wayebahlonipha abathengi bakhe uMaqhuzu, wabona
kunesidingo sokubachazela ukuthi sivezwe yini isidingo sokuba bashiye
okusazikhali abakuphethe endlini ethize eduze kwesango, nokuthi kufanele
ngani kusungulwe ikilabhu yabaphuzi, okuyothi labo abafisa ukuba
ngamalunga ayo baphathe izingqwenjana ezifakazela ukuthi bangobani,
ezinezithombe zabo, ukuze BEMUKELEKE. 

Nokho AQHUBEKE. 

Aphefumule kakhulu lapho uSteve, abuye AQHUBEKE, "Asiqale ezinye
izindaba, ayikho lento." 

Izalukazi-ke azisenaso lesiya sililo nezinyembezi okungathiwa
KUYABABAZEKA. 

Bahamba-ke bedabula lezonkalo nemimango, nezintaba EZESABEKAYO, baze
bafika lapha eNingizimu nezwe.

Kuthe lapho esehlangana khona lapho, sekuzosuka impi enkulu
EYESABEKAYO, kwaqhamuka uDingane ehlobe evathe ephelele.

Bathi dedelele lapho bezwa ukuthi akukho sigigaba ESIBABAZEKAYO
abalandisa ngaso uMaqhuzu. 

Ekuseni uNozitshela usehlezi emnyango ukuba emukele okuphumayo
angenise OKUDINGEKAYO. 

Yabe inenhliziyo elukhuni njengetshe; ingesabi lutho' umzimba wayo
umuhle ubunjwe kahle kakhulu, UTHANDEKA; amehlo ayo lawa ekhanya
inhlansi, elokoza umlilo - lapho esethukuthele ayeba bomvu sengathi
agcwele igazi.

Ongaliphethe lolo qwenjana wayeyogcina esangweni, akukhathalekile
ukuthi waziwa kangakanani nokuthi WEJWAYELE kangakanani ukuzophuza
kwaMaqhuzu. 

SIZOBUYELA futhi ukuze siyizwe kahle lendaba, siyiqale ekuqaleni
size sizofika lapho uDingane asusa khona isenzo esashaqisa izwe lonke.

BATAKADELA belu abanye nezinqola, nezinkomo, nemizi, nakho konke.

Naye wayeseze WEJWAYELA ukubulala abantu ngoba noma into iyimbi
inxa umuntu eseyenzele futhi ayibe isabambi. 

Kwase kuzobakhona nesiqiniseko sokuthi umuntu uzoziphuzela
ngenkululeko, angathi ephethe ingilazi yotshwala ngapha, ebe ejeqeza,
ELINDELE ukudonsa ivolovolo ngokuphazima kweso. 

Kodwa BAQULUSELA phambili kunokuba babuyele emuva ekuphathweni
umbuso wamaNgisi.

Yathi lendaba ukuba IPHUMELE ngaphandle kubantu kwaya ngokwanda
ukunengeka kukaShaka. 

Namatshe AYEQAQELE eqeleni phakathi kwezinyosi nezingwenya
ayezihlalele njena ngaphezulu. 

Kodwa baqulusela phambili kunokuba BABUYELE emuva ekuphathweni
umbuso wamaNgisi.

Lesi simo sabe sesimvula amehlo uMaqhuzu, wazibona kahle ukuthi
ukuhlakanipha kwakhe KUPHELELA obala uma kungenasesekelo
esiyisitifiketi. 

EzikaMaqhuzu zona zafikisa ubuhlungu ezinhliziyeweni zabantu ngoba
zazinamanembe egazi likaPamella, naku phela WAPHUMELA kuye umphefumulo
kaPamella. 

WEQELA ngaphesheya wasiphula isiqunga, wahlafuna impande yaso
wakhwifa, esusa wona umnyama wesidumbu. 


Onke amehlo abantu ANAMATHELA kuDingane, bambona ubuso bakhe
sebumanzi zinyembezi, ziwohloka emehlweni.

"Uminze emfuleni - WAFELA khona lapho."

Kwathi ukuba sisuke isidumo leso uMfundisi =Owen= wabopha
okungokwakhe wabamba indlela eqonde eThekwini, lapho wafika khona
WADLULELA phesheya eNgilande.

Namhla esewela uSuthu yahlamba eduze kwesikebhe yaye YAPHUMELA
ngaphesheya. 

Wasondela emzini wabona ukuthi kuphekwe emnyango, waququbala
buqamamana nomuzi, baze bephula bangena endlini, wasondela, izinja
zamuzwa, zamkhonkotha WABUYELA emuva, wafuna isu lokuyothatha
isikhuni esivuthayo lapho bekade bepheke khona. 

Kwathathwa izinyathelo zokuphepha eziqinile, ukuze kugwemeke ingozi
YOKUFELA ekhaya. 

Sonke lesi sikhati efuna umsebenzi, umqondo wakhe umtshela ukuthi
bayomcabangela labo abayomqasha, bamnike khathisimbe umsebenzi wokubhala
ehhovisi limbe noma-ke bamfake emsebenzini WOKWENGAMELA ophikweni
oluthile. 

Phela uma ikhona, babethi omakade ebona babasingi, uzibona
NGOKUBUNGELA kwazo othini; zingqengqe ngalo uma ulushutheka esidlekeni
sazo njengomkhuba ezisuke ziwejwayele. 

NoMdlunkulu kulezo zinsuku awuvunyelwe ukuhlala NOKUDLELA egcekeni.


Nxa sebegezile BABUYELE ekhaya, kufafazwe enye intelezi emnyango
welawu leNkosi, ingene khona, alandele uJeqe, afike endlale, ilale
elawini ngalobo busuku emva kokuba ikade ilala endlini yamakhosi
namadlozi. 

Amehlo awo wonke umuntu AGQOLOZELE ezitebhisini okwehle ngazo
iphoyisa elilande indoda yesando esitokisini. 

ESEWELELE kwelama Thonga yahlonga imizi eduze nomfula, wahamba
waze wadundubala phezu kwesihlambo somfula kwaba yikhona ebona imizi,
ezwa izinkomo zikhonya. 

USiphepho lowo kwabe kungumnumzane OVELELE endaweni yaseMaBheleni.


Wayengazimisele uSteve ukuxabana noMama wakhe ngalelo langa kodwa
le mibuzo ayembelesele ngayo YAYIHOLELA engxabanweni. 

Kwakuthi uma zivikisana nabazala bakhe ekhaya, kuzibonakalele nje
ukuthi yize abanye babo befunda emaNyuvesi, amanzi AYEHLELA ngakubo,
ivuthiwe insizwa kaMdletshe le ekhanda. 

Wedlula kwabamaphephandaba, wabanika yonke imininingwane ngoyise,
enzela ukuba izihlobo ezikude nabangane bezwe ngesifo esivele,
WAYESEDLULELA ekhaya. 

Laba abasekwayeni wathi angathi abakhiphe iminwe, wathi abacule
BAPHUMELE phandle bagcwale igceke. 

Emuva kwalokho wathi abaphume BABUYELE emakilasini abo bonke
ababengekho ekwayeni. 

Ngizwa kuthiwa noNdlela noNzobo izinduna zakho ezinkulu ZIGEBELA
ngakuye.

Uthe EBUYELA ezigabeni wafika lesi sithunywa sikaDingane sesihambile,
ethi uzosixoxela lendaba embi nebuhlungu yokuhlinza umuntu wesifazane
ekhulelwe. 

Ngalesi sikhathi iqembu elikhulu lamaBhunu, elalilandela, lafika nalo
lamisa otende bezindlu eduze nomfula uThukela, abanye njalo BENYUKELA enhla
bayokwakha enhla noMnambithi.

Bakhala ngezingane zabo EZIPHELELA ezimpini. 

Mina ngithi uwe ONGEVELA nesu ngoba usondele kakhulu kuye kunabo
bonke abantu. 

Ngesizathu sokuthi wayebahlonipha abathengi bakhe uMaqhuzu, wabona
kunesidingo sokubachazela ukuthi sivezwe yini isidingo sokuba bashiye
okusazikhali abakuphethe endlini ethize eduze kwesango, nokuthi KUFANELE
ngani kusungulwe ikilabhu yabaphuzi, okuyothi labo abafisa ukuba
ngamalunga ayo baphathe izingqwenjana ezifakazela ukuthi bangobani,
ezinezithombe zabo, ukuze bemukeleke. 

Lensizwa YAPHINDELA njengesikhonzi koMkhulu. 

Ukhula LUZALELA izinyoni emasimini ami ngikhuluma nje. 

Ukuphuthuma lokhu kwenziwa ukuba babegcina ukuthi yinhloli,
uthunywe kwaZulu ukuba azohlola KULANDELE impi ngoba ukulanda kwwakhe
kokufika kwakhe ezweni labo akubahlabanga umxhwele. 

Liyaphuma ilanga amabutho aseya emfuleni aseyogeza, sekugcwele
abafana namantombazana ABALETHELE amabutho ukudla. 

Cishu sakhohlwa ukulanda ukuthi laphaya oPhongolo lapha uJeqe
wayegula khona, kukhona inja yakuwo lowo muzi eyamejwayela, kuthi
lapho lomfazi OWAYELETHELA uJeqe ukudla eya kuJeqe, ihambe naye,
adle nokuncane ayishiyele, yaze yamejwayela, kwathi mhla ehambayo
yamlandela ngomkhondo yaze yamfica, yaba seyiba yinja yakhe njalo.


Nokho wabuye WAFEKELA lowo mqondo, wabona ukuthi kuyobe uyasehlisa
isithunzi sakhe, nokuhlonishwa kwakhe, nokwaziwa kwakhe njengomuntu
ongasohlangothini lomthetho. 

NGADUMELA umgxala ngawushutheka embhacwini owawuphakathi
kwezinguzunga ezimbili zamatshe ezazilakanyene. 

Kuthe sebe kude-buduze nezwe laseNatali, sebevinjelwe uKhahlamba
kuphela, uMnumzane uPieter =Retief= nedlanzana labanye nezinqola zabo,
BALANDULELA iqembu elikhulu, baze batheleka lapha eNatali ngonyaka
ka-1837.

Kwathi emva kweviki, bayovela eNkantolo oMaqhuzu, ngenhloso
YOKUBINGELELA iMantshi. 

Lapho sebebuyile ekugezeni badla, ngesikhathi zibuya inhlazane,
baqale manje UKUVUNULELA umkhosi. 

Uma ngabe ugugile, UGUGELE mina. 

Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,
kwabuye kwavunyelwanwa ngokuthi okungenani yena ANGAHLUTHULELA izicabha,
aqinisike ukuthi zihluthulekisisile phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi obucayi wokudidizelisa uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi bembamba ukuze angaloku eba yisiphazamiso. 

Lingena nje sebeke bahlangana abazali bezigebengu, bavumelana
ngokuthi kungeze kwaba yinto enhle uma bethatha ummeli ngoba loko
kuyobonakala sengathi kuyindlela abavuna ngayo izingane zabo, nabazama
ngayo ukuba izingane zabo zingasitholi isijezo ESIFANELE isenzo sazo.

Wathi akantshontshi emizini asuke ebulele kuwona ngoba usuke
ENGANGENELE kona ukuntshontsha. 

Owokuqala umqondo wakhe ukuba afe neNkosi yakhe njengoba nasempini
WAYELUNGELE ukufa. 

Waphaphama uJeqe, uthe ephaphama enye yezinceku YAYIKHWEZELA
isihlonti soqunga, wacikica amehlo, wacabanga. 

Mathathu amaphuzu AYEFAKAZELA loko. 

Ngifulathele amathongo mina NGILANDELE umfazi? 

NGIFULATHELE amathongo mina ngilandele umfazi? 

Yikhona engingakuthandi du lokhu kukhuthala kwakhe AKHUTHALELE
imisebenzi yamanye amadoda. 

"Dingane, ubizwe yimi, ngoba uMhlangana uthi nawe kusweleke ube
khona lapha nxashana SIQLELA lendaba yokuqeda lombango phakathi kwenu."

Mhla kuzokusa kube umkhosi iNkosi iyophuma lapho endlini kuvalwe,
iholwe inyanga iphethe ukhamba lwentelezi, iyifafaze intelezi baye
bafike emfuleni, uJeqe ELANDELA iNkosi ephethe eminye imithi okuzofikwa
emfuleni phakathi kobusuku yelapha. 

KUFANELE akwazi loku, senzele ukuthi noma ngabe kwenzekani
kuNobuhle, noma ngabe kwenzekani lapha ekhaya, angasisoli ukuthi
sasingamtsheli ngani. 

Naso-ke isizathu sokuqala ESABANGELA amaBhunu siwabone esephungwa
ngezithebe kwaZulu, ekhumbuza uDingane izinkonjane ezabikwa nguShaka
mhla efayo.

Wedlula kwabamaphephandaba, wabanika yonke imininingwane ngoyise,
ENZELA ukuba izihlobo ezikude nabangane bezwe ngesifo esivele,
wayesedlulela ekhaya. 

Wageza ENZELA ukuba abe nendlela emhlophe njengoba nakhu esuka
esidunjini. 

Lathi liqambe liba sokhakhayini, base bebuyile ukuyoyigcwalisa
ithange, BENZELA ukuthi umsebenzi wabo ungaphazanyiswa yinto
ewubuphukuphuku njengokuphelelwa u-petrol bengakafiki lapho beya khona.


Wayengawazi amandla kaNobuhle uMaqhuzu, ngaleso sizathu wamfundisa
amasu nezindlela zokusetshenziswa kwesibhamu, ENZELA ukuthi uma
imqhamukela kabi eyabafo, akwazi ukwelekelela uNobuhle. 

LeNkosikazi yasemaNgisini yayinenhliziyo emhlophe impela, ithanda
izinto ezilungileyo zodwa, ibusa ngesandla esilungileyo, esinozwela,
esikhuthazayo kuzo zonke izinhlangothi zezizwe ezingaphansi kwentende
yombuso wayo; kakhulu ezizweni ezimnyama, nezibuthakathaka, yayifike
IGCIZELELE ekuthini bonke abaziphetheyo - isho oHulumeni phela
ababengaphansi koMbuso waseNgilandi - mabazikhuthaze ekuhlaleni kwazo.
bazivulele izintuba zokuzakha, nazo zibengabantu abazihloniphayo
nabazethembayo, ingafuni nempela ukuba kube khona umahluko ekubusweni
kwabantu, kuthiwe laba banje ngakho kufanele baphathwe kanje.

Kufanele akwazi loku, SENZELE ukuthi noma ngabe kwenzekani
kuNobuhle, noma ngabe kwenzekani lapha ekhaya, angasisoli ukuthi
sasingamtsheli ngani. 

Ngesizathu sokuthi wayebahlonipha abathengi bakhe uMaqhuzu, wabona
kunesidingo sokubachazela ukuthi sivezwe yini isidingo sokuba bashiye
okusazikhali abakuphethe endlini ethize eduze kwesango, nokuthi kufanele
ngani kusungulwe ikilabhu yabaphuzi, okuyothi labo abafisa ukuba
ngamalunga ayo baphathe izingqwenjana EZIFAKAZELA ukuthi bangobani,
ezinezithombe zabo, ukuze bemukeleke. 

Besesukuma uMkabayi ephonsa elakhe kusenjalo abantu besadabukile,
ENZELA ukuze bayaqala bayacabanga useliphonsile.

Bahlala-ke SEBELUNGELE ukuze kulungiswe ingcwaba layo. 

Abone uMkabayi ukuthi uma engayiqedi lendaba zingahle ZIDUMELANE
khona lapho izinsizwa zomfowabo uSenzangakhona.

Lingena nje sebeke bahlangana abazali bezigebengu, BAVUMELANA
ngokuthi kungeze kwaba yinto enhle uma bethatha ummeli ngoba loko
kuyobonakala sengathi kuyindlela abavuna ngayo izingane zabo, nabazama
ngayo ukuba izingane zabo zingasitholi isijezo esifanele isenzo sazo.

Nempela lomqondo BAVUMELANA bonke ngawo.

Insizwa ingena khona izazi ukuthi ayibhedelwa, kodwa ithotshiswe
ngabafana abancane, bayishaye BADEDELANE ngayo ize ithambe potololo.


BAJAMELANA ngamehlo amabi.

Lokhu ukulwa, namazwi enhlamba ABAKHIPHELANA wona abikwe kuShaka.


Phezu kwakho konke lokhu osekuluthuthuva phakathi kukaZulu abanye
BABENGAVUMELANI. 

Amabutho nhlangothi zombili agxume kube sengathi AZODUMELANA.

OSiphiwosakhe benoSibongiseni besazitika ngoju nezinja zisazitika
ngamakhafilithi amanye ayemfimfithwa aphinyiswe yibo abanikazi bazo
izinja laba, NGAPHUMELELA ukushutheka umgxala ungene ntshi phakathi
kwamatshe lawo. 

Wayelivuma elokuthi bangcono kunaye ngoba banezitifiketi ezingcono
kunaloko AYEBAMBELELE kukona, kodwa-ke yize kunjalo, umuntu akahlali
ephethe isitifiketi ngesandla. 

Lokhu zikwenzela ukuba sithi SIFINYELELA ojwini lwazo sifice itshe
selome inhlama. 

Phela zenza kanjalo uma sezibona isitha SIPHIKELELE emaqeni azo
ekhethelo. 

Nabafana bami base bembe baze bakhathala BENGAFINYELELI eqeni
eligangileyo lendlovukazi yezinyosi. 

Wayengawazi amandla kaNobuhle uMaqhuzu, ngaleso sizathu wamfundisa
amasu nezindlela zokusetshenziswa kwesibhamu, enzela ukuthi uma
imqhamukela kabi eyabafo, akwazi UKWELEKELELA uNobuhle. 

Kuningi abanye ababekungabaza NGOKUPHELELA kwazo lapha kumfo
kaMshengu. 

Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,
kwabuye kwavunyelwanwa ngokuthi okungenani yena angahluthulela izicabha,
aqinisike ukuthi zihluthulekisisile phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi obucayi WOKUDIDIZELISA uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi bembamba ukuze angaloku eba yisiphazamiso. 

Isivakashi sasiyokwamukelwa kuphela uma sihamba nomuntu ophethe
uqwenjana lolo, aphinde futhi ANIKEZE isiqiniseko sokuthi singumuntu onjani.


Ngase kube ukhuluma indaba yokuthi uyashada nje kanti ukhuluma indaba
yalowa ntangayethu owayefuna ukungihlaba ngesibhakela emgwaqweni KUBUKELA
abantu? 

Bathe lapho beziphonsa phakathi esizibeni oNdongeni noSiphepho
noZidumo bamfica ESEPHANGALELE okaSenzangakhona.

Kuthe lapho esehlangana khona lapho, sekuzosuka impi enkulu
eyesabekayo, kwaqhamuka uDingane ehlobe evathe EPHELELE.

Waphupha kufike oyisemkhulu, onke amadlozi akubo EPHELELE, athi
kuye. 

Ngesikhashana esincane nje yilelo selimi kweyalo indawo, esehlome
ESEPHELELE, aseyahaya. 

"Ngoba nike naxoxa naye uButhelezi, kuhle UPHINDELE umncenge uthi
uDingane uyokuhlanza bonke ubumnyama bensila kaShaka akwakhele umuzi
omkhulu emva kokuba usugezwe ngentelezi, futhi mhla efayo uShaka
uyokulondoloza ungambelwa naye." 

UMaZwane wathi ngokubona ukuthi UZALELWE yinja endlini, wacela
umkhokheli uMaNzuza ukuba azomncengela uMdlalose ukuba asihoxise isinqumo
sakhe sokumkhipha enkonzweni. 

Cishe ukuba SATHAKASELWA nguwonk' uwonke lesi sinyathelo ngoba vele
eGoli akwethenjwa muntu. 

Kuthe ebusuku EFIKELWE isihlambi sobuthongo, ngoba buyinkosi, noma
umuntu elinde isidumbu wethuka esengquphazela nje, waphupha uJeqe.

Lathi liqambe liba sokhakhayini, base bebuyile ukuyoyigcwalisa
ithange, benzela ukuthi umsebenzi wabo ungaphazanyiswa yinto
ewubuphukuphuku NJENGOKUPHELELWA u-petrol bengakafiki lapho beya khona.


Babodwa ababethi uyogwetshwa isigwebo SOKUDILIKELWA yijele kanti
iningi lalithi wayezogwetshwa intambo. 

Loko KWAKUFAKAZELWA yizisihle ezazibonakala lapha phansi kwamehlo abo
uma usondela ubabhekisisa kahle. 

Sifile, SIVELELWE yingozi embi.

Nazo zase ZIPHELELWE yithemba. 
Nokho WAYENGAKEHLELWA yilokhu okwamehlela ngelinye ilanga,
besesigodlweni esingaphandle lapho kuhlala khona izinceku eziganiweyo.

Phela wona ayenazo izigqila ezimnyama, ziziningi impela,
ESETSHENZELWA yizo; futhi nje wona ayenomqondo othi bonke abantu
abamnyama badalelwa ukukhonza omhlophe, abe yisigqila sakhe.

NoMdlunkulu kulezo zinsuku AWUVUNYELWE ukuhlala nokudlela egcekeni.


Phela wona ayenazo izigqila ezimnyama, ziziningi impela,
esetshenzelwa yizo; futhi nje wona ayenomqondo othi bonke abantu
abamnyama BADALELWA ukukhonza omhlophe, abe yisigqila sakhe.

Lamadoda ayisandla sayo, njengoba nanamuhla iNkosi uGeroge weSihlanu
obusa eNgilandi EBANJELWE kulelizwe laseSouth Afrika nguLusibalukhulu.

"Angazi, noma kubuhlungu kangaka ukubona abantu imihla namalanga
BECEKELWA phansi lapha ekhaya nangemikhonto yezizwe." 

Onke amanya amabi akhishwa eNkosini ESULELWA kuJeqe. 

Njengoba insila yeNkosi IMBELWA nayo, wanele wabona nje uJeqe
ukuthi iNkosi yakhe sebeyigwazile, sekumelwe ukuba abulawe nxashana
isilahlwa, wafikelwa imicabango eminingi. 


"Kulungile, ngomuso kusasa nizoqonda emfuleni, njengemihla yonke,
nithi nibuya lapho bese niyovunula seniza ebandla, lapho kobe
sekubuthene abantu ABAZOBIKELWA ngenkatha.

Uselwa LWALUKHETHELWA abalo njalo okuye kuthi nxa iNkosi
isizokweshwama baye kolukha eduze nolwandle. 

Kuthe sebe kude-buduze nezwe laseNatali, SEBEVINJELWE uKhahlamba
kuphela, uMnumzane uPieter =Retief= nedlanzana labanye nezinqola zabo,
balandulela iqembu elikhulu, baze batheleka lapha eNatali ngonyaka
ka-1837.

SIVELELWE ishwa elibi ezweni namuhla.

Lelozwi lavuma ukuthi njengoba izigqila lezo bezibasiza abaninizo
zibasebenzela yonke imisebenzi lena bazobuyiselwa UKULAHLEKELWA kwabo
izigqila ngohlamvana lwemali.

Njengoba insila yeNkosi imbelwa nayo, wanele wabona nje uJeqe
ukuthi iNkosi yakhe sebeyigwazile, sekumelwe ukuba abulawe nxashana
isilahlwa, WAFIKELWA imicabango eminingi. 

KUTHANDAZELWA abagulayo. 

Intaka IBEKELWE amazolo namuhla. 

Phela iNkosikazi ibusa nje eNgilandi IBHEKELWE amadoda
ahlakaniphileyo kwamanye amazwe.

Wathula, Dingane, ubukhosi bakho BUZULELWA amanqe.

Uma-ke umuntu kuthiwa uyobingelela iMantshi kusuke kuqondwe ukuthi
uzovela nje phambi kweNkatholo, IBIKELWE iMantshi ukuthi lo ngusibanibani
wakwabani, owethweswe icala elithile, alenza ngosuku oluthile. 

Izimpendulo zikaNobuhle zazingaphezulu kwemibuzo kaMaqhuzu, into
eyenza ukuba AKHANYELWE uMaqhuzu ukuthi ufeleba lo unguphuma-langa-sikothe
nje nasekhanda uvuthiwe. 

Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,
kwabuye KWAVUNYELWANWA ngokuthi okungenani yena angahluthulela izicabha,
aqinisike ukuthi zihluthulekisisile phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi obucayi wokudidizelisa uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi bembamba ukuze angaloku eba yisiphazamiso. 

Abameli, owommangalelwa amnikwe nguHulumeni nabemindeni EFELWEYO,
nabo basezindaweni zabo. 

Wayitshela ngesimekemeke sendaba ayenziwe yiNkosi ukuba aqaqe
owesifazane EKHULELWE. 

Uthe ebuyela ezigabeni wafika lesi sithunywa sikaDingane sesihambile,
ethi uzosixoxela lendaba embi nebuhlungu yokuhlinza umuntu wesifazane
EKHULELWE. 

Ukuba NGIYESHELWA ngabe kade ngaqoma, noma ngabe kade ngashada.


Insizwa ingena khona izazi ukuthi AYIBHEDELWA, kodwa ithotshiswe
ngabafana abancane, bayishaye badedelane ngayo ize ithambe potololo.


Njengoba insila yeNkosi imbelwa nayo, wanele wabona nje uJeqe
ukuthi iNkosi yakhe sebeyigwazile, SEKUMELWE ukuba abulawe nxashana
isilahlwa, wafikelwa imicabango eminingi. 

"KANGITHULE, Zulu," kububula uDingane.

Emuva kwalokho wathi ABAPHUME babuyele emakilasini abo bonke
ababengekho ekwayeni. 

Wona amehlo ayeselokoza umlilo, isifuba lesi sakhe sehla senyuka,
kubonakala ukuthi uZibambile sekuthi MAKAQHUME.

Laba abasekwayeni wathi angathi abakhiphe iminwe, wathi ABACULE
baphumele phandle bagcwale igceke. 

"Ngizwile, Zulu. MANA njalo wena kaNdaba." kubonga uDingane.

Wathula eside isikhathi, amehlo akhe ETHE mbe kuDingane.

Badla utshwala nenyama kwathula KWATHI du. 

Lapho sekuthule KUTHE du.

Kuthule futhi KUTHI du.

Kukhnoa ijongosi lentombi yeThonga kulowo muzi elihle, LITHE klwi
ngothi lomzimba. 

Abantu sebethule BETHE du, uDingane noMkabayi bebheke phansi engekho
obheke omunye.

Sekuzwakala nezigqi zokuphefumula kubantu: umoya lona UNGASATHI
nyaka, nezinyoni imbala ezabe zixokozela, zathula, kwasengathi
zitsheliwe ukuthi nansi indaba embi.

"LALELA-ke, Dingane. Indaba kaMbopha kaSithayi sengiyilungisile.

"KHULUMA, Ndongeni, ungade ugwinya amathe sengathi kawazi ukuthi
uthini."

HAMBA umtshene ukuthi ngithi kakukho engikwesabayo mina lapha
ezweni.

SUKA uhambe khona manje ungalindi noma kuze kuse. 

XOLA nje Nyanda. 

`SUKUMA, Nkosi yesizwe, wena omiswe ngabangasekho ukuba ubuse
elikaSenzangakhona." esho eqondisa kuDingane.

Khiphani izwi LOKUGCINA.

Kwase kuzobakhona nesiqiniseko sokuthi umuntu uzoziphuzela
ngenkululeko, angathi ephethe ingilazi yotshwala ngapha, ebe ejeqeza,
elindele ukudonsa ivolovolo NGOKUPHAZIMA kweso. 

UMaZwane ngizoke ngithi ukumyeka-ke aqhubeke NOKUSONTA. 

Njengoba wayesehambe bonke ubusuku, kwenye indawo ehamba
NGOKUGIJIMA, wazumeka waze wavuka emini enkulu, kwabe nokulamba
sekuthe ngilapha. 

Wagcina ngakho nje UKUSUKUMA waxhiliba. 

EKUSENI ilanga lingakaphumi, umuntu usezwa umsindo ezigabeni,
behaya amagama bebhema insangu, bebonga amakhosi. 

Ilokhu ethunywa uJeqe nje ukuba abulale abantu, iNkosi ifuna
ukususa isihawu kuye abenjengayo ngesibindi SOKUBULALA njengoba
eyinsila yayo nje. 

NoMdlunkulu kulezo zinsuku awuvunyelwe UKUHLALA nokudlela egcekeni.


Sekukhona izinkunzi ezimbili ezimnyama ezicijileyo, ezihlabayo,
ezingazange ziyizeke insikazi, ezanela UKWEPHUSA zakhethwa eziyobanjwa
amabutho ngezandla bazidonye ngesibhakele zize zife. 

Kepha inqaba lapho ikhona ayivumi UKUQOMA. 

Babedlubhe amasudi AKWANOKUSHO bobane. 

Sekuzwakala nezigqi ZOKUPHEFUMULA kubantu: umoya lona ungasathi
nyaka, nezinyoni imbala ezabe zixokozela, zathula, kwasengathi
zitsheliwe ukuthi nansi indaba embi.

Kwathathwa izinyathelo ZOKUPHEPHA eziqinile, ukuze kugwemeke ingozi
yokufela ekhaya. 

Kuthe lapho besikhipha isidumbu sakhe emanzini, kwahlaluka ukuthi
okaSenzangakhona wabefinyele umsipha, wambamba ngamandla esemanzini
ajulile, kazathola nathuba LOKUPHEFUMULA.

"O, wena weZulu, sesaba NOKUKHULUMA," kuqhuba uNdongeni, ekhefuzela
uvalo.

Emuva kwesikhashana washaya insimbi umfo kaShabalala izingane zonke
eziculayo zabuthana ehholo zisaqhubeka NOKUMPONGOLOZA zicula. 

Bantwana kuyacaca ukuthi anifundisekile neze kahle UKUCULA. 

Uthe ephandle umqondo WOKWEQA wagunya. 

ZAZIKHAMISE kakhulu zakhipha izilimi zihefuzela. 

Sizobuyela futhi ukuze siyizwe kahle lendaba, siyiqale ekuqaleni
size sizofika lapho uDingane ASUSA khona isenzo esashaqisa izwe lonke.

Naphezu lokhu kuhlola abafana bami babeqale ngakho ngangikuphindela
ukuzenelisa ukuthi kwakungekho halakasha yini lwenyoka EZAZINGENISE
emgodini walo zihlala nalo izinyosi lezi. 

KUYASHISA elawini lezinsizwa. 

LeNkosikazi yasemaNgisini yayinenhliziyo emhlophe impela, ithanda
izinto ezilungileyo zodwa, ibusa ngesandla esilungileyo, esinozwela,
ESIKHUTHAZAYO kuzo zonke izinhlangothi zezizwe ezingaphansi kwentende
yombuso wayo; kakhulu ezizweni ezimnyama, nezibuthakathaka, yayifike
igcizelele ekuthini bonke abaziphetheyo - isho oHulumeni phela
ababengaphansi koMbuso waseNgilandi - mabazikhuthaze ekuhlaleni kwazo,
bazivulele izintuba zokuzakha, nazo zibengabantu abazihloniphayo
nabazethembayo, ingafuni nempela ukuba kube khona umahluko ekubusweni
kwabantu, kuthiwe laba banje ngakho kufanele baphathwe kanje.

`Sukuma, Nkosi yesizwe, wena omiswe ngabangasekho ukuba ubuse
elikaSenzangakhona." esho EQONDISA kuDingane.

YEHLISA umoya. 

Ngaso leso sikhathi amabutho amasha ayengekho eye kohlasela le
kwaSoshangane, abanye sebefike bazikhonzela kwezinye izizwe bathi:
Sikhathele uShaka ESIBULALISA ngezinye izizwe! 

Aqala UKUHLANGANISA amakhanda manje, efuna isu angalenza
lokubalekela ubuhlungu obungako.

THULISA uDingana kuqala.

EzikaMaqhuzu zona ZAFIKISA ubuhlungu ezinhliziyeweni zabantu ngoba
zazinamanembe egazi likaPamella, naku phela waphumela kuye umphefumulo
kaPamella. 

Ngalesi sikhathi iqembu elikhulu lamaBhunu, elalilandela, lafika nalo
LAMISA otende bezindlu eduze nomfula uThukela, abanye njalo benyukela enhla
bayokwakha enhla noMnambithi.

Sizoke siyizwe lento enkulu EYASUSA uthuli olungako ezweni
lakwaZulu, yaphemba umlilo omkhulu ongacimiyo kuze kube namuhla usazinge
ulokoza.

Ukuba uMaqhuzu wayenazo ezinye izindlela zokuziphilisa, neziletha
imali ngamawala njengomsebenzi wokudayisa utshwala, wayezothatha zona,
abuyeke utshwala ngoba BABUSONDEZA abantu abaningi eduze kwakhe,into
eyayingenza ukuthi nesitha esiqonde ukwenza umonakalo, singene kalula
ekhaya. 

Ukuze asondele eNkosini uShaka kwaya ngoba wadunyiswa enye induna
yathi uyifundile imithi yasenyakatho, kunjalo nje USESINDISE abaningi
ngamakhambi. 

Wathi angaqeda ukubabhaxabula abafana WAYESECULISA izindlela zonke
ngayinye. 

Naso-ke isizathu sokuqala esabangela amaBhunu siwabone esephungwa
ngezithebe kwaZulu, EKHUMBUZA uDingane izinkonjane ezabikwa nguShaka
mhla efayo.

Bala washesha ukuwamukela loko abe ekufundiswa, into EYAKHOMBISA
uMaqhuzu ukuthi wabe ezimisele kangakanani ukufa lapho efa khona.


Naye kahlalanga sikathi eside kwaZulu, ngoba kwathi esahlezi
izinyanga ezine kuphela uDingane WASUSA isidumo esikhulu kwaZulu, okuze
kube namuhla sisashaqisa izwe lonke.
=Adams= kwaqanjwa ngaye umuzi owaziwayo waseAdams,
oseManzimtoti, base benza-ke belinga UKUTHAMBISA izinhliziyo
zabakwaZulu.

Ukuba uMaqhuzu wayenazo ezinye izindlela zokuziphilisa, neziletha
imali ngamawala njengomsebenzi WOKUDAYISA utshwala, wayezothatha zona,
abuyeke utshwala ngoba babusondeza abantu abaningi eduze kwakhe, into
eyayingenza ukuthi nesitha esiqonde ukwenza umonakalo, singene kalula
ekhaya. 

Bala kwaba wukuqeda inkomishi yetiye ababemenzele yona UKWEHLISA
izintuli zendlela, wabe esebamba ebheke eMnsinsini emaphoyiseni. 

Enzansi laphaya osebeni lomfula babesabonakala ofeleba bezingwenya
bethe bukululu BEKHAMISE imilomo yaba yizinkebenkebe. 

Yiwona ayesho njalo, iningi labanye abamhlophe lalingaboni lutho
olungako OLWALUKHALISA amaBhunu, olungaze luwalumise izinyawo ababange
ngokuhamba.

Phela WAYESAZOVEZA ububi bakhe bonke uDingane; ngalenkathi waye
ngakaqini kangako.

Umfundisi esizwa kuthiwa uDingane wamvumela ukuba ahlale eduze
naye AFUNDISE abantu bakhe, kuthiwa nguMfundisi =Owen= Lowo.

Ekuseni uNozitshela usehlezi emnyango ukuba emukele okuphumayo
ANGENISE okudingekayo. 

Lomfo ufika uyabika uthi: "Ngimlinge ngamaqhinga amaningi uJeqe
ngithi asihlangane naye ADLISE uShaka." 

Komunye umhlangano wabo BAVEZA icebo lokuba bathume umuntu
njengesikhonzi ayothola uJeqe ukuba naye abe ngakubona, abadlisele
uShaka ngobuthi ekudleni kwakhe. 

Kwaba uye OSONDEZA amanzi okuyigeza, kwaba yilokhu imthuma ukuba
abheke ukuthi ukudla kwayo kulungiswe kahle na. 

Sizobuyela futhi ukuze siyizwe kahle lendaba, siyiqale ekuqaleni
size sizofika lapho uDingane asusa khona isenzo ESASHAQISA izwe lonke.

Kwaphela isonto uJeqe neNkosi nenyanga bevumbeleke kuleyondlu,
ibaphethe inyanga ibagcaba, IPHALAZISA iNkosi ngezintelezi ezinkulu,
ezimhlophe nezimnyama. 

Naye kahlalanga sikathi eside kwaZulu, ngoba kwathi esahlezi
izinyanga ezine kuphela uDingane wasusa isidumo esikhulu kwaZulu, okuze
kube namuhla SISASHAQISA izwe lonke.

UKHULUMISA okwesiwula, Dingane.

Yathi ukuba ingene esigodlweni sikaDingane, yangena maqede washaywa
uvalo uDingane, KWAZISE ukuthi yabe inesithunzi esesabekayo kakhulu.

Nababusi bawo abakhulu ababebusa ngesikathi amaNgisi engakanqobi
izwe, babe nalowomqondo: umuntu omnyama yisichaka somhlophe, futhi basho
BAQINISE ukuthi noma umuntu umphethe kabi, noma umenzani, kakusono leso,
ngoba uyinto yomhlophe phela.

Kwakungesizo izimotshwana nje, kwakuyizinqola impela EZIKHOMBISA
ukuthi nangamhla zithengwa kwacashunwa insavunsavu yamarandi, kwaphinda
kwasala enye insavunsavu. 

Kepha-ke Mntanami, uMaZwane BESISAHAMBISANA kahle kabi naye
ebusizikazini. 

Kwakuthi uma ZIVIKISANA nabazala bakhe ekhaya, kuzibonakalele nje
ukuthi yize abanye babo befunda emaNyuvesi, amanzi ayehlela ngakubo,
ivuthiwe insizwa kaMdletshe le ekhanda. 


Wayeloku ebabaze nje ukuba mnandi KOKUHAMBISANA negugu lakhe, aze
alikhiphe ngisho ukulikhipha elokuthi ubengakaqonywa sonke lesi sikhathi,
ubesadlala nje. 

Uma ngabe loko AKUHAMBISANI nawe, akusho ukuthi umshado ngeke
wabakhona. 

UKUDAZISANA ngohlobo lwesigwebo okwakucatshangwa ukuthi uMpungose
wayezosithola kwaqala abantu bephuma nje emnyango wenkantolo. 

WATHULISA wabuka, wambona emi ethe ne ngomhlane othangweni. 

Bantwana kuyacaca ukuthi ANIFUNDISEKILE neze kahle ukucula. 

Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,
kwabuye kwavunyelwanwa ngokuthi okungenani yena angahluthulela izicabha,
AQINISIKE ukuthi zihluthulekisisile phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi obucayi wokudidizelisa uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi bembamba ukuze angaloku eba yisiphazamiso. 

Kuthe kusenjalo kwafika izwi livela phesheya kuHulumeni lithi:
"Izwe lelo elithunjwe nguHulumeni walelizwe kumaXhosa MALIBUYISELWE
kuwona."

Lelozwi lavuma ukuthi njengoba izigqila lezo bezibasiza abaninizo
zibasebenzela yonke imisebenzi lena BAZOBUYISELWA ukulahlekelwa kwabo
izigqila ngohlamvana lwemali.

Libe-ke SELIHLEHILISWELWA olunye usuku icala, kunqunywe nemali
engaba yisibambiso sokukhululwa kwakhe okwaleso sikhashana ibheyili.


Wathi abaculi bonke ABAKHAMISE bafake iminwe emibili emlonyeni. 

Wathi ubafundisa UKUKHAMISA ngoba wayesethole kahle ukuthi
bayabhimba. 

Konke esasikwenza nabafana bami oSiphiwosakhe noSibongiseni sase
sikwenza NGOKUPHANGISA. 

Babhinjiswa ukwehlulwa UKUKHAMISA. 

Ngiyabona. Athule isikhashana uMaqhuzu, uthule nje uyazinxaphela
ngengaphakathi, uzwa kahle ukuthi ubhede WABHEDISISA. 

Usede ethi enhliziyweni BAQINISILE abathi ngayesuswa uShaka phansi
komthunzi welanga. 

Wathi uyaphinda UYAZIBHIDISA kwaba amabhekedwane. 

Uma ngabe ukhuluma indaba yokuthi uyashada nje uqonde ukuthi ushada
nalesiya salukazi engisaziyo, NGIYAXOLISA ndodana, a-ngi-zi. 

Lapho indaba ikhulunywa kuhlaluke ukuthi zombili lezi zintombi
zeNkosi ZIYELELESA. 

UMkabayi lona kwakuyinkosikazi EMANGALISAYO ngezindlela eziningi.

Kwaba uye osondeza amanzi okuyigeza, kwaba yilokhu imthuma ukuba
abheke ukuthi ukudla kwayo KULUNGISWE kahle na. 

`Sukuma, Nkosi yesizwe, wena OMISWE ngabangasekho ukuba ubuse
elikaSenzangakhona." esho eqondisa kuDingane.

BABHINJISWA ukwehlulwa ukukhamisa. 

Insizwa ingena khona izazi ukuthi ayibhedelwa, kodwa ITHOTSHISWE
ngabafana abancane, bayishaye badedelane ngayo ize ithambe potololo.


OSiphiwosakhe benoSibongiseni besazitika ngoju nezinja zisazitika
ngamakhafilithi amanye ayemfimfithwa aphinyiswe YIBO abanikazi bazo
izinja laba, ngaphumelela ukushutheka umgxala ungene ntshi phakathi
kwamatshe lawo. 

Lathi liqambe liba sokhakhayini, base bebuyile ukuyoyigcwalisa
ithange, benzela ukuthi umsebenzi wabo UNGAPHAZANYISWA yinto
ewubuphukuphuku njengokuphelelwa u-petrol bengakafiki lapho beya khona.


Futhi UNGENELISWA nayilokho, ubuye ugange, kusho enye kwenye. Zibe
sezidumelene, zishayane, ziklwebhane, zilumane kube nje. 

Izwe ladliwa kumaXhoza, KWAMISWA iziMantshi, ukuba zilibuse,
selahlukanisiwe.

Ukuze asondele eNkosini uShaka kwaya ngoba WADUNYISWA enye induna
yathi uyifundile imithi yasenyakatho, kunjalo nje usesindise abaningi
ngamakhambi. 

Bahlala-ke sebelungele ukuze KULUNGISWE ingcwaba layo. 


Anikwe amakhubalo aqinile abe yisibonda esiqinile seNkosi, kuzawulwe
ocabangweni lwakhe uJeqe, KUNGENISWE imbuzi emnyama ayibambe, athi nxa
eseyibambile ibhotshozwe malungana nenhliziyo kuthathwe igazi layo,
lithakwe namafutha engwe, nebhubesi, nenhlwathi, iNkosi incinde, uJeqe
akhothe udengezi. 

Intabazwe lena - =Harrismith= - yaqanjwa ngaye, KUHLONISHWA yena.

Uma-ke umuntu kuthiwa uyobingelela iMantshi kusuke kuqondwe ukuthi
uzovela nje phambi kweNkatholo, ibikelwe iMantshi ukuthi lo ngusibanibani
wakwabani, OWETHWESWE icala elithile, alenza ngosuku oluthile. 

Lowo mcabango WAVEZWA wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma sekuhlaziywa kahle,
kwabuye kwavunyelwanwa ngokuthi okungenani yena angahluthulela izicabha,
aqinisike ukuthi zihluthulekisisile phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi obucayi wokudidizelisa uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi bembamba ukuze angaloku eba yisiphazamiso. 

"NGANELISIWE mina, Ndaba, uma nezikaDingane zizosala, sihambe
nezakho sobabili."

Nokho wabuye wafekela lowo mqondo, wabona ukuthi kuyobe uyasehlisa
isithunzi sakhe, NOKUHLONISHWA kwakhe, nokwaziwa kwakhe njengomuntu
ongasohlangothini lomthetho.

Wayengawazi amandla kaNobuhle uMaqhuzu, ngaleso sizathu wamfundisa
amasu nezindlela ZOKUSETSHENZISWA kwesibhamu, enzela ukuthi uma
imqhamukela kabi eyabafo, akwazi ukwelekelela uNobuhle. 

Izwe ladliwa kumaXhoza, kwamiswa iziMantshi, ukuba zilibuse,
SELAHLUKANISIWE.

Ukukhalipha komqondo wakhe nxa kubuthene amadoda, kwakumeleka
ngesithunzi esimphumela waso kwabe KUWUKUHLONISHWA ngisho nayiyo inkosi
mbala. 

Sesehlukana uzwakalise isifiso sokuthi bekungaba yinto enhle uma
ETHUKUSWA uNobuhle ngoba ziyanda izinsongo zalaba bafana, zokuthi bafuna
ukuyibulala ingane yami. 

Wayedinwa agqunqe NASEBUSWENI uma ecabanga ukuthi phakathi kwabantu
abaziyo abafunda emaNyuvesi, kukhona abehluleka ngokungazenzisi
ukuhlonza ukuthi bayizifundiswa kangakanani. 

Wathi ukuba afike eNkosini, waba isithunywa senyanga yeNkosi
sokuya koxebula amagxolo ANGAMAKHUBALO nokuya kokukha amakhambi. 

Inyama yazo iyahlinzwa, IPHANYEKWE othangweni lwesibaya ingadliwa,
iyoze yelashwe iNkosi. 

"UNGETHUKI, Dingane," izwe lakhe uMkabayi lalipholile, lihlaba
emongweni.

Amabutho kaMhlangana agxume abheke phezulu KUTHI makazithathele
kwakaDingane.

Badla utshwala nenyama KWATHULA kwathi du. 

Kwakungesizo izimotshwana nje, kwakuyizinqola impela ezikhombisa
ukuthi nangamhla zithengwa kwacashunwa insavunsavu yamarandi, kwaphinda
KWASALA enye insavunsavu. 

"KULUNGILE, ngomuso kusasa nizoqonda emfuleni, njengemihla yonke,
nithi nibuya lapho bese niyovunula seniza ebandla, lapho kobe
sekubuthene abantu abazobikelwa ngenkatha.

Njengoba wayesehambe bonke ubusuku, kwenye indawo ehamba
ngokugijima, wazumeka waze wavuka emini enkulu, kwabe nokulamba
SEKUTHE ngilapha. 

"Wena uqonde uDingane kuphela kukho konke OKUKHULUMAYO," kusho
uDingane kuMhlangana.

Bafake amashoba abo ezingalweni nasezithweni, kube kuhle KUDELE.

Suka uhambe khona manje ungalindi noma kuze KUSE. 

`Singamlekelela nathi basizikazi abanye uma esebambeke kanjalo
okhuleni ukunokuba aze ayeke umsebenzi weNkosi ongaka',KUNCENGA
uMaNzuza'. 

Kusadingeka niphekwe impela nivuthwe tobo namuhla, KUSHO yena
uMphathi-sikole. 

Futhi ungeneliswa nayilokho, ubuye ugange, KUSHO enye kwenye. Zibe
sezidumelene, zishayane, ziklwebhane, zilumane kube nje. 

NoMfundisi ubesakuncoma kakhulu kabi ukukhuthala komkakho, KUQHUBA
uMaNzuza. 

"Ukuba bewuyimi ubuzokwenzenjani wena:" KUBUZA uMaqhuzu. 

Wona amehlo ayeselokoza umlilo, sifuba lesi sakhe sehla senyuka,
kubonakala ukuthi uZibambile SEKUTHI makaqhume.

Lapho uDingane SEKUTHI makaquleke uvalo, nolaka, kanye nokuzisola.

Weqela ngaphesheya wasiphula ISIQUNGA, wahlafuna impande yaso
wakhwifa, esusa wona umnyama wesidumbu. 

Waqhamuka ehamba nezinduna zakhe ZIHLOMILE zonke.

"SIFILE Ndaba. OweNkosi kasekho - uye koyisemkhulu-" ufile.

"NGIZWILE, Zulu. Mana njalo wena kaNdaba." kubonga uDingane.

UJeqe laphaya enhla nesibaya USEVUNULE naye, usebase umlilo wabeka
imbiza lapho iNkosi izopheka khona uselwa. 

NGITHE onqobile ohluliwe kosweleka azi kahle ukuthi wahluliwe,
angaphindi asuse uchuku ezweni.

Umfo wasebuThonga ukhuluma nje uJeqe ulapha eduze neNkosi
ULALELE. 

Inkantolo IGCWELE iyaphuphuma njengayizolo. 

Amabutho nhlangothi zombili AGXUME kube sengathi azodumelana.

Ndabezitha, UTHE okaNdaba angikubikele ukuthi ungesabi.

Bageze khona lapho kwesikabhadakazi wonke umuntu ULELE. 

SIFILE, Sivelelwe yingozi embi.

Uma ngabe UGUGILE, ugugele mina. 

Ngiyabona. Athule isikhashana uMaqhuzu, uthule nje uyazinxaphela
ngengaphakathi, uzwa kahle ukuthi UBHEDE wabhedisisa. 

Wayenesiphiwo sokuwathaka ezwakale amagama nxa ekhuluma, umlalele
noma UNGAQONDILE. 

Nabafana bami base bembe baze bakhathala bengafinyeleli eqeni
ELIGANGILEYO lendlovukazi yezinyosi. 

Kuthe lapho besikhipha isidumbu sakhe emanzini, kwahlaluka ukuthi
okaSenzangakhona wabefinyele umsipha, wambamba ngamandla esemanzini
AJULILE, kazathola nathuba lokuphefumula.

Ngithe ONQOBILE ohluliwe kosweleka azi kahle ukuthi wahluliwe,
angaphindi asuse uchuku ezweni.

Kwathathwa izinyathelo zokuphepha EZIQINILE, ukuze kugwemeke ingozi
yokufela ekhaya. 

Sekukhona izinkunzi ezimbili ezimnyama EZICIJILEYO, ezihlabayo,
ezingazange ziyizeke insikazi, ezanela ukwephusa zakhethwa eziyobanjwa
amabutho ngezandla bazidonye ngesibhakele zize zife. 

Wedlula kwabamaphephandaba, wabanika yonke imininingwane ngoyise,
enzela ukuba izihlobo ezikude nabangane bezwe ngesifo ESIVELE,
wayesedlulela ekhaya. 

Abantu ABEHLUKENE babembona, kube yilowo nalowo, ngendlela yakhe.


Ngabe uyambona ukuba USEBUYILE Ma. 

Ayi-ke wahlala nezwe LITHULILE bedla utshwala naye. 

Nxa SEBEGEZILE babuyele ekhaya, kufafazwe enye intelezi emnyango
welawu leNkosi, ingene khona, alandele uJeqe, afike endlale, ilale
elawini ngalobo busuku emva kokuba ikade ilala endlini yamakhosi
namadlozi. 

Ngaso leso sikhathi amabutho amasha ayengekho eye kohlasela le
kwaSoshangane, abanye SEBEFIKE bazikhonzela kwezinye izizwe bathi:
Sikhathele uShaka esibulalisa ngezinye izizwe! 

Ngingena njena SASESIDAMBILE isiwombe sazo sokuhlasela kithina
bahlaseli bazo. 

Asukume umshushisi athi: `Nkosi yeNkantolo! Ummangalelwa kula macala
awuchungechunge, uSimon Mpungose USESHONILE.' 

Yabe inenhliziyo elukhuni njengetshe; ingesabi lutho'umzimba wayo
umuhle ubunjwe kahle kakhulu, uthandeka; amehlo ayo lawa ekhanya
inhlansi, elokoza umlilo - lapho ESETHUKUTHELE ayeba bomvu sengathi
agcwele igazi.

Nabafana bami base BEMBE baze bakhathala bengafinyeleli eqeni
eligangileyo lendlovukazi yezinyosi. 

Sekuphume ILANGA kwaphuthunywa kwayoshwaywa izincingo kwabizwa
izingane zakhe. Ucingo lwesifo aluphendulwa-ke. 

SEKUPHUME ilanga kwaphuthunywa kwayoshwaywa izincingo kwabizwa
izingane zakhe. Ucingo lwesifo aluphendulwa-ke. 

Besesukuma uMkabayi ephonsa elakhe kusenjalo abantu BESADABUKILE,
enzela ukuze bayaqala bayacabanga useliphonsile.

Kufika nezithunywa zamakhosi ACEBILEYO zizoyeshela, kepha idimde
ihleke usulu nje. 

Anikwe amakhubalo AQINILE abe yisibonda esiqinile seNkosi, kuzawulwe
ocabangweni lwakhe uJeqe, kungeniswe imbuzi emnyama ayibambe, athi nxa
eseyibambile ibhotshozwe malungana nenhliziyo kuthathwe igazi layo,
lithakwe namafutha engwe, nebhubesi, nenhlwathi, iNkosi incinde, uJeqe
akhothe udengezi. 

Umfula wawungamanyathelo ATHI akabe ngama-30 kusuka esidlekeni
sezinyosi. 

Noma kanjani wawuqomile USAKHULA. 

Kuthe lapho esehlangana khona lapho, sekuzosuka impi enkulu
eyesabekayo, kwaqhamuka uDingane EHLOBE evathe ephelele.

Wathulisa wabuka, wambona EMI ethe ne ngomhlane othangweni. 

Wabataxa, wabataxa ETHI bayabhimba. 

Phela uma ikhona, BABETHI omakade ebona babasingi, uzibona
ngokubungela kwazo othini; zingqengqe ngalo uma ulushutheka esidlekeni
sazo njengomkhuba ezisuke ziwejwayele. 

Noma kanjani WAWUQOMILE usakhula. 

Babodwa ababethi uyogwetshwa isigwebo sokudilikelwa yijele kanti
iningi LALITHI wayezogwetshwa intambo. 

WAYEBUZA nje wayedidekile oKaMemela ukuthi umuntu oye koshaya
ucingo, khona lapha esitolo kwaMlamula, usengaze alibale kangaka. 

Wayebuza nje WAYEDIDEKILE oKaMemela ukuthi umuntu oye koshaya
ucingo, khona lapha esitolo kwaMlamula, usengaze alibale kangaka. 

Uma WAYESHILO kwakobulawa yena uJeqe kuthiwe umyekeleni. 

Ngenxa yokwazi ukuthi kuhlwa ngomnyama njengoba inyanga YAYIFILE,
ngangena mina emgodini owawusumbiwe abafana bami bewuqalelwe amachalaha
ami. 

Abanye BABETHI iyoba ngamashumi amathathu. 

Abanye BABETHI uzogwetshwa iminyaka engamashumi amabili.

ZAZINGASHWABENE izingubo wawungafunga ukuthi bezihlafunwe yinkomo
qede yaziphimisa. 

Ngalesi sikhathi iqembu elikhulu lamaBhunu, ELALILANDELA, lafika nalo
lamisa otende bezindlu eduze nomfula uThukela, abanye njalo benyukela enhla
bayokwakha enhla noMnambithi.

Babodwa ABEBETHI uyogwetshwa isigwebo sokudilikelwa yijele kanti
iningi lalithi wayezogwetshwa intambo. 

Uma kuvuma WAYEZOZABALAZA aqhubeke njalo aye ayogasela izifundo
zaseNyuvesi. 

"BENGINGATHI wathatha nomuthi esokeni lakho ukuba ubulale iNkosi."


Kwake kwakhulunywa eside isikhathi lesi ngoNsimbi, kukhona umbono
wokuthi noma UBENGASALA yena ngeke konakala lutho. 

Wayeloku ebabaze nje ukuba mnandi kokuhambisana negugu lakhe, aze
alikhiphe ngisho ukulikhipha elokuthi ubengakaqonywa sonke lesi sikhathi,
UBESADLALA nje. 

Zithukane kube nje abanye BALALELE. 

Futhi ungeneliswa nayilokho, ubuye UGANGE, kusho enye kwenye. Zibe
sezidumelene, zishayane, ziklwebhane, zilumane kube nje. 

Liphinde LIMEMEZE iphoyisa eliphethe imfuma yamafayela amacala
osuku. 

ASUKUME kudume inkundla yonke.

Amabutho kaMhlangana AGXUME abheke phezulu kuthi makazithathele
kwakaDingane.

ATHULE nje uMkabayi; kukhulume amehlo akhe kuphela.

ASUKUME umshushisi athi: `Nkosi yeNkantolo! Ummangalelwa kula macala
awuchungechunge, uSimon Mpungose useshonile.' 

Nxa sebegezile babuyele ekhaya, kufafazwe enye intelezi emnyango
welawu leNkosi, ingene khona, alandele uJeqe, afike ENDLALE, ilale
elawini ngalobo busuku emva kokuba ikade ilala endlini yamakhosi
namadlozi. 

Bonke bathi akubekhona okwenziwayo ukuze ingane IPHEPHE. 

Inceku enkulu ibasa umlilo omkhulu, ibekwe elangabini ISHE ize
iphele eduze nomnyango waleyondlu lapho laba abathathu bebona khona.


Bala kwathi phakathi kwamabili langa limbe, wacela ukhehla uKhumalo
ukuba isalukazi sakhe uMaMzobe, ATHANDAZE. 

Kwathi ukuba SISUKE isidumo leso uMfundisi =Owen= wabopha
okungokwakhe wabamba indlela eqonde eThekwini, lapho wafika khona
wadlulela phesheya eNgilande.

Nxa sebegezile babuyele ekhaya, kufafazwe enye intelezi emnyango
welawu leNkosi, ingene khona, ALANDELE uJeqe, afike endlale, ilale
elawini ngalobo busuku emva kokuba ikade ilala endlini yamakhosi
namadlozi. 

APHENDULE uNdongeni, umfo omude olaphaya wakwaZondi, athi "Mana
njalo Ndlovukazi yesizwe.

Kumnandi abantu behlezi emakhaya izwi LITHULE. 

Zisuke zizilungiselela isiqubu sokukhuza ibuya lapho zisuke zizothi
zingalwa uma zinqotshwa ZEMUKE. 

Sekukhona izinkunzi ezimbili ezimnyama ezicijileyo, ezihlabayo,
ezingazange ziyizeke insikazi, ezanela ukwephusa zakhethwa eziyobanjwa
amabutho ngezandla bazidonye ngesibhakele zize ZIFE. 

Nawe uma umlalela uyokusiza ukuba UPHENDUKE ukhethe iNkosi. 

Qha, ake UHLALE. 

Nxa sebegezile babuyele ekhaya, kufafazwe enye intelezi emnyango
welawu leNkosi, ingene khona, alandele uJeqe, AFIKE endlale, ilale
elawini ngalobo busuku emva kokuba ikade ilala endlini yamakhosi
namadlozi. 

Anikwe amakhubalo aqinile abe yisibonda esiqinile seNkosi, kuzawulwe
ocabangweni lwakhe uJeqe, kungeniswe imbuzi emnyama ayibambe, athi nxa
eseyibambile ibhotshozwe malungana nenhliziyo kuthathwe igazi layo,
lithakwe namafutha engwe, nebhubesi, nenhlwathi, iNkosi INCINDE, uJeqe
akhothe udengezi. 

Ndabezitha, uthe okaNdaba angikubikele ukuthi UNGESABI.

Ukuphuthuma lokhu kwenziwa ukuba babegcina ukuthi yinhloli,
uthunywe kwaZulu ukuba AZOHLOLA  kulandele impi ngoba ukulanda kwakhe
kokufika kwakhe ezweni labo akubahlabanga umxhwele. 

Kufika nezithunywa zamakhosi acebileyo ZIZOYESHELA, kepha idimde
ihleke usulu nje. 

"Nganelisiwe mina, Ndaba, uma nezikaDingane ZIZOSALA, sihambe
nezakho sobabili."

Uselwa lwalukhethelwa abalo njalo okuye kuthi nxa iNkosi
ISIZOKWESHWAMA baye kolukha eduze nolwandle. 

Mhla KUZOKUSA kube umkhosi iNkosi iyophuma lapho endlini kuvalwe,
iholwe inyanga iphethe ukhamba lwentelezi, iyifafaze intelezi baye
bafike emfuleni, uJeqe elandela iNkosi ephethe eminye imithi okuzofikwa
emfuleni phakathi kobusuku yelapha. 


Bahlala endlini, noma BEYOGEZA bayabuya bangene endlini. 

NGISHO naphakathi nesonto uMaZwane wehla enyuka nemisebenzi yeSonto
nje kuphela. 

LIYAPHUMA ilanga amabutho aseya emfuleni aseyogeza, sekugcwele
abafana namantombazana abalethele amabutho ukudla. 

Ngesikhashana esincane nje yilelo selimi kweyalo indawo, esehlome
esephelele, ASEYAHAYA. 

Loku kuhleka kwakhe kwamdida uMaqhuzu, akangaba nalwazi noma UHLEKA
nje umbona ubuphukuphuku yini noma kuyisima kanjani. 

BAYASHO-KE asebake balunguza khona ukuthi akusibhakela sidida
ompetha. 

Mina NGITHI uwe ongevela nesu ngoba usondele kakhulu kuye kunabo
bonke abantu. 

Bonke BATHI akubekhona okwenziwayo ukuze ingane iphephe. 

Lomfo ufika uyabika UTHI: "Ngimlinge ngamaqhinga amaningi uJeqe
ngithi asihlangane naye adlise uShaka." 

"USHO uMbopha kaSithayi?" kubuza uDingane, ethuka naye amehlo akhe
evutha umlilo.

Wathi ubafundisa ukukhamisa ngoba wayesethole kahle ukuthi
BAYABHIMBA. 

Ukuze angabonakali ukuthi UYEQA, waphuma entubeni engaphethe
zikhali, wahamba waye wafika emfuleni. 

UWELA nje usesifundeni sikaNdlebende iNkosi ephethe amaThonga
lapho. 

Nababusi bawo abakhulu ababebusa ngesikathi amaNgisi engakanqobi
izwe, babe nalowomqondo: umuntu omnyama yisichaka somhlophe, futhi BASHO
baqinise ukuthi noma umuntu umphethe kabi, noma umenzani, kakusono leso,
ngoba uyinto yomhlophe phela.

NGITHI wonke umuntu olapha ehholo akame ngezinyawo afake iminwe
emibili emlonyeni. 

NGIYABONA. Athule isikhashana uMaqhuzu, uthule nje uyazinxaphela
ngengaphakathi, uzwa kahle ukuthi ubhede wabhedisisa. 

"Dingane, ubizwe yimi, ngoba uMhlangana UTHI nawe kusweleke ube
khona lapha nxashana siqala lendaba yokuqeda lombango phakathi kwenu."

UTHI awube yintanga kaMa ongizalayo. 

ZIYAJABULA izinsizwa ezikhululekileyo eziya lapho zithanda khona.


Wabataxa, wabataxa ethi BAYABHIMBA. 

Phakathi kwalaba kwakukhona umfo wasebuThonga owayeseyisikhonzi
kuShaka ngoba waxoshwa kubo kuthiwa UYATHAKATHA. 

Wathi UYAPHINDA uyazibhidisa kwaba amabhekedwane. 

Lomfo UFIKA uyabika uthi: "Ngimlinge ngamaqhinga amaningi uJeqe
ngithi asihlangane naye adlise uShaka." 

Lapho sebebuyile ekugezeni BADLA, ngesikhathi zibuya inhlazane,
baqale manje ukuvunulela umkhosi. 

Besesukuma uMkabayi ephonsa elakhe kusenjalo abantu besadabukile,
enzela ukuze BAYAQALA bayacabanga useliphonsile.

Sesehlukana uzwakalise isifiso sokuthi bekungaba yinto enhle uma
ethukuswa uNobuhle ngoba ZIYANDA izinsongo zalaba bafana, zokuthi bafuna
ukuyibulala ingane yami. 

Lomfo ufika UYABIKA uthi: "Ngimlinge ngamaqhinga amaningi uJeqe
ngithi asihlangane naye adlise uShaka." 

Uma ngabe ukhuluma indaba yokuthi UYASHADA nje uqonde ukuthi ushada
nalesiya salukazi engisaziyo, ngiyaxolisa ndodana, a-ngi-zi. 

Kuthe ngakusasa esedlile esethi USEYAHAMBA, bathi.

UTHI bangaphezu kwesikhombisa abantu abahlukene ebezwa beyikhuluma
le ndaba. 

Bahlala endlini, noma beyogeza BAYABUYA bangene endlini. 

AYISEBENZI indaba yokuthi ukuba benginguwe. 

Uma ngabe ukhuluma indaba yokuthi uyashada nje uqonde ukuthi ushada
nalesiya salukazi engisaziyo, ngiyaxolisa ndodana, A-NGI-ZI. 

Cha, MaNzuza kulesi sinqumo sami ANGIGUQUKI. 

Emuva kwesikhashana washaya insimbi umfo kaShabalala izingane zonke
EZICULAYO zabuthana ehholo zisaqhubeka nokumpongoloza zicula. 

OFIHLAYO wayengasho nje ukuthi ungqubuzeke odongeni, noma kambe
athi uvule isivalo budedengu saye samsakaza, kodwa kwakucace njengezinqe
zeselesele ukuthi yizisihle zesibhakela leziya. 

Wasondela emzini wabona ukuthi kuphekwe emnyango, waququbala
buqamamana nomuzi, baze bephula bangena endlini, wasondela, izinja
zamuzwa, zamkhonkotha wabuyela emuva, wafuna isu lokuyothatha
isikhuni ESIVUTHAYO lapho bekade bepheke khona. 

Sekukhona izinkunzi ezimbili ezimnyama ezicijileyo, EZIHLABAYO,
ezingazange ziyizeke insikazi, ezanela ukwephusa zakhethwa eziyobanjwa
amabutho ngezandla bazidonye ngesibhakele zize zife. 

Cishu sakhohlwa ukulanda ukuthi laphaya oPhongolo lapha uJeqe
wayegula khona, kukhona inja yakuwo lowo muzi eyamejwayela, kuthi
lapho lomfazi owayelethela uJeqe ukudla eya kuJeqe, ihambe naye,
adle nokuncane ayishiyele, yaze yamejwayela, kwathi mhla EHAMBAYO
yamlandela ngomkhondo yaze yamfica, yaba seyiba yinja yakhe njalo.


Kuthandazelwa ABAGULAYO. 

Ekuseni lapho ilanga LIPHUMA ilichinsa ngomhlanga, obhotshozelwe
imbobo ebheke empumalanga, lapho lishona ilichinse ngembobo ebheke
entshonalanga. 

Ekuseni lapho ilanga liphuma ilichinsa ngomhlanga, obhotshozelwe
imbobo ebheke empumalanga, lapho LISHONA ilichinse ngembobo ebheke
entshonalanga. 

Kwathi ngonyaka ka-1883 kwafika izwi livela phesheya ELITHI zonke
izigqila azikhululwe abaninizo ziyekwe zifane nabantu bonke.

"Ngoba nike naxoxa naye uButhelezi, kuhle uphindele umncenge uthi
uDingane uyokuhlanza bonke ubumnyama bensila kaShaka akwakhele umuzi
omkhulu emva kokuba usugezwe ngentelezi, futhi mhla EFAYO uShaka
uyokulondoloza ungambelwa naye." 

Sizoke siyizwe lento enkulu eyasusa uthuli olungako ezweni
lakwaZulu, yaphemba umlilo omkhulu ONGACIMIYO kuze kube namuhla usazinge
ulokoza.

Yonke indlela lena bahamba belwa izimpi EZINGAPHELIYO nezizwe zabantu
ezasakazeka nezwe lonke belwa nezilwanyazana zasendle, belwa nezifo nendlala.

Bahamba-ke abakwaNdlovu beya kubayeni kanye nenjana yakhe
ENGASALIYO. 

Namabutho ayesezikhalela ETHI: Size siqhakaze izimvu singaganiwe,
singabazi ubumnandi bokuhlala emakhaya, kube yilokhu sihamba
ezintabeni, silale endle, sifa yindlala! 

Asukume eme ngezinyawo lapho uDingane, esethukuthele esebila,
isifuba sakhe SESIGUBHAZELA nje.

Kuthe lapho esebusa umfo kaSenzangakhona uDingane emva kokubulala
kwabo uShaka, kwafika izwi kuye livela kuMkabayi, udadewabo
kaSenzangakhona, LITHI ufuna ukuba kebabonane bobabili.

"Ngakho-ke ngomuso kusasa," kuqhuba uMkabayi "nizothi lapho nibuya
kogeza emfuleni njengemihla yonke, bese ngimeme izwe ukuze ngimkhethe
ozolibusa, phambi kwalo, LIBONA lonke.

Asukume eme ngezinyawo lapho uDingane, esethukuthele ESEBILA,
isifuba sakhe sesigubhazela nje.

Intamo yinde, amehlo mahle, ithi nxa IBHEKA ivunywe amashiya ayo.

Kuthe kuntambama kwakufika izinsizwa eziyisihlanu ziphuma eNkosini
ITHI azilande uJeqe aye kuyo. 

Wabheda wabheda uMaMzobe, kuthe lapho ETHI =Amen= khona, lase lithule
okokugcina ikhehla lakhe. 

Zazikhamise kakhulu zakhipha izilimi ZIHEFUZELA. 

Emuva kwesikhashana washaya insimbi umfo kaShabalala izingane zonke
eziculayo zabuthana ehholo zisaqhubeka nokumpongoloza ZICULA. 

Amhlabe ngamehlo akhe amakhulu amabi uMkabayi, ABESETHI.

Sizoke siyizwe lento enkulu eyasusa uthuli olungako ezweni
lakwaZulu, yaphemba umlilo omkhulu ongacimiyo kuze kube namuhla usazinge
ULOKOZA.

"Ngakho-ke ngomuso kusasa," kuqhuba uMkabayi "nizothi lapho NIBUYA
kogeza emfuleni njengemihla yonke, bese ngimeme izwe ukuze ngimkhethe
ozolibusa, phambi kwalo, libona lonke.

Sekuzwakala nezigqi zokuphefumula kubantu: umoya lona ungasathi
nyaka, nezinyoni imbala ezabe ZIXOKOZELA, zathula, kwasengathi
zitsheliwe ukuthi nansi indaba embi.

Kubuza uMkabayi, ETHUKUTHELA evutha.

Nxa umuntu EBUKA ubona sekumnyama izinkalo abantu. 

Amadoda asondela kuye abuza ukuthi uphumaphi, wawatshela ukuthi
uphuma kwaZulu uze kulelizwe uzofuna imithi yokwelapha ngoba wezwa
idumela ngabasuka lapha BETHI miningi imithi. 

Izinduna lapho sezijuluke zimanzi ZISHAYA, ziqoqa, eputshuka
ngalapha nangalapha. 

Wayenesiphiwo sokuwathaka ezwakale amagama nxa EKHULUMA, umlalele
noma ungaqondile. 

Esewelele kwelama Thonga yahlonga imizi eduze nomfula, wahamba
waze wadundubala phezu kwesihlambo somfula kwaba yikhona ebona imizi,
ezwa izinkomo ZIKHONYA. 

Abese qhubeka masinyane ETHI.

Ukhula luzalela izinyoni emasimini ami NGIKHULUMA nje. 

Kwakuthi uma zivikisana nabazala bakhe ekhaya, kuzibonakalele nje
ukuthi yize abanye babo befunda emaNyuvesi, amanzi ayehlela ngakubo,
ivuthiwe insizwa kaMdletshe le EKHANDA. 

Uthe ENGENA nje uDingane kwaba sobala ukuthi kabafunani
nokubhekana noMhlangana.

Ush' ukuthi kufanele ngihambe ngivimbela izinsizwa phandle lapha
NGITHI ngicela zingeshele khona ngizoziqoma. 

Kuthe ngakusasa esedlile ESETHI useyahamba, bathi.

Wawungabuyi ULAMBATHA owakhe umkhondo. 

Umfo wasebuThonga UKHULUMA nje uJeqe ulapha eduze neNkosi
ulalele. 

Uthi uDingane efika esigodlweni sakhe, kwakufika inceku kaMkabayi,
uZungu, ETHI.

Mhla kuzokusa kube umkhosi iNkosi iyophuma lapho endlini kuvalwe,
iholwe inyanga iphethe ukhamba lwentelezi, iyifafaze intelezi baye
bafike emfuleni, uJeqe elandela iNkosi ephethe eminye imithi okuzofikwa
emfuleni phakathi kobusuku YELAPHA. 

Naso-ke isizathu sokuqala esabangela amaBhunu siwabone esephungwa
ngezithebe kwaZulu, ekhumbuza uDingane izinkonjane ezabikwa nguShaka
mhla EFAYO.

UKHULUMA nje lomfo uShaka uyamphikisa uthi: "Awukalihambi leli
lakithi ubone izintombi ezinhle. 

Kuthe lapha kuthi hwaqa, wabanga emasimini, lokhu uwafica
EKHIHLIZA, nemfe isiyikhiphile iminyani, lokhu ingakavuthwa kahle. 

Kubuza uMkabayi, ethukuthela EVUTHA.

Izinduna lapho sezijuluke zimanzi zishaya, ZIQOQA, eputshuka
ngalapha nangalapha. 

Umfundisi ESIZWA kuthiwa uDingane wamvumela ukuba ahlale eduze
naye afundise abantu bakhe, kuthiwa nguMfundisi =Owen= Lowo.

Waphaphama uJeqe, uthe EPHAPHAMA enye yezinceku yayikhwezela
isihlonti soqunga, wacikica amehlo, wacabanga. 

Kuqhamuke iphoyisa ebelimlandile, ngejubane, SELIHEFUZELA. 

UNdlovu lo naye akuyena umuntu wokudabuka ebuThonga, wafika
ehamba ngokufuna imithi, ephuma emaHlutshini, wafika LINGAFI nkonyane,
wejwayela wayesehlala khona esenomuzi. 

Ekuseni ilanga LINGAKAPHUMI, umuntu usezwa umsindo ezigabeni,
behaya amagama bebhema insangu, bebonga amakhosi. 

Izinkomo sithi sibuya nazo zimboze izintaba nezinkalo, igazi
labaningi bakithi lichithekele ezizweni, SINGAKAPHUMULI useyasibiza
ukuba siyekohlasela kwezinye izindawo." 

Uma KUVUMA wayezozabalaza aqhubeke njalo aye ayogasela izifundo
zaseNyuvesi. 

Uthe ebuyela ezigabeni wafika lesi sithunywa sikaDingane sesihambile,
ETHI uzosixoxela lendaba embi nebuhlungu yokuhlinza umuntu wesifazane
ekhulelwe. 

LUYAVUTHWA laphaya uselwa, iNkosi iqale yaluhlabela ngoba nxa
lungaphathwanga yiyo abakwaZulu bathi aluvuthwa. 

"Ududwa ngoba unomuthi wentando, UBIZWA njalo yiNkosi. 

Kusadingeka niphekwe impela NIVUTHWE tobo namuhla, kusho yena
uMphathi-sikole. 

Sonke isikhathi IVULWA kuphela nxa kuzongena iNkosi noma unina
weNkosi, nabo bangene kukhona inyanga enkulu yeNkosi. 

Nempela LAQALWA-ke futhi iculo liqalwa nguye umfo kaMshengu
ngesihosho sakhe sezwi. 

Wafula ummbila wawetshatha, WAKHOHLWA manje ukuthi uzowosa
ngani. 

Isivakashi SASIYOKWAMUKELWA kuphela uma sihamba nomuntu ophethe
uqwenjana lolo, aphinde futhi anikeze isiqiniseko sokuthi singumuntu onjani.


Nempela KWENZIWA kanjalo. 

Kuthe lapha kuthi hwaqa, wabanga emasimini, lokhu uwafica
ekhihliza, nemfe isiyikhiphile iminyani, lokhu INGAKAVUTHWA kahle. 

Lowo mcabango wavezwa wukuthi, ngenxa yalobu khulu bakhe, awukho
umsebenzi owawungamlungela, kodwa-ke kuthe uma SEKUHLAZIYWA kahle,
kwabuye kwavunyelwanwa ngokuthi okungenani yena angahluthulela izicabha,
aqinisike ukuthi zihluthulekisisile phambi kokuba isuke imoto ngoba
oSteve noMaqhuzu kwakusobala ukuthi babezobhekana nomsebenzi omkhulu
kakhulu, futhi obucayi wokudidizelisa uPamella bazomfaka emotweni, bese
futhi bembamba ukuze angaloku eba yisiphazamiso. 

Yabe inenhliziyo elukhuni njengetshe; ingesabi lutho' umzimba wayo
umuhle UBUNJWE kahle kakhulu, uthandeka; amehlo ayo lawa ekhanya
inhlansi, elokoza umlilo - lapho esethukuthele ayeba bomvu sengathi
agcwele igazi.

Kusadingeka NIPHEKWE impela nivuthwe tobo namuhla, kusho yena
uMphathi-sikole. 

Ongaliphethe lolo qwenjana wayeyogcina esangweni, akukhathalekile
ukuthi WAZIWA kangakanani nokuthi wejwayele kangakanani ukuzophuza
kwaMaqhuzu. 

Umbiko lowo waye WATHOLWA nangabangane bakhe imbala, bathi yize
noma babexakeke kangakaya ezindaweni ezahlukene lapho babesebenza
khona, babengeke behluleka ukuza esifweni sikayise womngane wabo. 

Ekuseni ilanga lingakaphumi, umuntu USEZWA umsindo ezigabeni,
behaya amagama bebhema insangu, bebonga amakhosi. 

Kuya ngoba uhlala lapha koMkhulu, awuzizwa izindaba EZIKHULUNYWA
ngabantu ezifundeni lapha. 

Eseziphendulela EBUZWA nguMshushisi phambi kwezihlwele umfo
kaMpungose wathi abelungu ubabulala ngoba uyabazonda.
