Kwathi ngonyaka ka-1883 kwafika izwi livela phesheya elithi zonke
izigqila azikhululwe abaninizo ZIYEKWE zifane nabantu bonke.

Ngesizathu sokuthi wayebahlonipha abathengi bakhe uMaqhuzu, wabona
kunesidingo sokubachazela ukuthi sivezwe yini isidingo sokuba bashiye
okusazikhali abakuphethe endlini ethize eduze kwesango, nokuthi kufanele
ngani KUSUNGULWE ikilabhu yabaphuzi, okuyothi labo abafisa ukuba
ngamalunga ayo baphathe izingqwenjana ezifakazela ukuthi bangobani,
ezinezithombe zabo, ukuze bemukeleke. 

Inyama yazo iyahlinzwa, iphanyekwe othangweni lwesibaya INGADLIWA,
iyoze yelashwe iNkosi. 

Kwakungesizo izimotshwana nje, kwakuyizinqola impela ezikhombisa
ukuthi nangamhla ZITHENGWA kwacashunwa insavunsavu yamarandi, kwaphinda
kwasala enye insavunsavu. 

Isimnyama manje iNkosi IHLIKIHLWA, inindwa ngemithi, ayisabonakali
isimo sayo. 

Inyama yazo IYAHLINZWA, iphanyekwe othangweni lwesibaya ingadliwa,
iyoze yelashwe iNkosi. 

Luyavuthwa laphaya uselwa, iNkosi iqale yaluhlabela ngoba nxa
lungaphathwanga yiyo abakwaZulu bathi ALUVUTHWA. 

Sekuphume ilanga kwaphuthunywa kwayoshwaywa izincingo kwabizwa
izingane zakhe. Ucingo lwesifo ALUPHENDULWA-KE. 

Lembuzi AYIDLIWA okukhishwe kuyo igazi. 

"Jeqe, thatha lomfazi ubheke umkhonto omfishanyana, umqaqe isisu
kesibone ukuthi ingane ihlala kanjani esiswini INGAKAZALWA." 

Uma-ke umuntu KUTHIWA uyobingelela iMantshi kusuke kuqondwe ukuthi
uzovela nje phambi kweNkantolo, ibikelwe iMantshi ukuthi lo ngusibanibani
wakwabani, owethweswe icala elithile, alenza ngosuku oluthile. 

Phela ngalesisikathi base bebaningana aBelungu kwaZulu, ngoba
ngonyaka ka-1835 kwafika ABAFUNDISI abaziwayo kwaZulu, bezoshumayela
iVangeli.

UMfundisi =Adams= kwaqanjwa ngaye umuzi OWAZIWAYO waseAdams,
oseManzimtoti, base benza-ke belinga ukuthambisa izinhliziyo
zabakwaZulu.

Lapho indaba IKHULUNYWA kuhlaluke ukuthi zombili lezi zintombi
zeNkosi ziyelelesa. 

Umfundisi =Grout= lona nguye okwaqanjwa ngaye umuzi waseMvoti OTHIWA
kuseGroutville.

Sekukhona izinkunzi ezimbili ezimnyama ezicijileyo, ezihlabayo,
ezingazange ziyizeke insikazi, ezanela ukwephusa zakhethwa EZIYOBANJWA
amabutho ngezandla bazidonye ngesibhakele zize zife. 

Phinde zithambe, izinhliziyo ngoba uDingane uqobo lwakhe
wayengafuni ukuzwa lutho nje ngeVangeli leNkosi ENGABONWAYO.

Zisuke zizilungiselela isiqubu sokukhuza ibuya lapho zisuke zizothi
zingalwa uma ZINQOTSHWA zemuke. 

Kanti IXOXWA nje lendaba uJeqe usengenwe yisifiso esikhulu
sengathi angake ayibone lentombi eseyehlule amadoda nenhle kangaka.


Kuzothi-ke lapho inyanga ithathe yonke lemibengo iyixube ndawonye
emqubeni, iyifafaze ngemithi ibe ISIYOSIWA. 

Wawungacabanga ukuthi banezinyanga BAVALELWA esitokisini ngendlela
abase bezace ngayo. 

Munye kuphela owasola sengathi kukhona okukhona phakathi kukaMkabayi
noDingane - uMhlangana: ngoba nalapho bekhuluma esigodlweni sikaMkabayi
uDingane kwaba sengathi ukwazi konke OKWASEKUQONDWE nguMkabayi - nokho
kaze azihlupha kakhulu ngalokho; naye wayengakulindele neze lokho
ababekuqondile.

`Singamlekelela nathi basizikazi abanye uma esebambeke kanjalo
okhuleni UKUNOKUBA aze ayeke umsebenzi weNkosi ongaka', kuncenga
uMaNzuza'. 

Nababengahlakaniphile NGAPHEZU kwakhe babenamathuba angcono kunaye
uma benazo izitifiketi ezikhomba ukuthi bafunda bagcina emabangeni
angaphezu kwalelo yena agcina kulo. 

Nababengahlakaniphile ngaphezu kwakhe babenamathuba angcono KUNAYE
uma benazo izitifiketi ezikhomba ukuthi bafunda bagcina emabangeni
angaphezu kwalelo yena agcina kulo. 

Wabheda wabheda uMaMzobe, kuthe lapho ethi =Amen= khona, lase lithule
OKOKUGCINA ikhehla lakhe. 

Wayezizwa kahle umfokaKhumalo ukuthi kuyoyonke le misebenzi
ababhekene nayo, nguyena owabe ezokwenza umsebenzi osemqoka KUNABO
bonke. 

Ngesizathu sokuthi wayebahlonipha abathengi bakhe uMaqhuzu, wabona
kunesidingo sokubachazela ukuthi sivezwe yini isidingo sokuba bashiye
OKUSAZIKHALI abakuphethe endlini ethize eduze kwesango, nokuthi kufanele
ngani kusungulwe ikilabhu yabaphuzi, okuyothi labo abafisa ukuba
ngamalunga ayo baphathe izingqwenjana ezifakazela ukuthi bangobani,
ezinezithombe zabo, ukuze bemukeleke. 

"Awu, WENA kaBaba," kububula uDingane, ezesula ngesandla ibunzi
lakhe elase lijulukile limanzi.

"Kangithule, ZULU," kububula uDingane.

Uma wayeshilo kwakobulawa yena uJeqe kuthiwe UMYEKELENI. 

Mayelana nokuthi ungena KANJANI ngaphakathi wathi ziningi
izindlela namasu okuvula izicabha namafasitela njengoba labo asuke
ezobabulala uqala ngokubashunqisela udosi lwempisi. 

Isivakashi sasiyokwamukelwa kuphela uma sihamba nomuntu ophethe
uqwenjana lolo, aphinde futhi anikeze isiqiniseko sokuthi singumuntu ONJANI.


Umuntu uya athi fuqaqa phansi noma yini abeyenza, akukhathalekile
ukuthi beyibaluleke KANGAKANANI, aphuthume lapho kuvele khona isidumo.

Ngesizathu sokuthi wayebahlonipha abathengi bakhe uMaqhuzu, wabona
kunesidingo sokubachazela ukuthi sivezwe yini isidingo sokuba bashiye
okusazikhali abakuphethe endlini ethize eduze kwesango, nokuthi kufanele
ngani kusungulwe ikilabhu yabaphuzi, okuyothi labo abafisa ukuba
ngamalunga ayo baphathe izingqwenjana ezifakazela ukuthi BANGOBANI,
ezinezithombe zabo, ukuze bemukeleke. 

Ngenxa kaShaka mina ngethembekile kuye ngesivumelwano engasenza naye
ukuba ngimufele noma KUNJANI. 

"Khuluma, Ndongeni, ungade ugwinya amathe sengathi kawazi ukuthi
UTHINI."

Kufanele akwazi loku, senzele ukuthi noma ngabe kwenzekani
kuNobuhle, noma ngabe kwenzekani lapha ekhaya, angasisoli ukuthi
sasingamtsheli NGANI. 

"Ukuba bewuyimi UBUZOKWENZENJANI wena:" Kubuza uMaqhuzu. 

Amadoda asondela kuye abuza ukuthi UPHUMAPHI, wawatshela ukuthi
uphuma kwaZulu uze kulelizwe uzofuna imithi yokwelapha ngoba wezwa
idumela ngabasuka lapha bethi miningi imithi. 

Kwathi ashone phansi uJeqe, pho, UZOTHINI sekukhulume izulu
eliphezulu. 

Kufanele akwazi loku, senzele ukuthi noma ngabe kwenzekani
kuNobuhle, noma ngabe KWENZEKANI lapha ekhaya, angasisoli ukuthi
sasingamtsheli ngani. 

"Jeqe, thatha lomfazi ubheke umkhonto omfishanyana, umqaqe isisu
kesibone ukuthi ingane ihlala KANJANI esiswini ingakazalwa." 

Wayedinwa agqunqe nasebusweni uma ecabanga ukuthi phakathi kwabantu
abaziyo abafunda emaNyuvesi, kukhona abehluleka ngokungazenzisi
ukuhlonza ukuthi bayizifundiswa KANGAKANANI. 

Zafika zakhuluma nabakhona uJeqe engazi ukuthi kukhulunywa
NGANI.

Uze akhulume kanjalo nje UZWENI. 

Kwaba uye osondeza amanzi okuyigeza, kwaba yilokhu imthuma ukuba
abheke ukuthi ukudla kwayo kulungiswe kahle NA. 

Yayingasali noma EYAPHI. 

Wafula ummbila wawetshatha, wakhohlwa manje ukuthi uzowosa
NGANI. 

Ongaliphethe lolo qwenjana wayeyogcina esangweni, akukhathalekile
ukuthi waziwa KANGAKANANI nokuthi wejwayele kangakanani ukuzophuza
kwaMaqhuzu. 

Wakhohlwa ukuba uzotshela BANI ukuthi ubone lomuntu nokuthi
umehlule ngamandla. 

Bobabili bamane bashaqeka nje ukuthi uThisha Omkhulu uqale NINI ukuba
ngumbhidi. 

Ngesizathu sokuthi wayebahlonipha abathengi bakhe uMaqhuzu, wabona
kunesidingo sokubachazela ukuthi sivezwe yini isidingo sokuba bashiye
okusazikhali abakuphethe endlini ethize eduze kwesango, nokuthi kufanele
NGANI kusungulwe ikilabhu yabaphuzi, okuyothi labo abafisa ukuba
ngamalunga ayo baphathe izingqwenjana ezifakazela ukuthi bangobani,
ezinezithombe zabo, ukuze bemukeleke. 

Kwakuyizinkumbi abantu baseMaBheleni, kuyilowo nalowo efuna
ukuzizwela ukuthi lizohamba KANJANI. 

Noma KANJANI wawuqomile usakhula. 

Wawungafunga ukuthi ubekhona kuntshontshwa izimbuzi zomnumzane
mumbe, ngoba kwakhuthi lapho amaphoyisa ecela ukuba awacebise ukuthi
ngase kube lowo monakalo wenziwe NGUBANI, amane ashaye emhloleni, bala
ngqi, abanjwe amasela. 

Wawungafunga ukuthi ubekhona kuntshontshwa izimbuzi zomnumzane
mumbe, ngoba kwakhuthi lapho amaphoyisa ecela ukuba awacebise ukuthi
ngase kube lowo monakalo wenziwe NGUBANI, amane ashaye emhloleni, bala
ngqi, abanjwe amasela. 

Kwakusilele kona nje ukuthi zazingekho izincwadi ezazimfakazela
ukuthi uhlakaniphe KANGAKANANI. 

WAYA wafika wakhuleka komunye umuzi, wahlala phansi komuthi. 

KUYA ngoba uhlala lapha koMkhulu, awuzizwa izindaba ezikhulunywa
ngabantu ezifundeni lapha. 

Umuntu UYA athi fuqaqa phansi noma yini abeyenza, akukhathalekile
ukuthi beyibaluleke kangakanani, aphuthume lapho kuvele khona isidumo.


Bamupha ukudla, wadla walala kanti USEYE wabikwa enduneni,yathuma izinsizwa 
ezimbili zayombika eNkosini le emzini wayo. 

Ukuze angabonakali ukuthi uyeqa, waphuma entubeni engaphethe
zikhali, wahamba WAYE wafika emfuleni. 

Namhla esewela uSuthu yahlamba eduze kwesikebhe YAYE yaphumela
ngaphesheya. 

Ofihlayo wayengasho nje ukuthi ungqubuzeke odongeni, noma kambe
athi uvule isivalo budedengu SAYE samsakaza, kodwa kwakucace njengezinqe
zeselesele ukuthi yizisihle zesibhakela leziya. 

Umbiko lowo WAYE watholwa nangabangane bakhe imbala, bathi yize
noma babexakeke kangakaya ezindaweni ezahlukene lapho babesebenza
khona, babengeke behluleka ukuza esifweni sikayise womngane wabo. 

Uma kuvuma wayezozabalaza aqhubeke njalo AYE ayogasela izifundo
zaseNyuvesi. 

Mhla kuzokusa kube umkhosi iNkosi iyophuma lapho endlini kuvalwe,
iholwe inyanga iphethe ukhamba lwentelezi, iyifafaze intelezi BAYE
bafike emfuleni, uJeqe elandela iNkosi ephethe eminye imithi okuzofikwa
emfuleni phakathi kobusuku yelapha. 

Kuthe la kumpondozankomo, ENGAZANGE ehlangana namuntu, wangena
esihlahleni wahlala. 

Wezwa esengenwa uthando lwayo ENGAZANGE eyibona. 

Uthi uselihambe kakhulu naleli lakwaZulu kodwa AKAZANGE ayibone
intombi enhle njengayo. 

Sekukhona izinkunzi ezimbili ezimnyama ezicijileyo, ezihlabayo,
EZINGAZANGE ziyizeke insikazi, ezanela ukwephusa zakhethwa eziyobanjwa
amabutho ngezandla bazidonye ngesibhakele zize zife. 

Athi angalithola ithuba aye exhibeni lalo, limzekele okuningi
ngalentombi, waze wacishe wayazi ENGEZANGE ayibone.

Kwakuthi uma zivikisana nabazala bakhe ekhaya, kuzibonakalele nje
ukuthi YIZE abanye babo befunda emaNyuvesi, amanzi ayehlela ngakubo,
ivuthiwe insizwa kaMdletshe le ekhanda. 

Naye kahlalanga sikathi eside kwaZulu, ngoba kwathi esahlezi
izinyanga ezine kuphela uDingane wasusa isidumo esikhulu kwaZulu, OKUZE
kube namuhla sisashaqisa izwe lonke.

Kuthe sebe kude-buduze nezwe laseNatali, sebevinjelwe uKhahlamba
kuphela, uMnumzane uPieter =Retief= nedlanzana labanye nezinqola zabo,
balandulela iqembu elikhulu, BAZE batheleka lapha eNatali ngonyaka
ka-1837.

Cishu sakhohlwa ukulanda ukuthi laphaya oPhongolo lapha uJeqe
wayegula khona, kukhona inja yakuwo lowo muzi eyamejwayela, kuthi
lapho lomfazi owayelethela uJeqe ukudla eya kuJeqe, ihambe naye,
adle nokuncane ayishiyele, YAZE yamejwayela, kwathi mhla ehambayo
yamlandela ngomkhondo yaze yamfica, yaba seyiba yinja yakhe njalo.


Lapho yasukuma YAZE yagquma into yakwabo, kwazise umkhaba
wawunyomfozeka uma isukuma bese incisheka umoya. 

Cishu sakhohlwa ukulanda ukuthi laphaya oPhongolo lapha uJeqe
wayegula khona, kukhona inja yakuwo lowo muzi eyamejwayela, kuthi
lapho lomfazi owayelethela uJeqe ukudla eya kuJeqe, ihambe naye,
adle nokuncane ayishiyele, yaze yamejwayela, kwathi mhla ehambayo
yamlandela ngomkhondo YAZE yamfica, yaba seyiba yinja yakhe njalo.


Nabafana bami base bembe BAZE bakhathala bengafinyeleli eqeni
eligangileyo lendlovukazi yezinyosi. 

Bahamba-ke bedabula lezonkalo nemimango, nezintaba ezesabekayo, BAZE
bafika lapha eNingizimu nezwe.

Athi angalithola ithuba aye exhibeni lalo, limzekele okuningi
ngalentombi, WAZE wacishe wayazi engezange ayibone. 

Wasondela emzini wabona ukuthi kuphekwe endlini, wasondela, izinja
zamuzwa, zamkhonkotha wabuyela emuva, wafuna isu lokuyothatha
isikhuni esivuthayo lapho bekade bepheke khona. 

Esewelele kwelama Thonga yahlonga imizi eduze nomfula, wahamba
WAZE wadundubala phezu kwesihlambo somfula kwaba yikhona ebona imizi,
ezwa izinkomo zikhonya. 

Njengoba wayesehambe bonke ubusuku, kwenye indawo ehamba
ngokugijima, wazumeka WAZE wavuka emini enkulu, kwabe nokulamba
sekuthe ngilapha. 

Wachiphichiphiza uMaMzobe KWAZE kwezwa omakhelwane, bala beza
bazomhlalisa. 

Lingena nje sebeke bahlangana abazali bezigebengu, bavumelana
ngokuthi KUNGEZE kwaba yinto enhle uma bethatha ummeli ngoba loko
kuyobonakala sengathi kuyindlela abavuna ngayo izingane zabo, nabazama
ngayo ukuba izingane zabo zingasitholi isijezo esifanele isenzo sazo.


Udumo lwayo nobuhle bayo SEKUZE kwafika kude. 

Naye WAYESEZE wejwayela ukubulala abantu ngoba noma into iyimbi
inxa umuntu eseyenzele futhi ayibe isabambi. 

Wayelivuma elokuthi bangcono kunaye ngoba banezitifiketi ezingcono
kunaloko ayebambelele kukona, kodwa-ke YIZE kunjalo, umuntu akahlali
ephethe isitifiketi ngesandla. 

Amadoda asondela kuye abuza ukuthi uphumaphi, wawatshela ukuthi
uphuma kwaZulu uze kulelizwe UZOFUNA imithi yokwelapha ngoba wezwa
idumela ngabasuka lapha bethi miningi imithi. 

Sizoke siyizwe lento enkulu eyasusa uthuli olungako ezweni
lakwaZulu, yaphemba umlilo omkhulu ongacimiyo KUZE kube namuhla usazinge
ulokoza.

Namabutho ayesezikhalela ethi: SIZE siqhakaze izimvu singaganiwe,
singabazi ubumnandi bokuhlala emakhaya, kube yilokhu sihamba
ezintabeni, silale endle, sifa yindlala! 

SIZOKE siyizwe lento enkulu eyasusa uthuli olungako ezweni
lakwaZulu, yaphemba umlilo omkhulu ongacimiyo kuze kube namuhla usazinge
ulokoza.

Izinhliziyo zabantu sezinamathele kuDingane ezethemba ukuthi izwe
UZO-ke aliphumuze empini. 

UZE akhulume kanjalo nje uzweni. 

Munye kuphela owasola sengathi kukhona okukhona phakathi kukaMkabayi
noDingane - uMhlangana: ngoba nalapho bekhuluma esigodlweni sikaMkabayi
uDingane kwaba sengathi ukwazi konke okwasekuqondwe nguMkabayi - nokho
KAZE azihlupha kakhulu ngalokho; naye wayengakulindele neze lokho
ababekuqondile.

Naye kuyamkhanyela ukuthi izwe uliphethe kabi, kodwa wethembekile
eNkosini yakhe AKANAKUZE ayilimaze. 

Wayebuza nje wayedidekile oKaMemela ukuthi umuntu oye koshaya
ucingo, khona lapha esitolo kwaMlamula, USENGAZE alibale kangaka. 

Yiwona ayesho njalo, iningi labanye abamhlophe lalingaboni lutho
olungako olwalukhalisa amaBhunu, OLUNGAZE luwalumise izinyawo ababange
ngokuhamba.

Ukuba akangifanele ngabe ANGIZANGE ngizihluphe nokuzihlupha
ngokumthatha. 

`Singamlekelela nathi basizikazi abanye uma esebambeke kanjalo
okhuleni ukunokuba AZE ayeke umsebenzi weNkosi ongaka', kuncenga
uMaNzuza'. 

Wayeloku ebabaze nje ukuba mnandi kokuhambisana negugu lakhe, aze
ALIKHIPHE ngisho ukulikhipha elokuthi ubengakaqonywa sonke lesi sikhathi,
ubesadlala nje. 

Sekukhona izinkunzi ezimbili ezimnyama ezicijileyo, ezihlabayo,
ezingazange ziyizeke insikazi, ezanela ukwephusa zakhethwa eziyobanjwa
amabutho ngezandla bazidonye ngesibhakele ZIZE zife. 

Insizwa ingena khona izazi ukuthi ayibhedelwa, kodwa ithotshiswe
ngabafana abancane, bayishaye badedelane ngayo IZE ithambe potololo.


Ngangingazi ukuthi ukuzinikela eNkosini yami kuyakungenza NGIZE
ngenze izinto ezinengeka kanje. 

Suka uhambe khona manje ungalindi noma KUZE kuse. 

Sizobuyela futhi ukuze siyizwe kahle lendaba, siyiqale ekuqaleni
SIZE sizofika lapho uDingane asusa khona isenzo esashaqisa izwe lonke.

Inceku enkulu ibasa umlilo omkhulu, ibekwe elangabini ishe IZE
iphele eduze nomnyango waleyondlu lapho laba abathathu bebona khona.


Inyama yazo iyahlinzwa, iphanyekwe othangweni lwesibaya ingadliwa,
IYOZE yelashwe iNkosi. 

Munye kuphela owasola sengathi kukhona okukhona phakathi kukaMkabayi
noDingane - uMhlangana: ngoba nalapho bekhuluma esigodlweni sikaMkabayi
uDingane kwaba sengathi ukwazi konke okwasekuqondwe nguMkabayi - nokho
kaze AZIHLUPHA kakhulu ngalokho; naye wayengakulindele neze lokho
ababekuqondile.

Lesi simo sabe sesimvula amehlo uMaqhuzu, WAZIBONA kahle ukuthi
ukuhlakanipha kwakhe kuphelela obala uma kungenasesekelo
esiyisitifiketi. 

WAYEZIZWA kahle umfokaKhumalo ukuthi kuyoyonke le misebenzi
ababhekene nayo, nguyena owabe ezokwenza umsebenzi osemqoka kunabo
bonke. 

Ebuzwa ukuthi UYAZISOLA yini ngalezi zenzo zakhe zokubulala laba
belungu abaningi kangaka wathi, cha. 

Bathe lapho BEZIPHONSA phakathi esizibeni oNdongeni noSiphepho
noZidumo bamfica esephangalele okaSenzangakhona.

Uhlalile impela ngoba usuke lapha seliya KOZILAHLA kunina. 

OSiphiwosakhe benoSibongiseni besazitika ngoju nezinja ZISAZITIKA
ngamakhafilithi amanye ayemfimfithwa aphinyiswe yibo abanikazi bazo
izinja laba, ngaphumelela ukushutheka umgxala ungene ntshi phakathi
kwamatshe lawo. 

"Awu, wena kaBaba," kububula uDingane, EZESULA ngesandla ibunzi
lakhe elase lijulukile limanzi.

OSiphiwosakhe benoSibongiseni BESAZITIKA ngoju nezinja zisazitika
ngamakhafilithi amanye ayemfimfithwa aphinyiswe yibo abanikazi bazo
izinja laba, ngaphumelela ukushutheka umgxala ungene ntshi phakathi
kwamatshe lawo. 

Ukuba akangifanele ngabe angizange NGIZIHLUPHE nokuzihlupha
ngokumthatha. 

Wezwa lawo magama uNgwane qede WAZIBAMBA ukhanda, wabheka phansi.


Wona amehlo ayeselokoza umlilo, isifuba lesi sakhe sehla senyuka,
kubonakala ukuthi UZIBAMBILE sekuthi makaqhume.

Insizwa ingena khona IZAZI ukuthi ayibhedelwa, kodwa ithotshiswe
ngabafana abancane, bayishaye badedelane ngayo ize ithambe potololo.


KWAKUZIBONAKALELA nje ukuthi lapho besuka khona indlala abayazi
bayizwa ngendaba. 

WAZELULA, waphuma esihlahleni, wahamba eqonda ezinkomeni
ayezibona, ziklabile, ziyibanga. 

Ngaso leso sikhathi amabutho amasha ayengekho eye kohlasela le
kwaSoshangane, abanye sebefike BAZIKHONZELA kwezinye izizwe bathi:
Sikhathele uShaka esibulalisa ngezinye izizwe! 

Amabutho kaMhlangana agxume abheke phezulu kuthi MAKAZITHATHELE
kwakaDingane.

Namatshe ayeqaqele eqeleni phakathi kwezinyosi nezingwenya
AYEZIHLALELE njena ngaphezulu. 

Wathi akube yilowo AZIYELE lapho ethanda khona. 

Ebuzwa ukuthi kukhona yini AZIKHALELA kukho wathi, cha.

Ngiyabona. Athule isikhashana uMaqhuzu, uthule nje UYAZINXAPHELA
ngengaphakathi, uzwa kahle ukuthi ubhede wabhedisisa. 

Kwase kuzobakhona nesiqiniseko sokuthi umuntu UZOZIPHUZELA
ngenkululeko, angathi ephethe ingilazi yotshwala ngapha, ebe ejeqeza,
elindele ukudonsa ivolovolo ngokuphazima kweso. 

Akekho ongathandi UKUZIZWELA isigwebo sendoda yesando. 

LeNkosikazi yasemaNgisini yayinenhliziyo emhlophe impela, ithanda
izinto ezilungileyo zodwa, ibusa ngesandla esilungileyo, esinozwela,
esikhuthazayo kuzo zonke izinhlangothi zezizwe ezingaphansi kwentende
yombuso wayo; kakhulu ezizweni ezimnyama, nezibuthakathaka, yayifike
igcizelele ekuthini bonke abaziphetheyo - isho oHulumeni phela
ababengaphansi koMbuso waseNgilandi - mabazikhuthaze ekuhlaleni kwazo,
BAZIVULELE izintuba zokuzakha, nazo zibengabantu abazihloniphayo
nabazethembayo, ingafuni nempela ukuba kube khona umahluko ekubusweni
kwabantu, kuthiwe laba banje ngakho kufanele baphathwe kanje.

Namabutho AYESEZIKHALELA ethi: Size siqhakaze izimvu singaganiwe,
singabazi ubumnandi bokuhlala emakhaya, kube yilokhu sihamba
ezintabeni, silale endle, sifa yindlala! 

ESEZIPHENDULELA ebuzwa nguMshushisi phambi kwezihlwele umfo
kaMpungose wathi abelungu ubabulala ngoba yabazonda. 

Kwaba yimithonselana nje engemingaki eyathi ukuhambahamba emgxaleni
wami, yabuye YAZIBUYELELA emuva yayosithela. 

Ngakho-ke akulungile ukuba ngiphume ebusizikazini, KUZIPHENDULELA
uMaZwane. 

Futhi basebezwile ngezinhloli zabo ukuthi kukhona izwe lena
eNingizimu eligobhoza ubisi liconsa uju lwezinyosi; kuthiwa LIZIHLALELE
nje, abantu abakhe kulo bayingcosana kakhulu, abamnyama, futhi kabakho
abamhlophe abaningi.

Akukho sizwe esingahlasela uZulu EZITHULELE. 

Wabe UYAZIKHALELA owesifazane; wamqaqa uJeqe. 

Asiboni nakuphenduka kwanhliziyo yakhe NOKUZIPHATHA kwakhe. 

Lapho uDingane sekuthi makaquleke uvalo, nolaka, kanye NOKUZISOLA.

Wayedinwa agqunqe nasebusweni uma ecabanga ukuthi phakathi kwabantu
abaziyo abafunda emaNyuvesi, kukhona abehluleka NGOKUNGAZENZISI
ukuhlonza ukuthi bayizifundiswa kangakanani. 

LeNkosikazi yasemaNgisini yayinenhliziyo emhlophe impela, ithanda
izinto ezilungileyo zodwa, ibusa ngesandla esilungileyo, esinozwela,
esikhuthazayo kuzo zonke izinhlangothi zezizwe ezingaphansi kwentende
yombuso wayo; kakhulu ezizweni ezimnyama, nezibuthakathaka, yayifike
igcizelele ekuthini bonke abaziphetheyo - isho oHulumeni phela
ababengaphansi koMbuso waseNgilandi - MABAZIKHUTHAZE ekuhlaleni kwazo,
bazivulele izintuba zokuzakha, nazo zibengabantu abazihloniphayo
nabazethembayo, ingafuni nempela ukuba kube khona umahluko ekubusweni
kwabantu, kuthiwe laba banje ngakho kufanele baphathwe kanje.

Naphezu lokhu kuhlola abafana bami babeqale ngakho ngangikuphindela
UKUZENELISA ukuthi kwakungekho halakasha yini lwenyoka ezazingenise
emgodini walo zihlala nalo izinyosi lezi. 

Bala washesha ukuwamukela loko abe ekufundiswa, into eyakhombisa
uMaqhuzu ukuthi wabe EZIMISELE kangakanani ukufa lapho efa khona.


WAYENGAZIMISELE uSteve ukuxabana noMama wakhe ngalelo langa kodwa
le mibuzo ayembelesele ngayo yayiholela engxabanweni. 

Zisuke ZIZILUNGISELELA isiqubu sokukhuza ibuya lapho zisuke zizothi
zingalwa uma zinqotshwa zemuke. 

Ukuba uMaqhuzu wayenazo ezinye izindlela ZOKUZIPHILISA, neziletha
imali gamawala njengomsebenzi wokudayisa utshwala, wayezothatha zona,
abuyeke utshwala ngoba babusondeza abantu abaningi eduze kwakhe, into
eyayingenza ukuthi nesitha esiqonde ukwenza umonakalo, singene kalula
ekhaya. 

Ithi nxa IZIQHAYISA `Mina ngothanda insizwa okuyothi noma impofu,
ingenankomo ibe ithandwa yimi ngenhliziyo yami nayo ingithanda. 

Kwasamina NGIYAZISEBENZA Ma. 

Uthe lapho eseseduze nezinkomo ilanga selibantubahle, wababona
abafana SEBEZIQOQA, nemizi eseyibona eduze namasimu wahlala phansi
waphumula. 

Ush' ukuthi kufanele ngihambe ngivimbela izinsizwa phandle lapha
ngithi ngicela zingeshele khona NGIZOZIQOMA. 

Sizoke siyizwe lento enkulu eyasusa uthuli olungako ezweni
lakwaZulu, yaphemba umlilo omkhulu ongacimiyo kuze kube namuhla USAZINGE
ulokoza.

Kwakuyizinkumbi abantu baseMaBheleni, kuyilowo nalowo efuna
UKUZIZWELA ukuthi lizohamba kanjani.
